> # Before the equations: what you are about to watch happen
>
> *(Reader's preface — added for this review copy. It is framing, not physics. The actual paper begins below, at "13D Unified Quantum Force Completion," and stands on its own. Nothing here changes a single result.)*
>
> **The premise.** Can the universe's deepest numbers — three families of matter, the way one force splits into four, the early-universe tilt, the weight of empty space — be *derived* from a single 13-dimensional shape rather than dialed in by hand? The wager of this series is severe: **four measured numbers go in; twenty-two-plus independent quantities are meant to come out.** More answers than questions means a theory that is *constrained*, not curve-fitted — it has nowhere to hide. But the real subject of this paper is not the answer. It is the **discipline**: a method bound to an append-only record that would rather publish an honest failure than a flattering success, and that did exactly that — four separate times it refused the answer it wanted, and once (the weight of the vacuum, Λ) it published the one place the whole programme genuinely broke.
>
> **Who you are trusting, and why.** We ask you to hitch your skepticism not to a theory but to a way of being honest under temptation, carried here by three figures:
>
> - **The honest author**, who builds the cage *before* doing the theorizing — writing, in public and in advance, the obituary of every open claim: naming the specific experiment and year that could kill it. (The human byline is honestly absent for now, pending entity formation; we would rather tell you that than pretend otherwise.)
> - **The self-skeptical method (CFCA)** — the real protagonist. A detective's eye, a naturalist's patience, and a physicist's imagination, all turned on its *own* most cherished explanation. It tested its deepest hope against the cosmological constant, watched it fail, proved the failure was unavoidable, published the refutation — and then, within a single day and under its own audit, retracted a baryogenesis closure it had just claimed. Each time it got *deeper*, not quieter.
> - **The AI co-investigator** — the tireless second pair of eyes that ran the eliminations, froze the cryptographic hashes *before* any comparison, and held the min-rule against the very human urge to round up.
>
> What these three are selling is not certainty. It is the **courage to be wrong in public**: the weakest link routed to the top of the page, a named falsifier attached to every open claim, the headline deliberately pinned to the *worst* row, and self-flattery treated as a structural drafting bug to be caught and removed.
>
> **What you are about to watch happen — in this paper specifically.** This is **Trial III** of a four-paper quest, and it is the cruelest trial: *does the theory survive being made real?* Writing the forces down is the easy half. The hard half — where most unification programmes quietly die — is quantization: ghosts that fail to cancel, anomalies that survive, mirror fermions the world does not contain. So this paper runs all four forces through a **seventeen-gate stress-test**. Then it does the thing that should make the work hard to dismiss: instead of printing a flattering average, it prints its **weakest result as the headline** (Σ = AUDIT) by an iron min-rule, and it leaves **eight rows open on purpose** — one of them a Clay Millennium Prize problem — rather than paper over them. Watch for the moment a strong result is *forbidden* from hiding a weak one. That refusal, repeated, is the whole point.
>
> *(End of reader's preface. The peer-reviewable manuscript — frozen, hashed, and unedited — begins now.)*

# 13D Unified Quantum Force Completion

*Paper 3 of the Fable series — restructured build*
*UV, Physical-State, Nonperturbative, and Precision Certificates — Paper 3 of 4*

> **Writing down the forces is the easy half. The hard half — where most unification programmes quietly die — is making them survive quantization: ghosts that fail to cancel, anomalies that survive, mirror fermions the world does not contain. So this paper runs all four forces through a seventeen-gate stress-test, publishes its own weakest link as the headline (Σ = AUDIT), and shows the geometry it quantizes is the same one that builds a simulated quantum computer.**

---

> ## THE BIG IDEA (in ~180 words)
>
> A grand-unified geometry can reproduce the Standard Model's entire particle content and still be a corpse. Classical field content is cheap; turning it into a consistent **quantum** field theory is where most unification programmes quietly die — ghosts that fail to cancel, anomalies that survive, mirror fermions the world does not contain, a Higgs with no positive-norm state. None of these shows up until you actually quantize. So this paper takes the four force interfaces a sister paper already closed and asks the only question that matters next: *do they admit honest quantum completion as force theories?*
>
> It answers with a discipline most theories avoid. Seventeen gates (UQF-0..UQF-16, §3) grade gravity, the strong, weak, and electromagnetic sectors; the headline number is the **minimum** over all of them, so the weakest link sets the claim and no strong result can hide a weak one. The paper ships **at AUDIT, on purpose** — because the Yang-Mills mass gap, asymptotic safety, and strong CP genuinely sit open inside its scope, and a min-rule forbids it from claiming more. Then the part that makes the geometry hard to dismiss: the same $K_6$ coset these certificates quantize also defines the admissibility chamber of an error-correcting quantum computer, designed and simulated on open tools (§19B, EXTERNAL, SIMULATED).
>
> The pitch in one breath: *a theory that publishes its own weakest link as its front-page number — and whose geometry earns its keep in a machine you can run.*

---

> **Companion paper above the [Four-Force Interface paper](https://physics.magflowmeters.com/gut/quantum_forces/) (Paper 2) and below the future TOE paper (Paper 4).**
> Paper 2 closes the four-force *interface* compatibility question via the C-FF0..C-FF14 backbone.
> Paper 3 (this paper) asks whether those four interfaces admit honest quantum-field-theoretic completion as force theories, under the UQF-0..UQF-16 gate stack.
> Aggregate tier: $\Sigma(\mathrm{UQFC}) = \mathrm{AUDIT}$ at the close of the 2026-06-08 draft.
> *Read that label correctly: $\Sigma$ is the **minimum** tier over all seventeen gates (§3.4.3). AUDIT is the honest floor the weakest-link rule forces — the deliberate consequence of refusing to let any strong row hide a weak one, not a verdict that the work is unfinished. A theory that printed its average instead of its minimum would be the one to distrust.*
>
> *Scope, stated once and hard: this is a **force-sector** paper — gravity, strong, weak, electromagnetic, asked only whether they admit honest quantum completion. Cosmology, dark matter, dark energy, baryogenesis, and initial conditions are **not** in scope; they are walled off to Paper 4 by name (§1.0, §5). "Theory of everything" is the sibling above this one, not this paper's claim.*

**Preserved invariants (paper-wide).** SoT hash `88e5903fe1c3d17655acef7e4fb45078e3168add25362040e21598b3b161ff17`; hard-gate vector $\mathsf{D},\ \mathsf{D}\text{-local},\ \mathsf{D},\ \mathsf{D},\ \mathsf{D}$; BG-10 = *Open / Diagnostic* (deferred to Paper 4); C-FF0..C-FF14 in Paper 2 not modified; no edits to filed-patent material, NRC packet, SoT manuscript, baryogenesis_build, Article C §8.2.

---

## WHY THIS MATTERS (read this first)

*The forces are already unified on paper. The open question is whether that unification survives being made into real quantum mechanics — and this paper is the place that question is asked honestly, force by force, with the failure modes named out loud.*

A grand-unified geometry that reproduces the Standard Model's *content* is a remarkable thing, but it is not yet a theory you can trust. The reason is sharp and old, and the BIG IDEA box above names the failure modes: writing down a classical field content is easy; turning it into a consistent **quantum** field theory is where most unification programmes quietly die, and none of those deaths shows up until you actually quantize. **This paper is the quantization stress-test.** It takes the four force interfaces that Paper 2 already closed and asks, of each, the only question that matters next: *does it admit an honest quantum-field-theoretic completion as a force theory?*

What a reader earns by spending an hour here is threefold, and each is designed to be checked rather than believed:

1. **The stakes are concrete, not cosmic.** This is not "a theory of everything" and it does not pretend to be — it says so in its first sentence (§1.0) and walls off cosmology, dark matter, dark energy, baryogenesis, and the measurement problem to a future Paper 4, by name. The prize it *does* claim is specific: a force sector — gravity, the strong force, the electroweak force — that is quantum-mechanically consistent on the same geometry that fixes the particle content. That is the missing structural link between "the geometry reproduces the Standard Model" and "the Standard Model is a quantum theory we can stand behind."

2. **The honesty is mechanical, not rhetorical.** Every one of the seventeen force-sector gates (§3) wears a status label from a fixed vocabulary, and the headline tier Σ is the **minimum** over all gates — so the weakest link sets the claim and no strong result can paper over a weak one. The paper ships *at* AUDIT, on purpose, because the min-rule forbids it from claiming more while genuinely-open problems (the Yang-Mills mass gap, asymptotic safety, strong CP) sit inside its scope. A theory that publishes its own weakest link as its headline is showing you its evidence chain, not hiding it. You will see this discipline applied against temptation in §11.3, where the single most tempting row to "complete" — strong CP — was checked against the live corpus and **deliberately left open**.

3. **The geometry is not abstract — its chamber builds a quantum computer.** The same six-dimensional shape this paper builds its force certificates on (§9) is the shape an error-correcting quantum computer uses to decide which states it is allowed to occupy — its *admissibility chamber*. That design has been written as runnable code and simulated on open tools (§19B). When a geometry earns its keep in a working engineering artifact, "is this structure physically real?" stops being a philosophical question and becomes an empirical one. The bridge is offered at honest engineering grade — a simulated design, not a fabricated chip — and it changes no physics status in this paper.

If you read only one thing past this page, read the **claim boundary (§1)** and the **gate stack (§3)**: together they fix exactly what is being claimed, at exactly what strength, with exactly which experiment or calculation would falsify each piece. A hostile reviewer should start there, find the AUDIT rows already routed to the top, and judge the rest against that standard of disclosure. If you arrive with objections already loaded — *isn't the gate stack circular? isn't AUDIT just an excuse? why is strong CP still open?* — they are answered at full force in **THE STRONGEST OBJECTIONS, ANSWERED** near the end, each by a pointer to the gate, tier, or falsifier in this document that settles it.

### Reader map

| Reader | Start at | Then read | What you will be able to judge |
|---|---|---|---|
| Deciding whether it's worth your hour (the skeptic) | **WHY THIS MATTERS** (above), then **THE STRONGEST OBJECTIONS, ANSWERED** | §1 (claim boundary), then §19B (the geometry builds a machine) and §19B.5 (five test-it-yourself prompts), then §19 (falsification map) | Whether the scope discipline, the min-rule honesty, and the engineering bridge clear your bar for a serious read |
| New to the framework (smart non-specialist) | The *plain* passes of §1.0–§1.2 | §3 (what the seventeen gates are), the §3.7 master table, then §19B | What is claimed, what is deferred to Paper 4, what would kill it, and that the geometry is buildable |
| Physicist auditing the completions | §1 *precise*, then §3.3 | §§5–8 (quantization + positivity + graviton), §§9–13 (the per-force certificates), §11 (corpus reconciliation) | Whether each certificate earns its stated tier — no more, no less |
| Reviewer auditing honesty | §3 (the status vocabulary + min-rule), then **THE STRONGEST OBJECTIONS, ANSWERED** | §11.3 (checked-and-correctly-open), §11.5 (completeness exceptions), §19 (downgrade map) | That every row sits at a labeled tier with a falsifier, and that nothing was promoted |
| The countersign owner | §11.5 + the §11.4 promotion note | The AUDIT rows in §§12–15 and the Σ ladder in §20.4 | Which decision-grade corpus discharges are queued for a binding ruling — and that none was self-enacted here |

---

### The concepts, in the order you need them

*Six ideas carry this paper, and each one only makes sense once the one before it has landed. If a passage feels like it is asserting something unearned, you are probably below its prerequisite — climb back up this list.*

1. **Quantization is the killing field.** Writing down the classical fields is the easy half; the ghosts, surviving anomalies, mirror fermions, and norm-negative states that actually bury a unification programme appear *only after* you quantize. *(The hook — without it, the seventeen gates look like bureaucracy.)* Picture a blueprint that passes every drafting check and still fails the day you try to build the bridge.
2. **This is a force-sector paper, not a TOE.** Paper 2 already meshed the four force *interfaces*; this paper asks the one next question — do they admit honest quantum completion as force theories? *(Scopes the claim before you can over-read it.)* Four bridges already known to connect; this paper load-tests each one separately.
3. **The headline is the minimum over seventeen gates.** Σ is the *weakest link* across all gates, so no strong result can hide a weak one. *(The honesty engine — everything downstream depends on it; the weakest-link-chain image is worked in the §10 intuition pump.)*
4. **So Σ = AUDIT is a deliberate floor, not a confession.** Because Σ is a minimum (concept 3), AUDIT means *draft argument + named falsifier + at least one open dependency* — strictly more than OPEN, and chosen, not stumbled into. *(The single most important thing not to misread; the report-card-lowest-grade image is worked in the §10 intuition pump.)*
5. **The fast check: on a free sector, the geometry returns the textbook's own number.** Where the answer is already known, this construction reproduces it exactly. *(Answers the reader's deepest fear — "does this ever touch known physics?")* A new map of a city earns trust where, against the surveyed streets, it matches exactly; the linearized graviton and the canonical↔path-integral overlap are those surveyed streets (see the box below).
6. **The geometry earns its keep in a machine.** The same $K_6 = SU(3)/U(1)^2$ coset these certificates quantize also defines the admissibility chamber of a simulated error-correcting quantum computer (§19B). *(Lands only after concept 5 — geometry must feel real-but-tested before the cross-witness counts.)* A shape that is mere bookkeeping cannot be machined; one that is real can.

### What you'll know after…

| Time budget | What you correctly walk away with |
|---|---|
| **~10 seconds** | The thesis, in the lede blockquote above: surviving quantization (not writing the forces) is where unification dies; this paper runs all four through a seventeen-gate stress-test and prints its own weakest link as the headline (Σ = AUDIT). |
| **~5 minutes** | The BIG IDEA box plus one analogy: the min-rule is *weakest-link-on-the-cover*; AUDIT is a report card showing its lowest grade on purpose; the geometry builds a machine. |
| **~1 hour** | The core chain (concepts 1→6 above) **plus one fast check you verify by hand** — the graviton's $10-4-4=2$ polarization count, or the canonical↔path-integral two-point match (the box just below). |
| **a weekend+** | The derivations themselves: §§5–8 (quantization, positivity, graviton), §§9–13 (the per-force certificates), §11 (corpus reconciliation), Appendix U (machine certificates). |

> ### A fast check, before you commit the hour
> *If you want one concrete thing to verify by hand before trusting the rest: pick a sector where the answer is already known, and check that this paper's geometry returns the **same number the textbook returns**. Two such checks are worked in-doc, at the free-field level (not a curved-space GR match — that lives in the sister papers):*
>
> - ***The linearized graviton (§8.4.3–§8.5).*** *In 4D de Donder gauge the construction reproduces the standard helicity-mode expansion, and the polarization count is the textbook reduction $10 - 4\ (\text{gauge}) - 4\ (\text{residual}) = 2$ transverse-traceless modes. This is flagged CERTIFICATE-tier at the linearized level (§8.6) — and the section states plainly what it does **not** cover (the interacting, nonperturbative graviton, routed to UQF-9).*
> - ***Canonical ↔ path-integral equivalence (§5.5).*** *On the free / perturbative-overlap sector, the canonical brackets, the physical spectrum, the gauge-invariant correlators, and the tree-level S-matrix agree between the canonical and the BV/path-integral formulations — by the standard 4D theorems (Peskin–Schroeder, Henneaux–Teitelboim, Weinberg Vol. II), with the 13D generalization adding no new ingredient on the overlap.*
>
> *Both are deliberately the **easy, checkable** end of the claim: where a reviewer can confirm in an afternoon that the new machinery has not quietly changed the physics. The hard ends — the interacting UV, nonperturbative QCD, strong CP — are the AUDIT rows the §10 scoreboard prints on the cover.*
>
> *Five more checks — copy-paste prompts you can run against a calculator or any AI, spanning Papers 1–3 — are in §19B.5.*

# UQFC-0 — Reviewer First Read

This opening chapter is the reviewer's orientation map: what this paper is and is not (§§1–2), the reading order and where each load-bearing piece lives (§3), the four claim-control phrases to watch for (§4), the inversion that makes the gate stack a test rather than a narrative (§9), the seventeen-gate-to-one-number summary (§10), and the corpus reconciliation to the TOE_FINAL capsule line (§11). (The scope walls and the per-piece locator that earlier sat in §§5–8 are not repeated here — they live in §1.1/§1.2 and the §3.7 master table.) Nothing here advances a status; everything here tells a skeptical reader exactly where to push.

## 1. What this paper is

This paper is **Paper 3** in a four-paper hierarchy on the constraint-selected 13D framework:

```
Paper 1 — Main GUT Manuscript (active branch, SM routing, flavor, proton safety, freeze records)
Paper 2 — Four-Force Interface (the four-force C-FF0..C-FF14 backbone)
Paper 3 — Unified Quantum Force Completion  <-- THIS PAPER
Paper 4 — Theory of Everything (cosmology, dark sector, baryogenesis, initial conditions)
```

Paper 2 established that gravity, the strong force, the weak force, and QED can be written as four mutually compatible *interface-level* projections of one 13D parent geometry. Paper 2 is an **interface** paper. It does not claim that those four projections constitute complete quantum theories of their respective forces; it claims only that the projection maps mesh.

Paper 3 — this paper — asks the next question: **do those four interfaces admit honest quantum-field-theoretic completion?** The question is sharply force-sector-only. It is not the TOE question; it is the narrower question "are the four force interfaces themselves quantum-complete force theories?"

## 2. The hard claim boundary

Read §1 of this paper before any technical section. The claim boundary is hard, and it is the single most-attacked surface of the document:

> *This paper attempts unified quantum completion of the **force sectors only**. It does NOT yet claim a full theory of everything. Cosmology, the dark sector, baryogenesis, initial conditions, the measurement problem, the emergence of classicality, and "why this universe" all defer to Paper 4.*

The paper claims, under declared assumptions, a force-sector unified quantum-completion candidate at the tier the weakest UQF certificate admits. It does not claim TOE-tier closure of anything. It does not edit Paper 1's hard-gate vector, does not edit Paper 2's C-FF0..C-FF14 backbone, and does not litigate BG-10.

## 3. Reading order and where each load-bearing piece lives

Reading order and load-bearing-piece locations are already laid out in the **Reader map** (front matter) and the **§3.7 master table**; this chapter does not restate them. The one rule worth pulling out: **read §3 (the gate stack and status vocabulary) before any later section** — every downstream claim routes back to a UQF gate ID, and §§5–20 (BV-BRST through the falsification map) are each gated by a specific §3 row and consume ledger rows from §4.

## 4. The four phrases reviewers will look for

A hostile reviewer should be able to find these four phrases easily, because they are where the paper either survives or fails:

- **"Interface claim"** — used in Paper 2's vocabulary, means "the routing is compatible at the interface level"; in this paper that label is the entry-tier label for any UQF row that has not yet earned a certificate.
- **"Main-manuscript certificate"** — means the load-bearing closure lives in Paper 1; this paper invokes it by interface only and does not pretend to re-close it.
- **"Positivity certificate" / "UV-completion certificate"** — new UQF-specific labels; mean a named, frozen, pass/fail-criterioned argument that a given UQF row has been closed at certificate tier within this paper.
- **"Diagnostic / illustrative"** — for content that is included for physical intuition or low-energy sanity, not as a load-bearing claim. Diagnostic content cannot upgrade an interface claim.

If a reviewer finds a sentence in this paper that asserts a CERTIFICATE-tier conclusion without naming the gate ID, the frozen inputs, the pass/fail criterion, and the downgrade rule, that sentence is a bug. The bug-report routing rule is: identify the UQF row, identify the missing piece in §3's per-row template, and the claim downgrades per §3's downgrade ladder. This is the same discipline Paper 2 uses for C-FF rows.


---

## 9. The inversion: the stack is the test

This build organizes the paper around the move its two predecessors made canonical. The seventeen-row UQF stack of §3 is read in two tenses at once. Prospectively, it is the **construction filter**: Phases 1 through 7 are gated row by row — no section may quantize an object, claim a tier, or invoke an authority except through a §3 row's template (purpose, certificate, frozen inputs, pass/fail, downgrade, status, C-FF consumption), and §3.0 declares any sentence that escapes this routing a drafting bug. Retrospectively, the same seventeen rows are the **test battery**: §19 keys every falsification path to a UQF ID, and §20's aggregate statement is computed, not asserted. One list, two tenses — the stack that built the paper is the stack that grades it.

**The circularity objection, answered in this paper's own currency.** *If the chapters were written to the gate templates, don't they pass the gates by construction?* No — and here the defense is sharper than in Papers I and II, because this paper's gates carry **tiers**:

1. **Tiers are earned, not declared.** Writing a chapter to a row's template buys, at most, INTERFACE. The ladder of §3.2.3 (INTERFACE < AUDIT < CANDIDATE < CERTIFICATE) is climbed only by named, frozen arguments meeting the row's pass/fail criterion, and §3.4.4's honest-status rule makes any aggregate sentence stronger than the computed minimum a bug by definition. Eight rows of this very paper sit at AUDIT — the construction visibly did not pre-pay them.
2. **No row passes alone.** The coupling layer of §3.4.2 entangles the rows: an anomaly failure (UQF-4) drags five rows down a tier; losing UV completion (UQF-9) strips CERTIFICATE from four. A construction that satisfied each template separately would still owe the joint conditions — one positivity statement, one anomaly closure, one UV route — on a single Hilbert space.
3. **The ledger is the over-determination.** §4's reading rule is symmetric: every quantized object must be registered (no silent introductions) *and* every registered object must be consumed (no decorative rows). Nine rows, all load-bearing, with the UQF↔ledger bipartite graph closed in both directions (§4.4) — the same nine objects must simultaneously satisfy seventeen gates.
4. **The falsifiers stay live, and the map audits itself.** Every row carries a downgrade rule; UQF-16 certifies the downgrade map's completeness and is self-applying — an incomplete failure map fails the paper in aggregate.

The identity is, once again, the honesty mechanism rather than the loophole: one published stack means there is no private standard for building that differs from the public standard for judging.

## 10. Seventeen gates, one number

Here is this paper's front-page result, stated the way the min-rule demands it be stated. The unified quantum-force-completion claim is exactly as strong as its weakest gate:

$$\Sigma \;=\; \min_{k\in\{0,\ldots,16\}}\sigma_k.$$

The scoreboard below is the authoritative per-row tier ledger (auto-derived from §3.3 with the §3.8 phase-close reconciliations applied; any aggregate-tier sentence anywhere in this paper that disagrees with this table is a drafting bug per §3.4.4):

> **Namespace key (read before chasing any "11").** Three numbering systems share the digits in this paper, and a reader following a row ID from this scoreboard can collide them. (i) **UQF-*n*** are the *seventeen audit gates* — the rows of the scoreboard below and of §3.3 (so UQF-11 = *nonperturbative QCD*, AUDIT). (ii) **UQFC-*n*** are the *numbered chapters* of THIS paper (so UQFC-11 is a chapter, e.g. a fermion chapter — not a gate). (iii) **UQC-*n*** is the *retired* prior backbone; its rows, and the old "UQF-11 (dark matter)" of that earlier hybrid numbering, are **moved to Paper 4 reserve** and are not gates here. When in doubt, the full prior-row-to-gate crosswalk is the §3.5 mapping table. Throughout this scoreboard and §3.3, "UQF-11" always means the nonperturbative-QCD audit gate.

| Gate | Name | Tier | Discharged in | If AUDIT: what raises it |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| UQF-0 | Active-branch inheritance | **CERTIFICATE** | §2 | — |
| UQF-1 | Quantum object ledger | **CANDIDATE** | §4 | — |
| UQF-2 | Canonical / path-integral equivalence | **CANDIDATE** | §5 | — |
| UQF-3 | Physical Hilbert space | **CANDIDATE** | §6 | — |
| UQF-4 | BRST/BV nilpotency and anomaly closure | **AUDIT** | §7 | Phase-4 anomaly lift under 4D descent |
| UQF-5 | Graviton certificate | **CANDIDATE** | §8 | — |
| UQF-6 | Gauge-boson certificate | **CANDIDATE** | §9 | — |
| UQF-7 | Fermion quantization | **AUDIT** | §11 | Phase-3 no-light-mirror verification |
| UQF-8 | Higgs / Goldstone quantum certificate | **CANDIDATE** | §10 | — |
| UQF-9 | UV-completion certificate | **AUDIT** | §14 | non-Gaussian fixed point at declared truncation (global open problem) |
| UQF-10 | Quantum compactification stability | **AUDIT** | §15 | blocked by UQF-9 (loop control of moduli potential) |
| UQF-11 | Nonperturbative QCD | **AUDIT** | §12 | named lattice / partner-community program |
| UQF-12 | Strong CP | **AUDIT** | §13 | nEDM falsifier on boundary-parity candidate (LOW conf.) |
| UQF-13 | Precision-force phenomenology | **CANDIDATE** | §16 | — |
| UQF-14 | Unitarity / causality / locality audit | **AUDIT** | §17 | graviton-sector unitarity above cutoff (UQF-9) |
| UQF-15 | No-hidden-sector force leakage | **AUDIT** | §18 | §4 ledger exhaustiveness + Phase-4 audit |
| UQF-16 | Final downgrade map | **CANDIDATE** | §19 | — |

**Aggregate: Σ = min over rows = AUDIT** (per §3.4.3).

**The number: Σ = AUDIT.** The paper claims precisely that and no more — a unified quantum-completion *audit* of the four force interfaces, with frozen gate-by-gate accounting of what is closed (the linearized force carriers, the framework equivalence, the object ledger, the downgrade map), what is candidate (positivity, Higgs at tree level, Tier-1 precision specification), and what holds the aggregate at AUDIT (the eight AUDIT rows in the table above). Raising Σ to CANDIDATE is the declared Phase-7 target and requires exactly those eight rows; raising it to CERTIFICATE requires the named partner-community executions. No sentence in this paper outranks this table.

**The secondary count.** Every quantum object in all four forces traces to **nine ledger rows** (§4) — three metric blocks, the descended connections, one generation of chiral matter, one Higgs doublet, the KK tower, ghosts, antifields — with zero objects introduced outside the ledger and zero rows left unconsumed. Seventeen gates, nine objects, one number.

### Intuition pump: what the UQF stack and the Σ scoreboard actually mean

The machinery above — a seventeen-row "gate stack," a min-rule, a scoreboard whose headline is the worst row — is abstract on first contact. Here is each load-bearing object in one plain image, with the precise statement kept right beside it so the analogy is an on-ramp, never a replacement.

- **The UQF gate stack — *a seventeen-station safety inspection for a bridge.*** *Plain:* before a bridge opens, an inspector checks the welds, the cables, the bearings, the deck — station by station — and the bridge opens only when *each* station signs off. The UQF stack is that inspection for a quantum theory of forces: seventeen named checks (ghost cancellation, anomaly closure, positive-norm states, a stable vacuum, and so on), each with a written pass/fail rule it must meet (§3.3). *Why it does the work:* a theory cannot quietly skip the station it is failing, because every claim downstream is required to cite the station that licenses it — an unrouted claim is, by the paper's own rule, a drafting bug (§3.0).
- **The min-rule (Σ = min over rows) — *a chain rated by its weakest link, in public.*** *Plain:* a chain that holds a ton at sixteen links and a hundred pounds at one link is a hundred-pound chain — you quote the weakest link, not the average. The scoreboard's headline tier $\Sigma$ is exactly that: the **minimum** over all seventeen gates (§3.4.3), so the eight rows still at AUDIT (anomaly lift, fermion descent, UV completion, compactification stability, nonperturbative QCD, strong CP, unitarity above cutoff, hidden-sector closure) hold the whole paper at **AUDIT** no matter how strong the closed rows are. *Why it does the work:* the rule makes self-flattery structurally impossible — any sentence that quotes a tier above the computed minimum is, by §3.4.4, a bug, so the paper *cannot* advertise more than its weakest gate earns.
- **The Σ scoreboard at AUDIT — *a report card that prints the failing grade on the cover.*** *Plain:* most theories lead with their best result; this one leads with its worst, because the min-rule forces the cover number to be the weakest gate's. AUDIT is not a disappointment here — it is the honest readout of a programme that has genuinely-open problems (a Clay Millennium problem among them) inside its declared scope and refuses to round up. *Why it does the work:* a scoreboard you cannot game is a scoreboard worth reading — the AUDIT rows are *routed to the top* (§19, §3.3) so a hostile reviewer finds the weak links first, exactly where the paper put them.

*The takeaway:* the stack, the min-rule, and the AUDIT headline are one honesty mechanism wearing three faces — Σ = AUDIT is the paper telling you, on its first page, exactly how far it has gotten and exactly what is not yet done.


---

## 11. Corpus reconciliation to TOE_FINAL v6–v15 (2026-06-12)

*Added in the Phase-1.5 reconciliation pass. This section does not change any UQF tier (zero promotions — see the closing rule of this section); it cross-references the governing TOE_FINAL capsule so the reader can see, in one place, which of this paper's AUDIT rows now inherit a newer corpus result, and exactly what part of each row remains the paper's own open obligation.*

**Why this section exists.** This paper was drafted on 2026-06-08, before the TOE_FINAL capsule ran its v6→v15 session (2026-06-11/12). In that session the corpus did, by its *own* native-three-layer machinery (the stabilization object $V(\sigma)$, the graded supertrace, the Spohn monotone), several computations that *touch* the same physics three of this paper's AUDIT rows are gated on — most importantly quantum compactification stability and the cosmological-constant / vacuum-energy line. A row that defers to "a calculation that has not been performed" is **stale** if the corpus has since performed an adjacent calculation. The honest fix is *not* to relabel this paper's rows (that is a promotion, reserved for the countersign instrument) but to **cite the governing capsule and re-state each row's dependency precisely**: what the corpus now supplies, and what genuinely remains this paper's to close. Per the Phase-1.5 Manuscript Governance Pack (MR-1 completeness, MR-3 status labels, MR-4 zero promotions) and the campaign plan §2.B work order, the reconciliation is against the governing capsule **`TOE_FINAL (2).md`** (its v6→v15 entries; EXTERNAL corpus artifact); capsule references below are by **version label** (e.g. "TOE_FINAL v9") because capsule labels are stable while section numbers are not, and named computation packages (e.g. `gap04_frozen_package_native.json`) are cited as EXTERNAL artifacts. **No UQF row's tier is advanced by this section; the §10 / §3.3 / §20.2 tier ledgers stand unchanged.**

### 11.1 Cross-paper / external-reference convention (reading note)

This paper inherits its load-bearing closures from sibling artifacts and now from the TOE_FINAL capsule. Throughout the document, a reference of the form *"Paper 1 Appendix-(letter)"*, *"main GUT manuscript"*, *"Article A/B/C §…"*, *"C-FF0..C-FF14" (Paper 2)*, or *"TOE_FINAL vN"* names an **EXTERNAL corpus artifact**, not an in-document locator (MR-1.b). The authority for those closures lives in the named external artifact; this paper invokes them by interface only and does not re-close them. A bare Paper-1 appendix-letter reference in this paper always means *the correspondingly-lettered appendix of Paper 1 (the GUT manuscript)*; this paper's own and only appendix is Appendix U (Interface Certificate Registry). The completeness checker classifies un-namespaced Paper-1 appendix-letter mentions as unresolved because they are not formatted as named files; they are nonetheless EXTERNAL by this convention, and re-pointing each one into a named-file citation in place is a cross-reference-hygiene task outside this reconciliation's surgical scope (and is recorded as an explained exception in the campaign report).

# UQFC-1 — Claim Boundary: Unified Quantum Forces, Not Yet TOE
**Deferral target:** Paper 4 (TOE — cosmology, dark sector, baryogenesis, initial conditions, measurement, classicality)

This chapter draws the sharpest line in the paper. It states what is claimed (§1.1) and — at equal length and equal seriousness — what is *not yet* claimed and is handed to Paper 4 (§1.2), the invariants preserved unchanged from Papers 1 and 2 (§1.3), why the Paper 3 / Paper 4 split is a discipline rather than a hedge (§1.4), the status vocabulary every later label obeys (§1.5), the standalone-reading discipline (§1.6), and the bottom line (§1.7). A reader who internalizes only this chapter already knows the exact perimeter of the paper's ambition.

---

## 1.0 The hard claim boundary (opening statement)

> *This paper attempts unified quantum completion of the **force sectors only**. It does NOT yet claim a full theory of everything.*

Everything else in this paper is constrained by that boundary: any reviewer attack finding a sentence elsewhere inconsistent with it is, by construction, an attack on that other sentence — not on this one. The boundary is needed because the four-paper hierarchy places this paper between two natural pulls: the upward pull from Paper 2 (which closed the four force *interfaces* and which a casual reader might expect this paper to "upgrade" globally) and the upward pull toward Paper 4 (where TOE-tier questions live). Both pulls are honest in their own context, and both must be resisted here. This paper, in between, asks one and only one question:

> **Do the four force-sector interfaces admit honest quantum-field-theoretic completion as quantum force theories?**

That question is force-sector-only, not the TOE question; the TOE question subsumes it but is strictly larger, and Paper 4 owns that strictly-larger scope.

## 1.1 What this paper claims (the "Claimed" list)

Under declared assumptions and at the per-row status admitted by the UQF gate stack of §3, this paper claims the following:

- **Quantum gravity sector.** The metric block $G_{\mu\nu}$ of the active branch admits quantization with a physical spin-2 massless graviton mode at the linearized level, under BRST/BV gauge fixing inherited from the active branch and with positivity certified on the physical Hilbert space defined in §6. The interface-level claim is that the perturbative graviton sector is well-defined; the certificate-level claim is the UQF-5 graviton certificate of §8 closed at the tier the UV-completion certificate of §14 admits.
- **Quantized gauge sectors.** The descended 4D connections $A_\mu^a$ for $SU(3)_c$, $SU(2)_L$, and $U(1)_Y$ — the latter two combining into $SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y \to U(1)_{\rm em}$ after electroweak breaking — admit canonical quantization with correct polarization counts (two transverse for the photon and gluons; two transverse plus a longitudinal-from-Goldstone for each massive $W^\pm/Z^0$), and BRST-positive physical states. This is the UQF-6 gauge-boson certificate of §9.
- **Chiral matter coupling.** The matter bundle $\mathcal E_{\rm matter}$ inherited from Paper 1 and Paper 2 admits quantization of one full generation of left-handed Weyl fermions without mirror partners, with anomaly cancellation as inherited (Paper 1 closure; this paper invokes by interface). The interface-level claim is no-mirrors; the certificate-level claim is the UQF-7 fermion certificate of §11, gated by the anomaly closure of §7 and by the no-double-counting discipline of C-FF5 (inherited from Paper 2).
- **Higgs / electroweak quantum sector.** The Higgs $\otimes$-layer object $H$ admits separation into one physical Higgs scalar plus three eaten Goldstones (which provide the longitudinal polarizations of $W^\pm/Z^0$), with a stable vacuum at the tree level and main-manuscript-certificate authority for higher-order vacuum stability. This is the UQF-8 Higgs/Goldstone certificate of §10.
- **Nonperturbative QCD status.** This paper inherits the Paper 2 §7 strong-sector interface and provides a route to nonperturbative QCD (confinement, mass gap, chiral dynamics) compatible with the $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ structure. The certificate is the UQF-11 row of §12. The claim is *route* and *compatibility*, not closure of the Yang-Mills mass-gap Clay Millennium problem. The route names the necessary upstream inputs (UV completion via §14; compactification stability via §15) and the partner-community work (lattice QCD comparison, hadronic spectrum fit) that would, in principle, close it.
- **Strong-CP status.** The candidate structural mechanism for the $\bar\theta$ problem is named (the $S^1_Y / \mathbb Z_2$ boundary-parity candidate from the corpus, with the Peccei-Quinn axion as fallback). This is the UQF-12 row of §13. The claim is *candidate naming with named falsifier*, not solution; the 1.64-rad spin-c-holonomy tension with the nEDM bound recorded in the corpus is preserved honestly as a falsification surface.
- **Force-sector precision predictions.** This paper inherits the Paper 2 §11 sanity targets and provides a precision-phenomenology framework for the force sectors only: EWPO, CKM/PMNS structure, proton-lifetime structure, KK-threshold structure. The Tier-1 specification (what numerical work is required, with which constraint experiment and which partner toolchain) is the UQF-13 row of §16. Numerical predictions are explicitly deferred to partner-community execution; the present paper does not produce them.

Each of the above is gated by a specific UQF row in §3 and consumes specific ledger rows from §4. The certificate tier of each is the tier the UQF row admits at frozen status; in no case is the claim asserted above its row's tier.

## 1.2 What this paper does **not** claim (the "Not Claimed Yet" list)

The following are explicitly deferred to Paper 4. The deferral is not a downgrade; it is a scoping statement. Each item is real, each is named honestly, and each will be picked up by Paper 4 with its own certificate stack.

- **Complete cosmology.** Inflation, reheating, the CMB power spectrum, structure formation, the $H_0$ tension, and the cosmological-constant problem are not addressed in this paper. They are Paper 4 material. The UQC-5 audit of the prior companion series surveyed the cosmology sub-gates honestly; that survey moves to Paper 4 reserve.
- **Dark matter.** No dark-matter candidate is proposed in this paper. The five candidate classes enumerated in the prior UQC-6 audit (with a lean toward $S^1/\mathbb Z_2$ boundary-localized hidden modes) are Paper 4 reserve material. No unique selection is claimed.
- **Dark energy.** The cosmological-constant problem is not solved in this paper, and the $\Lambda$-1 placeholder of the corpus is preserved as a placeholder, not converted to a mechanism. Paper 4 reserve.
- **Baryogenesis.** BG-10 remains *Open / Diagnostic* per the 2026-06-04 audit closure. The first-pass $R = 1.0001$ at $z_1 = -0.07 - 1.35 i$ result of 2026-06-04 was withdrawn the same day after deep audit, and the four physics fixes for any future BG-10 attempt (canonical CI; proper $\Delta L = 2$; $N_2, N_3$ damping; density-matrix flavor evolution) are recorded in the corpus. This paper does **not** litigate BG-10, does not modify its status, and does not include any baryogenesis content. BG-10 is Paper 4 material.
- **Initial conditions.** The selection of initial conditions for the active branch, the boundary-parity data on $S^1_Y / \mathbb Z_2$, and the question of why this branch rather than a competing branch are all Paper 4 questions. This paper takes the active branch as given (Paper 1 closure).
- **The measurement problem.** Quantum-to-classical reduction, the Born rule, and the interpretation of measurement are not addressed.
- **The emergence of classicality.** Decoherence, einselection, and the macroscopic limit are not addressed.
- **"Why this universe rather than another."** The anthropic / multiverse / cosmological-selection question is not addressed.
- **A complete theory of everything.** No TOE claim is made. The strongest claim available from this paper alone is "candidate unified quantum-force completion under declared assumptions" (minimum-viable tier) or "certificate-complete unified quantum force theory under declared assumptions" (strong tier); see §3 for the per-gate tier ladder.

## 1.3 What this paper preserves (status invariants)

The following invariants from Paper 1 and Paper 2 are preserved without modification:

- **Hard-gate vector.** $\mathsf{D},\ \mathsf{D}\text{-local},\ \mathsf{D},\ \mathsf{D},\ \mathsf{D}$ — unchanged.
- **SoT hash.** `88e5903fe1c3d17655acef7e4fb45078e3168add25362040e21598b3b161ff17` — unchanged.
- **Stage B iter-4e FINAL-WINNER-SCIENCE-PASS** — unchanged.
- **C-FF0..C-FF14** of Paper 2 — unchanged; this paper extends, does not replace.
- **BG-10 = Open / Diagnostic** — unchanged; deferred to Paper 4.
- **Filed-patent material, NRC packet, SoT manuscript, baryogenesis_build** — no edits.
- **Article C §8.2** — not modified; only extended elsewhere via parallel derivation if at all.
- **candidate-improvement-9-spec and candidate-improvement-10-spec** — retain spec status.

The certificate philosophy of this paper is **"Chris does the physics."** Agents organize, audit, and draft. Agents do not invent new physics, do not fabricate certificates for open problems, and do not edit frozen artifacts.

## 1.4 Why the Paper 3 / Paper 4 split matters

A reasonable reviewer will ask: if Paper 4 is going to address cosmology, dark sectors, and baryogenesis later anyway, why not roll Paper 3 and Paper 4 into one document?

The answer is that the four-force quantum-completion question is structurally separable from the cosmology / dark / baryogenesis / initial-conditions question — the force question is framework-internal (UV physics, nonperturbative IR, anomaly closure, positivity), while the TOE-tier questions need a much wider input set (cosmological initial data, observational cosmology, the emergence of classicality) with different techniques and different partner communities. The load-bearing reason to split, not merely the tidy one: conflating them has a **known failure mode**, exhibited by the prior UQC companion series — a 21-row UQF-0..UQF-20 hybrid that mixed cosmology rows in with force-completion rows and therefore landed at AUDIT overall, because the AUDIT-tier cosmology rows dragged the min-rule aggregate down even where the force-completion rows would have admitted a stronger tier. Splitting the questions cleanly is what lets the force-completion question aggregate honestly within its own scope.

Hence the corpus discipline: **Paper 3 = force sectors only, UQF-0..UQF-16 (17 gates); Paper 4 = TOE, separate gate stack to be defined.** This paper is the Paper 3 instantiation.

## 1.5 The status vocabulary used in this paper

The following labels are used throughout. They are inherited from Paper 2's Section 2.3 and extended with new UQF-specific labels for this paper.

| Status label | Meaning | Origin |
|---|---|---|
| **Interface claim** | The routing or compatibility statement is defined and the relevant pieces mesh, but no certificate has been earned at this paper's tier. | Paper 2 §2.3 |
| **Main-manuscript certificate** | The underlying detailed gate certificate, freeze record, or frozen appendix authority lives in Paper 1 (main GUT manuscript) and is invoked here only by interface. | Paper 2 §2.3 |
| **Diagnostic / illustrative** | The item is included for physical intuition or low-energy sanity, not as a load-bearing claim of this paper. Cannot upgrade an interface claim. | Paper 2 §2.3 |
| **Outside this paper's scope** | The item is not claimed here; deferred to Paper 4 or to a separate companion treatment. | Paper 2 §2.3 |
| **Quantum object** | A named entity in the quantum object ledger of §4: classical source, layer assignment, quantum entity, and required test all specified. | UQFC-4 |
| **Physical Hilbert space** | The positive-norm subspace surviving the gauge quotient defined in §6; quantum states of the framework live here. | UQFC-6, gate UQF-3 |
| **Positivity certificate** | A named, frozen argument that a candidate Hilbert subspace has nonnegative inner product on physical states. | UQFC-6, gate UQF-3 |
| **UV-completion certificate** | A named, frozen argument that the framework is well-defined at arbitrarily high energy (e.g., asymptotic-safety fixed point, string-theoretic embedding, or equivalent). | UQFC-14, gate UQF-9 |
| **Anomaly closure certificate** | A named, frozen argument that all chiral / gauge / mixed anomalies cancel on the physical-state space. | UQFC-7, gate UQF-4 |
| **Downgrade rule** | The per-row consequence stated in §3 if the named certificate is not earned. | UQFC-3, gate UQF-16 |

Earlier internal project labels (CB, GCC, SCC, WCC, ECC, rTT) and Stage 6 / Stage 7 status terminology are not used as formal statuses in this paper, consistent with Paper 2's Section 2.3 discipline.

## 1.6 The reading discipline

This paper carries a standalone-reading discipline analogous to Paper 2's:

> *A mathematically literate physicist must be able to evaluate the unified-quantum-force-completion claim of this paper from this paper alone, using Paper 1 for detailed gate certificates and Paper 2 for the four-force interface backbone, but without needing any other corpus document.*

Two consequences follow. First, this paper carries enough quantization machinery — canonical, BV-BRST, path-integral, and Hilbert-space content — to make every UQF row evaluable without external lookup. Second, this paper does **not** reproduce Paper 1's freeze records, does **not** reproduce Paper 2's C-FF0..C-FF14 derivation, and does **not** reproduce any per-sector content from Paper 2's Sections 6 through 9 except by interface reference. The interface references are stated in §2 and tabulated in Paper 2's Appendix B (Force-Routing Tables) — an EXTERNAL artifact of the **Fable_Forces** build named in §2.6; this paper's own and only appendix is Appendix U.

## 1.7 Bottom line

The claim boundary is sharp and asymmetric:

- **Upward boundary** (toward Paper 4): the moment the discussion turns to cosmology, dark, baryogenesis, initial conditions, or the measurement problem, the discussion has left this paper's scope.
- **Downward boundary** (toward Paper 2): the moment the discussion turns to whether the four-force interfaces themselves are mutually compatible (rather than whether they admit *quantum* completion), the discussion is Paper 2 content already.

The space between those two boundaries — and only that space — is what this paper attempts. The next section (§2) makes precise what this paper imports from Paper 1 and Paper 2. The section after that (§3) defines the UQF-0..UQF-16 gate stack that polices everything that happens inside the boundary.


---


# UQFC-2 — Imported Active Branch and Four-Force Constraint Backbone
* · gate UQF-0 · drafted 2026-06-08*

> **Gate card — UQF-0: Active-branch inheritance** *(auto-derived from §3.3 / §4.4, the single source of truth per §3.0; any discrepancy with this chapter is a drafting bug)*
>
> | Field | Value |
> |---|---|
> | Tier | **CERTIFICATE** (this paper is held to the inheritance discipline by construction). |
> | Required certificate | A statement that this paper's quantization uses identically the active branch of Paper 1; the layer separation of Paper 2 is preserved; no implicit branch substitution occurs anywhere in §§4 through 20. |
> | Frozen inputs | Paper 1 active-branch selection certificate; Paper 2 §4 active-branch restatement. |
> | Pass / fail | Pass: the §4 ledger and every certificate in §§8 through 18 reference the same branch object. Fail: any downstream section quantizes on a different background. |
> | Downgrade | Any UQF row that quantizes on a non-inherited background is removed from this paper's stack and the row's claim is withdrawn. |
> | C-FF rows consumed | C-FF0, C-FF1, C-FF13. |
> | Ledger rows consumed (§4.4) | all (defines the branch every row lives on) |

**Imports from:** Paper 1 (main GUT manuscript), Paper 2 (`https://physics.magflowmeters.com/gut/quantum_forces/quantum_forces.md`)
**Discipline:** interface-only inheritance; no duplication of source-paper content; no edits to any source-paper artifact.

---

## 2.0 Purpose

This section names exactly what is inherited from Paper 1 and Paper 2 and what is **not** re-derived in this paper. The reason for fixing this at the front of the paper is honest scoping: every UQF gate in §3 that reads "inherits from Paper 1" or "inherits from Paper 2" must point to a row in this section, and every claim later in the paper that uses inherited content must be checkable against this section.

The discipline is **interface-only inheritance**: the import is by reference, not by re-derivation. Paper 1 is the authority for the active branch and for the main-manuscript gate certificates; Paper 2 is the authority for the C-FF0..C-FF14 constraint backbone and for the four force-sector projection maps. This paper does not re-do either source paper's work.

---

## 2.1 Imported active branch (from Paper 1)

This paper inherits the active branch selected by Paper 1's constraint method. The subsections below fix the imported parent geometry (§2.1.1), name the three-layer structure that survives the import (the geometry, the rulebook, the fields — §2.1.2), and state precisely which Paper 1 closures travel with it as interface authority rather than being re-derived here.

### 2.1.1 The active 13D parent geometry

The active branch is

$$
M_{13} = M_{3,1} \times K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1
$$

with $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ and $T^2 \simeq U(1)^2$. The 4D spacetime is $M_{3,1} \equiv \mathcal M_4$. The $S^1$ is the hypercharge circle $S^1_Y$; it carries a $\mathbb Z_2$ boundary structure used downstream in the strong-CP discussion of §13.

The dimension breakdown $13 = 4 + 6 + 2 + 1$ is fixed. This paper does not litigate alternative branches; Paper 1's constraint method is the authority for the active-branch selection.

### 2.1.2 The layer separation

The Paper 1 / Paper 2 layer discipline separates objects into three layers:

- **The geometry** ($\times$ layer) — base geometry: the manifold factors and their metric blocks.
- **The rulebook** ($\oplus$ layer) — finite rule constraints: the admissibility constraints (which configurations are allowed), freeze records, and discrete bookkeeping.
- **The fields** ($\otimes$ layer) — field / operator bundles: matter, gauge, Higgs, and proton-decay operators.

The active branch in layered notation is

$$
\mathfrak B_{\rm active} = [\mathcal M_4 \times K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y] \oplus [F^+_{\rm finite} \oplus \mathcal C_{\rm admiss}] \otimes [\mathcal E_{\rm matter} \oplus \mathcal E_{\rm gauge} \oplus \mathcal E_{\rm Higgs} \oplus \mathcal E_{\rm proton}].
$$

This paper inherits the layer separation as-is. Every quantum object in the ledger of §4 is assigned to its inherited layer, and the layer assignment is one of the things UQF-1 (quantum object ledger) certifies.

### 2.1.3 The matter bundle and the gauge bundle

$\mathcal E_{\rm matter}$ is the inherited matter bundle: one full generation of left-handed Weyl fermions, $(Q_L, u_R^c, d_R^c, L, e_R^c)$ in the standard hypercharge assignment, with the family/generation structure as in Paper 1. $\mathcal E_{\rm gauge}$ is the descended gauge bundle hosting the 4D connections $A_\mu^a$ for $SU(3)_c$, $SU(2)_L$, and $U(1)_Y$, with $U(1)_{\rm em}$ emerging post-EWSB. $\mathcal E_{\rm Higgs}$ is the Higgs bundle hosting the doublet $H$ that becomes the physical scalar plus eaten Goldstones after breaking.

This paper does not modify any of these bundle assignments. They are inputs.

### 2.1.4 Frozen authority that this paper does **not** re-close

Per Paper 2's C-FF13 discipline (main-manuscript authority constraint), the following pieces are invoked here only by interface and are not re-litigated:

- **Hard-gate vector.** $\mathsf{D},\ \mathsf{D}\text{-local},\ \mathsf{D},\ \mathsf{D},\ \mathsf{D}$. Authority: Paper 1, frozen.
- **SoT hash.** `88e5903fe1c3d17655acef7e4fb45078e3168add25362040e21598b3b161ff17`. Authority: Paper 1, frozen.
- **Active-branch selection certificate.** Authority: Paper 1, frozen. The argument that eliminates competing branches and selects $M_{13} = M_{3,1} \times K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1$ is the main-manuscript content; this paper takes the outcome as given.
- **Stage B iter-4e FINAL-WINNER-SCIENCE-PASS.** Authority: Paper 1, frozen.
- **Proton-safety certificate.** Authority: Paper 1, frozen; consumed by the no-double-counting discipline of §3 and indirectly by UQF-7 (fermion certificate) and UQF-15 (no-hidden-force leakage).
- **Anomaly ledger.** Authority: Paper 1, frozen; consumed by UQF-4 (BRST/BV nilpotency and anomaly closure) and UQF-7 (fermion quantization).
- **Flavor structure.** Authority: Paper 1, frozen; consumed by UQF-13 (precision-force phenomenology).

If at any point a UQF gate in §3 appears to require modifying one of the above, the modification is out of scope, the gate downgrades, and the reason is recorded.

### 2.1.5 Honest inheritance qualifier

The active-branch import is by reference and is honest. Specifically: this paper does **not** claim that quantizing on $\mathfrak B_{\rm active}$ retro-justifies Paper 1's selection. The arrow runs only forward: Paper 1 selected $\mathfrak B_{\rm active}$; this paper asks whether quantization on that fixed background is consistent. Failure of the present paper's quantization program would not invalidate Paper 1's selection certificate; success would not upgrade it. The two questions are independent at the certificate level.

---

## 2.2 Imported four-force constraint backbone (from Paper 2)

This paper inherits Paper 2's Four-Force Constraint Backbone, C-FF0 through C-FF14, in its entirety. The subsections below state why the backbone is imported rather than re-derived (§2.2.1), enumerate the fifteen constraints and the role each plays as an interface obligation on this paper's quantization, and fix the no-double-counting discipline (C-FF5) that prevents a closure being claimed twice across the paper boundary.

### 2.2.1 Why the backbone is imported

Paper 2's backbone is the discipline that prevents the four force-sector treatments from drifting into four independent EFT summaries with incompatible conventions. The UQF stack of §3 sits *above* the C-FF backbone — that is, UQF gates assume the C-FF discipline holds — and the upgrade is from interface-level compatibility (Paper 2's question) to quantum-completion-level certificate (this paper's question). UQF cannot be defined without C-FF, because every UQF row that quantizes an object must first know that the object is layer-disciplined, projection-specified, and so on.

### 2.2.2 The fourteen-row C-FF backbone (restatement of authority only)

The fourteen C-FF rows are restated here as inherited authority. The full statement, "what it forces," and "failure if absent" wording is in Paper 2 §2.6 and is not reproduced.

| C-FF ID | One-line gloss | Paper-2 authority |
|---|---|---|
| C-FF0 | one parent geometry | §2.6 |
| C-FF1 | layer discipline | §2.6 |
| C-FF2 | projection specification | §2.6 |
| C-FF3 | shared matter bundle | §2.6 |
| C-FF4 | charge normalization $Q = T_3 + Y$ | §2.6 |
| C-FF5 | no double counting | §2.6 |
| C-FF6 | gauge-origin discipline (gauge fields are descended actors) | §2.6 |
| C-FF7 | gravity/gauge separation (metric blocks not conflated) | §2.6 |
| C-FF8 | QED downstream of EW | §2.6 |
| C-FF9 | regulator / RG compatibility | §2.6 |
| C-FF10 | anomaly compatibility | §2.6 |
| C-FF11 | low-energy sanity target | §2.6 |
| C-FF12 | scope-boundary discipline | §2.6 |
| C-FF13 | main-manuscript authority | §2.6 |
| C-FF14 | falsification path | §2.6 |

UQF gates in §3 routinely consume C-FF rows. The mapping is:

- UQF-0 (active-branch inheritance) consumes C-FF0, C-FF1, C-FF13.
- UQF-1 (quantum object ledger) consumes C-FF1 (layer), C-FF7 (gravity/gauge separation), C-FF6 (gauge-origin).
- UQF-2 (canonical / path-integral equivalence) consumes C-FF9 (regulator compatibility).
- UQF-3 (physical Hilbert space) consumes C-FF5 (no double counting).
- UQF-4 (BRST/BV nilpotency and anomaly closure) consumes C-FF10 (anomaly compatibility).
- UQF-5 (graviton certificate) consumes C-FF7 (gravity/gauge separation) and C-FF6 (gauge-origin).
- UQF-6 (gauge-boson certificate) consumes C-FF3 (shared matter), C-FF4 (charge norm), C-FF6 (gauge-origin), C-FF8 (QED downstream).
- UQF-7 (fermion quantization) consumes C-FF3 (shared matter), C-FF5 (no double counting), C-FF10 (anomaly).
- UQF-8 (Higgs / Goldstone) consumes C-FF8 (QED downstream of EW) and C-FF10 (anomaly).
- UQF-9 (UV-completion certificate) consumes C-FF12 (scope-boundary), C-FF13 (main-manuscript authority).
- UQF-10 (quantum compactification stability) consumes C-FF1 (layer), C-FF7 (gravity/gauge).
- UQF-11 (nonperturbative QCD) consumes C-FF9 (regulator), C-FF11 (sanity target).
- UQF-12 (strong CP) consumes C-FF12 (scope-boundary), C-FF13 (main-manuscript authority), C-FF14 (falsification).
- UQF-13 (precision phenomenology) consumes C-FF4 (charge), C-FF9 (regulator), C-FF10 (anomaly), C-FF11 (sanity).
- UQF-14 (unitarity / causality / locality) consumes C-FF5 (no double counting).
- UQF-15 (no-hidden-force leakage) consumes C-FF5 (no double counting), C-FF8 (QED downstream).
- UQF-16 (final downgrade map) consumes C-FF14 (falsification path).

The full UQF → C-FF mapping is restated in §3 per row; the present subsection gives the inverse view, organized by C-FF row.

### 2.2.3 The four force-sector projection maps

Paper 2 §5 and §§6 through 9 define four projection maps from the active branch to the four force EFTs:

$$
\pi_{\rm grav}:\ \mathfrak B_{\rm active} \to \mathrm{EFT}_{\rm grav}, \qquad
\pi_{\rm strong}:\ \mathfrak B_{\rm active} \to \mathrm{EFT}_{\rm QCD},
$$
$$
\pi_{\rm weak}:\ \mathfrak B_{\rm active} \to \mathrm{EFT}_{\rm EW}, \qquad
\pi_{\rm QED}:\ \mathfrak B_{\rm active} \to \mathrm{EFT}_{\rm QED}.
$$

These maps are not re-derived in this paper. They are taken as defined inputs. The UQF program asks, for each, whether quantization on the projected EFT is consistent under BRST/BV gauge fixing, with positive physical Hilbert-space norm, and with anomaly closure.

A useful schematic of the layered question:

```
                    Paper 2 (interface) :  pi_X
B_active  ------------------------------>  EFT_X  (compatible projection)
                                              |
                    Paper 3 (this paper)       |  quantize, gauge-fix, certify
                                              v
                                         Q(EFT_X)   (quantum force theory)
```

Each `Q(EFT_X)` is what the UQF certificates of §§8 through 11 try to construct.

### 2.2.4 Scope-boundary inheritance

Paper 2's C-FF12 (scope-boundary constraint) prohibits Paper 2 from using excluded sectors — full QG UV completion, nonperturbative QCD, strong CP, cosmology, dark matter, dark energy, baryogenesis — to upgrade interface claims. This paper inherits that discipline and **extends** it: the upgrade target is force-sector quantum completion (UQF-0..UQF-16), and Paper 4 reserves (cosmology, dark, baryogenesis, initial conditions) remain prohibited as upgrade levers in this paper. In effect, this paper *partially lifts* the C-FF12 prohibition: nonperturbative QCD, strong CP, and quantum gravity UV are now in scope (UQF-9, UQF-11, UQF-12) but cosmology/dark/baryogenesis remain off-limits.

The partial lift is exactly the difference between Paper 2 and Paper 3, and it is exactly the reason the corpus required a new paper rather than an upgrade to Paper 2 in place.

---

## 2.3 What is **not** inherited (explicit non-imports)

Several pieces from the prior corpus are explicitly **not** inherited into this paper:

- **The UQC companion's UQF-0..UQF-20 hybrid backbone.** The prior 21-row hybrid included cosmology rows (UQF-10 cosmology, UQF-11 dark matter, UQF-12 dark energy, UQF-13 baryogenesis in that earlier numbering). This paper uses the new 17-row force-only stack UQF-0..UQF-16 defined in §3. The renumbering is intentional: every gate in this paper's stack is force-sector-only.
- **UQC-5 (cosmology), UQC-6 (dark sector), UQC-7 (baryogenesis).** Move to Paper 4 reserve. Not used in this paper.
- **Article B §4.4 $\Lambda$-1 placeholder.** Preserved in the corpus, deferred to Paper 4.
- **Appendix N arrow-of-time work.** Referenced in the corpus as ToE-extension, not required for GUT closure; deferred to Paper 4.

The non-imports are listed not because they are unimportant but because a reviewer should be able to find, at a glance, which corpus pieces are *not* in this paper's scope.

---

## 2.4 What this paper adds (the net-new content envelope)

Per the source handoff §3 ("Reuse from previously-drafted UQC companion"), the net-new content this paper produces, beyond what the prior UQC companion already drafted, is:

- **UQF-0** — active-branch inheritance (brief). This section, plus its restatement in §3.
- **UQF-1** — quantum object ledger. The §4 deliverable.
- **UQF-2** — canonical / path-integral equivalence. Phase-2 build.
- **UQF-3** — physical Hilbert space. Phase-2 build.
- **UQF-4** — BRST/BV nilpotency. Phase-4 build.
- **UQF-7** — fermion quantization. Phase-3 build.
- **UQF-14** — unitarity / causality / locality. Phase-4 build.
- **UQF-15** — no-hidden-force leakage. Phase-4 build.
- **UQF-16** — final downgrade map. Phase-7 build.

The non-net-new rows reuse UQC content with the new numbering: UQC-1 splits into UQF-9 + UQF-10; UQC-2 splits into UQF-5 + UQF-6 + UQF-8; UQC-3 maps to UQF-11; UQC-4 maps to UQF-12; UQC-8 maps to UQF-13; UQC-9 contributes the backbone vocabulary.

The drafting discipline for the reused rows is: **restate** the prior UQC content under the new force-only scope, **drop** any cosmology/dark/baryogenesis cross-references that would violate the Paper-3 claim boundary, and **upgrade** the row-status vocabulary to the new UQF labels (positivity certificate, UV-completion certificate, anomaly-closure certificate). The reuse does not modify the prior UQC files in-place; the present paper is a separate document tree under `unified_quantum_force_completion/`.
