## 2.5 Bottom line for §2

- Paper 1 supplies the active branch, the layer discipline, and the frozen authority (hard-gate vector, SoT hash, anomaly ledger, proton safety, flavor structure).
- Paper 2 supplies the C-FF0..C-FF14 backbone and the four force-sector projection maps $\pi_{\rm grav}, \pi_{\rm strong}, \pi_{\rm weak}, \pi_{\rm QED}$.
- This paper assumes both as inputs and adds nine net-new UQF rows plus a renumbered-and-rescoped reuse of the prior UQC content, restricted to the force-sector quantum-completion question.
- No edits to either source paper. No re-derivation of either source paper's content. No upgrade to either source paper's status (or downgrade, for that matter; if a UQF row fails, the consequence is a UQF-16 downgrade in this paper's status, not in Paper 1's or Paper 2's).

The next section (§3) defines the UQF-0..UQF-16 stack, the status vocabulary, and the per-gate downgrade ladder that police every claim built on top of these imports.


---

## 2.6 Named builds and the two-hop downgrade inheritance

**Named builds.** Throughout this paper, *Paper 1 / the main GUT manuscript* means the **Fable_GUT** build (organized around the gate–constraint inversion, §1.3; the two-anchor fixing, Section 8; certificate registry R0.R; an earlier draft circulated as *final_manuscript*). *Paper 2 / the four-force interface* means the **Fable_Forces** build (the C-FF backbone run through the inversion, §1.2; coverage master table, §5.6; Q-certificate registry, Appendix Q). Paper 2's module-level numbering (the §6/§7/§8/§9 force modules and the §1–§5 spine) is preserved in that build, so every "Paper 2 §6.x / §7.x / §8.x / §9.x / §2.6 / §5.4" citation in this paper resolves to the same module of **Fable_Forces**; deep sub-locators quoted from the prior Paper 2 draft (*quantum_forces.md* — e.g. the §6.3a equivalence-principle check, the §6.9.3a Einstein-frame caveat) resolve inside the named module through that build's own ladder (its §6.6.3.3a Einstein-frame caveat / §6.6.3.3b universal-coupling test) and per-section mapping (the Fable_Forces build header and §5.6 master coverage table; EXTERNAL).

**Two-hop inheritance, binding and one-way.** Downgrades flow forward only:

| Hop | Rule |
|---|---|
| Paper 1 → Paper 2 | Per Fable_Forces §14.3: a Paper 1 gate downgrade automatically downgrades the C-FF rows that consume it. |
| Paper 2 → Paper 3 | Per §3.4.2 final row of this paper: a C-FF downgrade drops every UQF row that lists it under "C-FF rows consumed" by one tier — and hence, by the min-rule, can lower Σ directly. |

Composed: a single Paper 1 gate failure can propagate Gate → C-FF → UQF → Σ with no renegotiation at any hop. The converse never holds at either hop: nothing in this paper upgrades, re-closes, or substitutes for a C-FF row or a Paper 1 gate (C-FF13; UQF-0's own pass/fail). Worked example of the full chain: Paper 1 Gate 5 (anomaly) ↦ C-FF10 ↦ UQF-4, which by §3.4.2 drags UQF-3/5/6/7/8 one tier each ↦ Σ falls. The inheritance is what makes the three papers one auditable object rather than three documents that cite each other.


# UQFC-3 — UQF Gate Stack and Status Vocabulary

This chapter is the paper's instrument panel. It states the purpose of a gate stack (§3.0), why the count is seventeen force-sector rows and not the older twenty-one (§3.1), the fixed status vocabulary every quantitative claim downstream must wear (§3.2), the seventeen rows themselves with their certificates and downgrade rules (§3.3), the per-gate downgrade ladder (§3.4), the auto-derived master coverage table that is the single source of truth (§3.7), and the phase-close reconciliation ledger (§3.8). Everything after this chapter is graded against the rows defined here.

## 3.0 Purpose

This section is the certificate spine of the paper. Every claim made in §§5 through 20 routes back to one of the 17 UQF rows defined here. Every row carries:

1. **Purpose statement** — what physical question the gate answers.
2. **Required certificate** — the named object whose construction or invocation closes the row.
3. **Frozen inputs** — what is taken as given (from Paper 1, Paper 2, or earlier UQF rows).
4. **Pass/fail criterion** — what success looks like and what failure looks like.
5. **Downgrade rule** — the consequence in the paper if the certificate is not earned.
6. **Status vocabulary** — the label from §3.2 that summarizes the current row state.
7. **C-FF rows consumed** — Paper 2 backbone rows that the gate assumes.

A reviewer who finds a sentence in §§5 through 20 whose certificate, frozen inputs, pass/fail criterion, or downgrade rule cannot be traced to a row here is finding a drafting bug.

---

## 3.1 Why 17 rows, not 21

The prior UQC companion drafted a 21-row UQF-0..UQF-20 hybrid backbone (UQC-9). That backbone served the UQC scope, which was a 9-extension companion covering UV completion, force carriers, nonperturbative QCD, strong CP, **cosmology, dark sector, baryogenesis**, and precision phenomenology, plus a disciplinary-gates layer. Four of those rows (UQC-10..UQC-13 in the prior numbering, mapping to cosmology / dark matter / dark energy / baryogenesis) are out of scope for this Paper 3 by §1's hard claim boundary. They move to Paper 4 reserve.

The remaining rows, restated under the new force-only scope and the new naming, give the 17 rows below. The renumbering is deliberate: UQF-0..UQF-16 in this paper means *force-sector-only*; any reviewer who finds a "UQF-17" or later in this paper is finding a drafting bug.

The full mapping between the prior 21-row stack and this paper's 17-row stack is given in §3.4.

---

## 3.2 Status vocabulary

Three vocabulary layers are used. The Paper-2 vocabulary is inherited; the UQF-specific vocabulary is new to this paper; the tier vocabulary is the aggregate-tier convention from the prior UQC companion adapted to this paper's scope.

### 3.2.1 Inherited (Paper 2 §2.3)

| Label | Meaning |
|---|---|
| **Interface claim** | The routing is compatible at the interface level; no certificate earned at this paper's tier. |
| **Main-manuscript certificate** | The detailed closure lives in Paper 1; this paper invokes by interface only. |
| **Diagnostic / illustrative** | Included for physical intuition or low-energy sanity; not load-bearing. Cannot upgrade an interface claim. |
| **Outside this paper's scope** | Deferred to Paper 4 or another companion. |

### 3.2.2 UQF-specific (new to this paper)

| Label | Meaning |
|---|---|
| **Quantum object** | An entry in the §4 ledger: classical source, layer assignment, quantum entity, and required test all specified. |
| **Physical Hilbert space** | The positive-norm subspace surviving the gauge quotient (UQF-3). |
| **Positivity certificate** | Named, frozen argument that a candidate Hilbert subspace has nonnegative inner product on physical states — *plainly:* no state has negative probability. |
| **UV-completion certificate** | Named, frozen argument that the framework is well-defined at arbitrarily high energy (asymptotic safety, string embedding, or equivalent). |
| **Anomaly-closure certificate** | Named, frozen argument that all chiral / gauge / mixed anomalies cancel on physical states — *plainly:* the quantum symmetry-breaking that would make the theory inconsistent cancels out. |
| **BRST nilpotency certificate** | Named, frozen argument that the BRST operator $s$ satisfies $s^2 = 0$ and that physical states sit in $\ker(s)/\mathrm{im}(s)$ — *plainly:* the bookkeeping that strips the gauge-redundant states, leaving a clean self-consistent set. |
| **Confinement / mass-gap candidate** | A route to nonperturbative confinement and mass gap compatible with the active branch, with named partner-community work that would close it; **not** a Clay-Millennium-prize-closing proof. |
| **Strong-CP candidate** | A named structural mechanism for the $\bar\theta$ problem, with named falsification surface; **not** a solution. |
| **Precision-likelihood specification** | A Tier-1 specification of what numerical force-sector precision work is required, with named experiments and partner toolchains; **not** the numerical values themselves. |

### 3.2.3 Per-row tier ladder

Each UQF row carries one of the following per-row tiers at any frozen status:

| Tier | Meaning |
|---|---|
| **INTERFACE** | The gate is defined and consistent at the interface level (Paper 2 wording), but no certificate has been earned. |
| **AUDIT** | The gate has a draft argument and a named falsification surface, with at least one open dependency. |
| **CANDIDATE** | The gate has a frozen candidate construction with declared assumptions, named falsification surface, and named pass/fail criterion; certificate strength conditional on listed open items. |
| **CERTIFICATE** | The gate is closed at certificate strength under declared assumptions; frozen inputs locked, pass/fail criterion met, downgrade rule not triggered. |

The aggregate tier of the paper is the min over the 17 rows. The aggregate convention is the same min-rule used by the prior UQC backbone (the chain is no stronger than its weakest link, and that is what the certificate stack is *for*).

### 3.2.4 Tier ladder for the unified claim (from the source handoff)

- **Minimum viable** ("candidate unified quantum-force completion under declared assumptions"): BRST/BV model + physical-state definition + graviton/gauge/Higgs certificates + anomaly closure + truncated UV certificate + nonperturbative QCD route + strong-CP candidate + precision comparison.
- **Strong** ("certificate-complete unified quantum force theory under declared assumptions"): + positive physical Hilbert space + stable UV trajectory + quantum compactification stability + nonperturbative QCD certificate + strong-CP certificate + global force-sector likelihood + reproduction artifacts.
- **Full** ("complete unified quantum theory of all known forces"): everything above with very few "diagnostic only" rows.

---

## 3.3 The seventeen-row UQF stack

Each row below is one gate. It names its purpose, the certificate it requires, the frozen inputs it consumes, its pass/fail criterion, its downgrade rule, its current status label, and the Paper 2 C-FF rows it depends on. The rows are ordered UQF-0 (active-branch inheritance) through UQF-16 (map structure); the overall claim tier Σ is the minimum over all rows (the min-rule, §3.4), so the weakest row sets the headline and no strong row can mask a weak one.

### UQF-0 — Active-branch inheritance

- **Purpose.** Lock the same active branch $\mathfrak B_{\rm active} = M_{3,1} \times K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$ (with layer structure) used by Paper 1 and Paper 2.
- **Required certificate.** A statement that this paper's quantization uses identically the active branch of Paper 1; the layer separation of Paper 2 is preserved; no implicit branch substitution occurs anywhere in §§4 through 20.
- **Frozen inputs.** Paper 1 active-branch selection certificate; Paper 2 §4 active-branch restatement.
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: the §4 ledger and every certificate in §§8 through 18 reference the same branch object. Fail: any downstream section quantizes on a different background.
- **Downgrade.** Any UQF row that quantizes on a non-inherited background is removed from this paper's stack and the row's claim is withdrawn.
- **Status.** **CERTIFICATE** (this paper is held to the inheritance discipline by construction).
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF0, C-FF1, C-FF13.

### UQF-1 — Quantum object ledger

- **Purpose.** Identify every quantized object in the paper: metric modes, gauge connections, Higgs / Goldstones, chiral fermions, ghosts, antifields, KK modes.
- **Required certificate.** The §4 ledger, with every row specifying: classical source, layer ($\times$, $\oplus$, or $\otimes$), quantum object, required test, route-to-UQF-gate.
- **Frozen inputs.** Active branch (UQF-0); layer discipline (C-FF1).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: every object quantized in §§5 through 18 appears as a §4 ledger row. Fail: any object is quantized without a ledger entry (the object has no declared classical source, no declared layer, or no declared required test).
- **Downgrade.** Any ledger-orphan object is removed from the paper or downgraded to "diagnostic only."
- **Status.** **CANDIDATE** as drafted (§4 is the Phase-1 deliverable; closing it to CERTIFICATE depends on Phase 2 actually consuming every row).
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF1 (layer), C-FF6 (gauge-origin), C-FF7 (gravity/gauge separation).

### UQF-2 — Canonical / path-integral equivalence

- **Purpose.** Show that the canonical quantization formalism (operator-valued fields, equal-time commutators) and the path-integral / BV-BRST formalism (Faddeev-Popov ghosts, BV master equation) yield identical predictions where both are applied.
- **Required certificate.** A demonstration on the active branch's free-field sectors (graviton, gauge, Higgs, fermion) that canonical and path-integral two-point functions, $S$-matrix elements, and physical-state norms agree.
- **Frozen inputs.** UQF-0, UQF-1; regulator compatibility (C-FF9).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: agreement on free sectors with truncation error bound declared; on interacting sectors, agreement in perturbation theory with named scheme. Fail: any sector where the two formalisms disagree without an explanation routing the disagreement to a scheme choice.
- **Downgrade.** If agreement fails for an interacting sector, that sector's certificate (e.g. UQF-5 graviton, UQF-6 gauge boson) drops one tier.
- **Status.** **CANDIDATE** *(phase-close reconciliation, §3.8: the §5 framework build — three-formulation equivalence on the free/perturbative overlap, §5.5/§5.8 — discharges the Phase-2 target; CERTIFICATE on interacting sectors per declared scheme remains open).* Original Phase-1 entry: INTERFACE.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF9.

### UQF-3 — Physical Hilbert space

- **Purpose.** Define a positive-norm physical Hilbert space $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$ after the gauge quotient is taken.
- **Required certificate.** A positivity certificate: $\langle \psi | \psi \rangle \geq 0$ for all $|\psi\rangle \in \mathcal H_{\rm phys}$, with equality only for the zero vector; physical states defined as the BRST cohomology $\ker(s)/\mathrm{im}(s)$ on the BRST-extended Fock-like space.
- **Frozen inputs.** UQF-2 (canonical / path-integral equivalence); UQF-4 (BRST nilpotency).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: positivity holds on free-sector physical states and on perturbative-interaction states with declared truncation; pass on the nonperturbative confined-QCD sector is conditional on UQF-11. Fail: any negative-norm physical state remains in $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$.
- **Downgrade.** Negative-norm states surviving the quotient downgrade UQF-3 to INTERFACE and force a re-cohomology pass; if unfixable, UQF-5, UQF-6, UQF-7, UQF-8 each downgrade one tier.
- **Status.** **CANDIDATE** at Phase 2 close; CERTIFICATE conditional on Phase 4 anomaly/unitarity closure.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF5 (no double counting).

### UQF-4 — BRST/BV nilpotency and anomaly closure

- **Purpose.** Prove (under declared assumptions) that the BRST operator $s$ satisfies $s^2 = 0$ on the BRST-extended phase space and that all chiral, gauge, and mixed anomalies cancel on the physical states.
- **Required certificate.** A BRST nilpotency certificate and an anomaly-closure certificate. The anomaly-closure piece inherits the Paper 1 anomaly ledger (one full generation of left-handed Weyl fermions, hypercharge assignments, color/weak ledger) and verifies that the inherited cancellation survives the descent to 4D and the choice of regulator.
- **Frozen inputs.** UQF-0, UQF-1; Paper 1 anomaly ledger (C-FF10); regulator scheme (C-FF9).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: $s^2 = 0$ verified order by order on the BV action; all anomaly polynomials cancel on $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$. Fail: any uncancelled anomaly remains, or BRST fails to be nilpotent at one-loop or beyond.
- **Downgrade.** Uncancelled anomaly: UQF-7 (fermion quantization) and UQF-6 (gauge-boson certificate) each downgrade one tier; UQF-3 (physical Hilbert space) loses CERTIFICATE; the paper as a whole cannot exceed AUDIT until resolved.
- **Status.** **AUDIT** (Paper 1 anomaly ledger is closed; lifting it under the 4D-descent + BRST quantization here requires explicit verification, deferred to Phase 4).
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF10 (anomaly), C-FF9 (regulator), C-FF5 (no double counting).

### UQF-5 — Graviton certificate

- **Purpose.** Extract a physical, positive-norm, massless spin-2 graviton mode from the linearized metric block $G_{\mu\nu}$, with the correct gravitational coupling to stress-energy.
- **Required certificate.** Linearized graviton extraction with BRST gauge fixing (e.g., harmonic / de Donder gauge), two physical polarizations, correct dispersion relation, Newtonian limit at low energy. Higher-curvature corrections enumerated; UV-completion route named (UQF-9).
- **Frozen inputs.** Active-branch metric block (UQF-0); BRST nilpotency (UQF-4); Hilbert positivity (UQF-3).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: linearized graviton with positive norm, correct polarization count, Newtonian limit recovered. Fail: ghost graviton mode survives, polarization count wrong, or low-energy gravitational coupling absent.
- **Downgrade.** Failure here means the gravity sector of the paper drops to "interface only inherited from Paper 2 §6"; the unified-quantum-force-completion claim cannot include gravity in that case.
- **Status.** **CANDIDATE** (linearized analysis is straightforward; CERTIFICATE conditional on UQF-9 UV-completion).
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF7 (gravity/gauge separation), C-FF6 (gauge-origin discipline).

### UQF-6 — Gauge-boson certificate

- **Purpose.** Extract physical gauge-boson modes — gluons, $W^\pm$, $Z^0$, photon — with correct polarization counts, correct masses (zero for gluons and photon; EWSB-determined for $W^\pm$, $Z^0$), and BRST-positive physical states.
- **Required certificate.** Per-sector extraction: gluons (eight massless, two transverse polarizations each, $SU(3)_c$ color algebra); $W^\pm$, $Z^0$ (massive, three polarizations including longitudinal-from-Goldstone, EWSB-determined masses); photon (massless, two transverse polarizations, $U(1)_{\rm em}$ post-EWSB).
- **Frozen inputs.** Paper 2 projection maps $\pi_{\rm strong}, \pi_{\rm weak}, \pi_{\rm QED}$; BRST (UQF-4); Higgs/Goldstone (UQF-8); Hilbert positivity (UQF-3).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: each gauge boson appears with correct polarization count, correct mass, correct algebra. Fail: any wrong-polarization, wrong-mass, or BRST-non-positive gauge state.
- **Downgrade.** Per-sector. Failure on gluons drops the strong-sector certificate; failure on $W^\pm/Z^0$ drops the weak-sector certificate; failure on photon drops the QED-sector certificate.
- **Status.** **CANDIDATE** for gluons / $W^\pm/Z^0$ / photon at perturbative level; CERTIFICATE conditional on UQF-8 (Higgs) for the massive electroweak gauge bosons, and on UQF-11 (nonperturbative QCD) for the full QCD picture.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF3 (shared matter), C-FF4 (charge normalization), C-FF6 (gauge-origin), C-FF8 (QED downstream).

### UQF-7 — Fermion quantization

- **Purpose.** Quantize one full generation of left-handed Weyl fermions on the active branch without mirror partners, without wrong-statistics states, and without anomaly leaks.
- **Required certificate.** A canonical and path-integral quantization of $\mathcal E_{\rm matter}$ giving Weyl fermions in the inherited representations ($Q_L \sim (\mathbf 3, \mathbf 2, +\tfrac 1 6)$, $u_R^c \sim (\bar{\mathbf 3}, \mathbf 1, -\tfrac 2 3)$, $d_R^c \sim (\bar{\mathbf 3}, \mathbf 1, +\tfrac 1 3)$, $L \sim (\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2, -\tfrac 1 2)$, $e_R^c \sim (\mathbf 1, \mathbf 1, +1)$ with $Q = T_3 + Y$), with explicit absence of mirror partners arising from the compactification, with spin-statistics theorem satisfied, and with the anomaly closure of UQF-4 surviving the quantization.
- **Frozen inputs.** Paper 1 matter bundle (C-FF3); anomaly ledger (UQF-4); active branch (UQF-0).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: one chiral generation, no mirrors, anomaly-closed, spin-statistics satisfied. Fail: surviving mirror pair, wrong-statistics fermion, or anomaly leak.
- **Downgrade.** Surviving mirror → row drops to INTERFACE and §11 of the paper retracts the chiral-quantization claim, downgrading the unified-completion claim to "non-chiral candidate."
- **Status.** **AUDIT** (Paper 1 anomaly ledger is closed; demonstrating that the 4D-descent from the active branch preserves chirality at the quantum level — i.e., no light mirror partners arise from KK or quotient subtleties — requires explicit verification, deferred to Phase 3). *Open-item narrowing (corpus reconciliation, 2026-06-12, see §11 Corpus Reconciliation):* the **classical** chiral inventory this row inherits — the three-family count and the no-mirror-at-zero-mode structure — is a *load-bearing closed* result in the corpus (TOE_FINAL v6 closed-core/stabilization entries: the APS index **(+3, 0)** zero-mode inventory, "the three families are the spin-structure witness", twice-derived against the BWB scan with $|\mathrm{index}|=3$; EXTERNAL). The index count is therefore **not** UQF-7's open item. The residual open obligation that keeps this row at AUDIT is narrowed to the **quantum-descent** question only: that the 4D BV-BRST quantization of the descent introduces no light mirror from KK / quotient / loop subtleties beyond the classical zero-mode count. Tier preserved at AUDIT; no promotion.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF3 (shared matter), C-FF5 (no double counting), C-FF10 (anomaly).

### UQF-8 — Higgs / Goldstone quantum certificate

- **Purpose.** Separate the physical Higgs boson from the three eaten Goldstones; protect the EW vacuum at tree level (with higher-order vacuum stability invoked by main-manuscript-certificate authority).
- **Required certificate.** Higgs doublet $H$ decomposed post-EWSB into one physical real scalar $h$ plus three Goldstones $\pi^\pm, \pi^0$ absorbed as longitudinal $W^\pm, Z^0$; gauge-eaten Goldstones removed from physical Hilbert space by BRST; vacuum stability at tree level explicit; higher-order vacuum stability invoked by reference to Paper 1 Appendix-H authority.
- **Frozen inputs.** Paper 2 weak/QED interface; BRST (UQF-4); gauge-boson certificate (UQF-6 conditional).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: physical Higgs separated, Goldstones eaten, $W^\pm/Z^0$ get correct longitudinal modes, vacuum stable at declared order. Fail: ghost Higgs, surviving physical Goldstone, or vacuum instability.
- **Downgrade.** Surviving physical Goldstone → UQF-6 weak-sector certificate drops; vacuum instability at higher order → UQF-8 drops to AUDIT pending main-manuscript Appendix-H authority.
- **Status.** **CANDIDATE** at tree level; AUDIT at higher order pending Paper 1 Appendix-H invocation.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF8 (QED downstream of EW), C-FF10 (anomaly).

### UQF-9 — UV-completion certificate

- **Purpose.** Prove or certify (under declared assumptions) controlled high-energy behavior of the unified quantum theory.
- **Required certificate.** A named UV-completion route with a frozen truncation. The corpus default candidate is asymptotic safety: a non-Gaussian UV fixed point of the renormalization-group flow for the unified action, with finitely many relevant directions. The fixed point is exhibited at declared truncation (e.g., FRG with the matter content of Paper 1's anomaly ledger and the geometric structure of the active branch). Alternative UV routes (string-theoretic embedding, finite N=4-like structures) may be invoked but only with the same certificate discipline.
- **Frozen inputs.** Truncation specification (named, with cutoff scheme); matter content (UQF-7); anomaly closure (UQF-4); regulator compatibility (C-FF9).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: fixed point exhibited at declared truncation with finitely many relevant directions; truncation-error estimate declared; flow back to observed low-energy force physics demonstrated. Fail: no fixed point at the declared truncation, or infinitely many relevant directions.
- **Downgrade.** No fixed point → UQF-9 drops to AUDIT, UQF-5 (graviton) and UQF-6 (gauge) lose CERTIFICATE tier (because the perturbative force-carrier certificates need a UV completion to be sustainable above the cutoff); UV completion remains as named open problem rather than as solved.
- **Status.** **AUDIT** (asymptotic-safety non-Gaussian fixed point existence is a global open problem, not a corpus-internal one; the present paper at most extends or restates the prior UQC-1 audit and does **not** claim closure). *Corpus guard (Λ line; §11, 2026-06-12):* the corpus has since closed the **vacuum-energy / cosmological-constant** reading of high-energy structure as an honest fail — TOE_FINAL **v12** the exact-weight graded supertrace shows no structural cancellation at any coefficient order; **v14** the chamber-cancellation route is **THEOREM_REFUTED** (Λ operator = unit operator); **Λ stays Weinberg-open as a computed one-loop certificate** (EXTERNAL). This does **not** supply the UV fixed point (UQF-9 stays correctly AUDIT — see the checked-and-correctly-open list, §11.3), but it is a binding guard: nothing in §14's UV-route narrative may be read as implying a live Λ / vacuum-energy cancellation mechanism. No promotion.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF12 (scope-boundary), C-FF13 (main-manuscript authority).

### UQF-10 — Quantum compactification stability

- **Purpose.** Show that the compact factors $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$ remain stable under quantum corrections; no Casimir-driven runaway, no moduli destabilization, no light unobserved scalar modes from compactification.
- **Required certificate.** Effective potential for the compactification moduli computed at declared loop order; no unstable directions; light-moduli mass bounds (e.g., absence of fifth-force-mediating moduli below current direct-test bounds) verified; Casimir contributions accounted for.
- **Frozen inputs.** UV completion (UQF-9); active-branch geometry (UQF-0); ledger row for $G_{AB}$ moduli (UQF-1, §4).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: declared-order effective potential has a stable minimum at the inherited compactification volumes; no light-modulus violations of fifth-force / equivalence-principle bounds. Fail: tachyonic moduli, or light scalar violating direct-test bounds.
- **Downgrade.** Tachyonic moduli → UQF-10 drops to AUDIT, UQF-5 (graviton) drops one tier (because the active-branch background is no longer a self-consistent solution at the quantum level), and §15 of the paper records the open problem.
- **Status.** **AUDIT** (depends on UQF-9; without a UV-completion certificate the moduli effective potential at higher loops is not controllable). *Corpus reconciliation (2026-06-12, see §11):* the compactification-stability **existence** question was independently discharged at **decision grade** by the corpus's native stabilization object — TOE_FINAL v8 `H04_DISCHARGED_AT_DECISION_GRADE`, v9 Gap 04 **CLOSED at decision grade** (package `gap04_frozen_package_native.json`), v10 boundary-sign event ($c_{bdry}=-1.08\times10^{-2}$) ⟹ well exists **unconditionally** in $c_{loop}$ (all EXTERNAL). That route is **not** the §14 FRG-6 route this row's S-2/S-7 are conditioned on, so the corpus result is inherited as a decision-grade *input* (the background is stable) but is **not** converted into this paper's own certificate-grade FRG result; this row's tier is therefore preserved at AUDIT pending its own §14-FRG verification. No promotion.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF1 (layer), C-FF7 (gravity/gauge separation).

### UQF-11 — Nonperturbative QCD

- **Purpose.** Provide a route to nonperturbative QCD compatible with the $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ structure: confinement, mass gap, hadronic spectrum, lattice-continuum bridge, chiral condensate.
- **Required certificate.** A *route* statement, not a closure. (a) Confinement: Wilson-loop area law compatibility with the inherited $SU(3)_c$ algebra; named lattice-QCD comparison program. (b) Mass gap: candidate mass-gap value $\Delta > 0$ inherited from lattice-QCD partner work; not derived in this paper. (c) Hadronic spectrum: inherited from partner-community lattice work. (d) Chiral condensate: candidate origin in the inherited chiral structure; not closed here. The Yang-Mills mass-gap Clay Millennium problem is explicitly **not** claimed to be solved.
- **Frozen inputs.** Paper 2 §7 strong interface; UV completion (UQF-9 for high-energy controllability); gauge-boson certificate (UQF-6 for gluons).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: each of the four sub-rows has a named lattice / partner-community work program with a stated falsifier. Fail: any sub-row that asserts closure without partner work or without a falsifier.
- **Downgrade.** Any sub-row asserting unfounded closure drops UQF-11 to AUDIT and forces a §12 retraction.
- **Status.** **AUDIT + ROADMAP** (per UQC-3 inheritance; framework supplies UV completion only with IR inheritance from partner-community work).
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF9 (regulator), C-FF11 (sanity target).

### UQF-12 — Strong CP

- **Purpose.** Explain or eliminate $\bar\theta$.
- **Required certificate.** A named candidate structural mechanism with a named falsifier. The corpus default candidate is the $S^1_Y / \mathbb Z_2$ boundary-parity mechanism; the named fallback is a Peccei-Quinn axion (which requires additional geometric structure not present in the active branch as-inherited and is therefore a *fallback* not a *primary*). The 1.64-rad spin-c-holonomy contribution to $\bar\theta$ from Article B §5.4 is preserved honestly and is the falsification surface.
- **Frozen inputs.** Active branch $S^1_Y$ boundary structure (UQF-0); Paper 1 strong-CP scope-out at Gate 11 (C-FF12 inherited).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: candidate mechanism named with explicit falsifier (nEDM bound, neutron-EDM next-generation experiments named). Fail: candidate mechanism not named, or named without falsifier.
- **Downgrade.** If the boundary-parity candidate fails the nEDM bound by more than declared margin → UQF-12 drops to AUDIT, falls back to PQ-axion candidate (which itself requires additional geometric structure beyond the active branch and so the fallback drops to AUDIT-with-extension-required).
- **Status.** **AUDIT (LOW confidence)** per UQC-4 inheritance; strong CP remains *Excluded from scope* of Paper 1 per Gate 11 of the geometry SoT; this paper provides a candidate and a falsifier, not a solution.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF12 (scope-boundary), C-FF13 (main-manuscript authority), C-FF14 (falsification path).

### UQF-13 — Precision-force phenomenology

- **Purpose.** Provide a global force-sector likelihood specification against observed precision data (EWPO, CKM/PMNS structure, proton-lifetime structure, KK-threshold structure).
- **Required certificate.** Two-tier per UQC-8 inheritance. **Tier-1** (specification): per observable, name the required calculation, the constraint experiment, and the partner toolchain (HEPfit, CKMfitter, NuFIT, flavio, RBC-UKQCD, etc.). **Tier-2** (values): explicitly deferred to partner-community execution; this paper produces **no numerical predictions**.
- **Frozen inputs.** Paper 2 §11 sanity targets; UQF-7 (fermion quantization for flavor structure); regulator compatibility (C-FF9).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass (Tier-1): every observable in the force-sector precision set has a named calculation, named experiment, named partner. Pass (Tier-2): not in this paper. Fail (Tier-1): any observable missing one of the three named pieces.
- **Downgrade.** Tier-1 incompleteness → UQF-13 drops to AUDIT; the precision-likelihood claim becomes "Tier-1 partial specification."
- **Status.** **CANDIDATE (Tier-1)** with **AUDIT (Tier-2)** per UQC-8 inheritance.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF4 (charge), C-FF9 (regulator), C-FF10 (anomaly), C-FF11 (sanity target).

### UQF-14 — Unitarity / causality / locality audit

- **Purpose.** Audit the unified quantum-force theory for negative probabilities, superluminal signaling, and nonlocal failures.
- **Required certificate.** Per-sector unitarity bound check (e.g., partial-wave unitarity on $WW \to WW$, gluon-gluon scattering, graviton-graviton scattering at perturbative scale); causality check via Lorentz-covariance and spectral conditions on physical states; locality check via cluster decomposition on $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$.
- **Frozen inputs.** UQF-3 (physical Hilbert space); UQF-4 (BRST); UQF-9 (UV completion for high-energy unitarity).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: per-sector unitarity within declared cutoff; Lorentz covariance respected; cluster decomposition holds on $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$. Fail: any negative probability, any superluminal signal, any cluster-decomposition violation.
- **Downgrade.** Per-sector. Unitarity violation in the graviton sector at scale $\Lambda_\star < M_{\rm Planck}$ → UQF-5 graviton certificate drops one tier; gauge-sector unitarity violation → corresponding UQF-6 sub-row drops.
- **Status.** **AUDIT** (per-sector bounds are routine where the sector is perturbative; the graviton sector's unitarity above the cutoff is conditional on UQF-9). *Corpus guard (§11):* because this row's high-energy unitarity inherits from UQF-9, the same Λ-line guard applies — the corpus's vacuum-energy verdict (TOE_FINAL v12 supertrace FAIL, v14 chamber route THEOREM_REFUTED; Λ Weinberg-open as a computed certificate, EXTERNAL) means no high-energy-completion reading here implies a Λ / vacuum-energy cancellation. Tier preserved at AUDIT.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF5 (no double counting).

### UQF-15 — No-hidden-sector force leakage

- **Purpose.** Verify that no unobserved fifth-force, hidden vector, or hidden scalar mode survives the quantization incorrectly.
- **Required certificate.** Enumeration of all $\otimes$-layer fields not used by the four force EFTs; declaration of each as either (a) eaten by EWSB and not physical, (b) confined inside QCD and not directly observed, (c) bounded below current direct-test limits, or (d) outside this paper's scope (i.e., a Paper-4-reserve hidden-sector candidate, in which case it is declared and deferred but not silently retained).
- **Frozen inputs.** UQF-1 ledger (§4); UQF-7 (fermion); UQF-8 (Higgs/Goldstone); UQF-10 (compactification stability).
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: every non-force-EFT $\otimes$-layer field accounted for. Fail: any silent residual field in $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$ that would mediate an unobserved force.
- **Downgrade.** Silent residual → UQF-15 drops to AUDIT, the residual is enumerated explicitly in §18, and the unified-completion claim is conditioned on the residual being below current direct-test bounds.
- **Status.** **AUDIT** (depends on the §4 ledger being exhaustive and on Phase 4 audit closure).
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF5 (no double counting), C-FF8 (QED downstream of EW).

### UQF-16 — Final downgrade map

- **Purpose.** Make the per-gate downgrade ladder explicit and exhaustive. Every failed certificate has a named consequence; no failure is silent.
- **Required certificate.** The downgrade map of §19 of the paper, listing for each of UQF-0..UQF-15 the per-row downgrade rule (already stated in each row above) plus the aggregate-tier rule (min over rows).
- **Frozen inputs.** All of UQF-0..UQF-15.
- **Pass/fail.** Pass: every UQF row has a downgrade rule in §19 matching the row's per-gate statement here. Fail: any UQF row lacks a §19 downgrade entry, or §19 contradicts the per-row downgrade.
- **Downgrade.** Self-applying: if UQF-16 fails (i.e., the downgrade map is incomplete), the paper drops to AUDIT in aggregate.
- **Status.** **CANDIDATE** at draft; CERTIFICATE conditional on §19 being written to the rule of this row.
- **C-FF rows consumed.** C-FF14 (falsification path).

---

## 3.4 Per-gate downgrade ladder

The downgrade ladder is the rule that turns a failed certificate into an honest paper-level status statement rather than into a silent retraction. The ladder has three layers.

### 3.4.1 Per-row layer (already stated in §3.3 row by row)

Each UQF row's "Downgrade" entry above is the per-row layer. Read row by row.

### 3.4.2 Cross-row coupling layer

Some failures propagate. The coupling rules are:

| If this gate fails | Then these gates downgrade |
|---|---|
| UQF-4 (BRST nilpotency / anomaly closure) | UQF-3, UQF-5, UQF-6, UQF-7, UQF-8 each drop one tier |
| UQF-9 (UV completion) | UQF-5, UQF-6, UQF-10, UQF-14 each lose CERTIFICATE |
| UQF-3 (physical Hilbert space, positivity) | UQF-5, UQF-6, UQF-7, UQF-8, UQF-14 each lose CERTIFICATE |
| UQF-10 (compactification stability) | UQF-5 drops one tier; UQF-15 forced to AUDIT |
| UQF-11 (nonperturbative QCD) | UQF-6 (gluon sub-row) drops one tier; UQF-13 (precision, QCD observables) drops one tier |
| UQF-7 (fermion quantization) | UQF-4 anomaly piece drops one tier; UQF-13 (flavor observables) drops one tier |
| Any C-FF row from Paper 2 | Per Paper 2's downgrade map; this paper additionally drops the dependent UQF row(s) one tier |

### 3.4.3 Aggregate layer (min-rule)

The aggregate tier of the paper is

$$
\Sigma \;=\; \min_{k \in \{0, 1, \ldots, 16\}} \;\sigma_k
$$

where $\sigma_k$ is the per-row tier of UQF-$k$ from the ladder of §3.2.3 (INTERFACE < AUDIT < CANDIDATE < CERTIFICATE). The aggregate tier is honest by min-rule: the chain is no stronger than its weakest link.

At the Phase-1 close represented by this document, the aggregate tier is **AUDIT** (UQF-4, UQF-7, UQF-9, UQF-10, UQF-11, UQF-12, UQF-14, UQF-15 are AUDIT; UQF-2 is CANDIDATE after the §3.8 reconciliation — its stale Phase-1 INTERFACE entry would have forced Σ = INTERFACE; the rest are CANDIDATE or CERTIFICATE). The aggregate target after Phase 7 is **CANDIDATE** (minimum-viable claim language: "candidate unified quantum-force completion under declared assumptions"). The aggregate target after partner-community execution is **CERTIFICATE** (strong claim language: "certificate-complete unified quantum force theory under declared assumptions").

### 3.4.4 Honest-status rule

The aggregate-tier statement of the paper, wherever it appears (abstract, introduction, conclusion, reviewer-first-read), must match $\Sigma$ computed by the rule above. Any sentence in the paper that asserts a stronger aggregate tier than $\Sigma$ is a drafting bug. The bug-report routing is to §3.4.3.

---

| UQF-7 | Fermion quantization | AUDIT | §11 | U04, U08 | C-FF3, C-FF5, C-FF10 | Row 5 (primary) |
| UQF-8 | Higgs / Goldstone quantum certificate | CANDIDATE | §10 | U03 | C-FF8, C-FF10 | Row 6 (primary); Row 4 (longitudinal $W^\pm/Z^0$) |
| UQF-9 | UV-completion certificate | AUDIT | §14 | U08 | C-FF12, C-FF13 | Row 1 (graviton UV); Rows 4, 5, 6 (force-sector UV) |
| UQF-10 | Quantum compactification stability | AUDIT | §15 | U04 | C-FF1, C-FF7 | Row 3 (primary); Row 7 (KK tower) |
| UQF-11 | Nonperturbative QCD | AUDIT | §12 | U08 | C-FF9, C-FF11 | Row 4 (gluon sub-row primary); Row 5 (quark fermions) |
| UQF-12 | Strong CP | AUDIT | §13 | U08 | C-FF12, C-FF13, C-FF14 | Row 4 (gauge $\bar\theta$ angle); Row 5 (CKM phase contribution) |
| UQF-13 | Precision-force phenomenology | CANDIDATE | §16 | U08 | C-FF4, C-FF9, C-FF10, C-FF11 | Rows 4, 5, 6, 7 (every observable sector) |
| UQF-14 | Unitarity / causality / locality audit | AUDIT | §17 | U08 | C-FF5 | Rows 1, 4 (high-energy scattering); Row 8 (ghost-loop cancellation in optical theorem) |
| UQF-15 | No-hidden-sector force leakage | AUDIT | §18 | U04 | C-FF5, C-FF8 | Rows 3, 7 (silent residual moduli or KK modes); Rows 4, 5, 6 (declared residuals) |
| UQF-16 | Final downgrade map | CANDIDATE | §19 | U06, U01 | C-FF14 | all (downgrade map covers every row) |

## 3.6 Bottom line for §3

- 17 UQF rows, force-sector-only.
- Each row has purpose, certificate, frozen inputs, pass/fail, downgrade rule, status, and C-FF consumption explicitly stated.
- The aggregate-tier rule is min over rows.
- Failures propagate per §3.4.2 and are accounted for honestly by §3.4.4.
- The cosmology / dark / baryogenesis rows from the prior UQC stack are explicitly removed and moved to Paper 4 reserve.

The next section (§4) instantiates UQF-1 by drafting the quantum object ledger. Every object the paper quantizes anywhere downstream of §4 must appear there.

# UQFC-4 — Quantum Object Ledger
* · gate UQF-1 · drafted 2026-06-08*

> **Gate card — UQF-1: Quantum object ledger** *(auto-derived from §3.3 / §4.4, the single source of truth per §3.0; any discrepancy with this chapter is a drafting bug)*
>
> | Field | Value |
> |---|---|
> | Tier | **CANDIDATE** as drafted (§4 is the Phase-1 deliverable; closing it to CERTIFICATE depends on Phase 2 actually consuming every row). |
> | Required certificate | The §4 ledger, with every row specifying: classical source, layer ($\times$, $\oplus$, or $\otimes$), quantum object, required test, route-to-UQF-gate. |
> | Frozen inputs | Active branch (UQF-0); layer discipline (C-FF1). |
> | Pass / fail | Pass: every object quantized in §§5 through 18 appears as a §4 ledger row. Fail: any object is quantized without a ledger entry (the object has no declared classical source, no declared layer, or no declared required test). |
> | Downgrade | Any ledger-orphan object is removed from the paper or downgraded to "diagnostic only." |
> | C-FF rows consumed | C-FF1 (layer), C-FF6 (gauge-origin), C-FF7 (gravity/gauge separation). |
> | Ledger rows consumed (§4.4) | all (this section *is* UQF-1) |

## 4.0 Purpose and reading rule

This section is the load-bearing deliverable of Phase 1. **Every quantum object that the paper quantizes anywhere in §§5 through 18 must trace back to a row of the ledger below.** If a downstream section quantizes an object that has no row here, the object is either (a) not actually being quantized (and the sentence should be reframed), (b) absorbed into an existing row (and the existing row should be updated), or (c) a missing row (and this ledger should be amended). What the rule prohibits is silent introduction of a quantum object without ledger registration.

Conversely, every row here promises that the paper will consume it. A ledger row whose paper consumption is missing at the end of Phase 7 is itself a drafting bug; the row should either be removed (and the absence rationalized in §18 "No-Hidden-Force Leakage") or the missing consumption should be added.

The reading rule for this section is therefore symmetric: read this ledger before reading any quantization section in the paper; read the ledger again after reading any quantization section to confirm that every object used there appears here.

## 4.1 Ledger column definitions

Each ledger row carries the following columns:

- **Object.** The symbolic name of the classical entity from the active branch.
- **Layer.** The Paper-1 / Paper-2 layer assignment: $\times$ (base geometry), $\oplus$ (finite rule constraints), or $\otimes$ (field / operator bundle).
- **Classical source.** The piece of the active branch $\mathfrak B_{\rm active} = M_{3,1} \times K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$ (with layer overlays) that the object lives on, and the projection map (from Paper 2 §5) under which it descends.
- **Quantum object.** The named quantum entity the paper attempts to construct: graviton mode, gauge-boson mode, fermion field, ghost field, antifield, etc.
- **Required test.** The named test the quantum object must pass for its UQF row to close at CERTIFICATE: positive norm, anomaly closure, correct polarization count, no surviving mirror, etc.
- **Route-to-UQF-gate.** The UQF row(s) from §3 that consume this ledger row.
- **Status at Phase-1 close.** Per-row tier following §3.2.3.
- **Failure-mode summary.** One-line statement of what failure of the required test would mean.

A row is *load-bearing* if its failure would force any UQF row to drop tier. All rows in §4.2 are load-bearing.

## 4.2 The ledger

The ledger contains **nine** quantum-object rows. Seven correspond to the handoff §3 template (G_MN, G_μA, G_AB, A_μ^a, Ψ, H, ghosts); two additional rows (antifields, KK modes) are added because they appear in the BV-BRST formalism and the compactification stability sections, respectively, and would otherwise be silently quantized.

### Row 1 — Metric block $G_{\mu\nu}$ (graviton sector)

- **Object.** $G_{\mu\nu}$, the 4D spacetime-facing block of the 13D metric.
- **Layer.** $\times$ (base geometry).
- **Classical source.** Restriction of the 13D metric $G_{MN}$ to $M_{3,1}$ via the gravity projection $\pi_{\rm grav}$ (Paper 2 §6). Layer assignment per C-FF7 (gravity/gauge separation) keeps this block strictly $\times$.
- **Quantum object.** Linearized graviton field $h_{\mu\nu}$ defined by $G_{\mu\nu} = \eta_{\mu\nu} + \kappa\, h_{\mu\nu}$ at the linearized level on a flat-background expansion; in BV-BRST, $h_{\mu\nu}$ is paired with the diffeomorphism ghost $c^\mu$ (Row 8) and antifield $h^{*\mu\nu}$ (Row 9). Physical massless spin-2 graviton mode with two transverse-traceless polarizations after BRST gauge fixing.
- **Required test.** Positive-norm spin-2 sector with two physical polarizations; Newtonian limit at low energy; correct coupling to the canonical stress-energy tensor of the matter row (Row 5).
- **Route-to-UQF-gate.** UQF-5 (graviton certificate, primary); UQF-3 (physical Hilbert space, positivity for the graviton sector); UQF-9 (UV completion, for behavior above the cutoff); UQF-14 (unitarity, partial-wave bounds on graviton scattering).
- **Status at Phase-1 close.** **CANDIDATE** (linearized analysis is straightforward; CERTIFICATE conditional on UQF-9 closing).
- **Failure-mode summary.** Surviving negative-norm graviton mode (ghost graviton), wrong polarization count, or absence of Newtonian limit forces UQF-5 to INTERFACE and removes the gravity sector from the unified-completion claim.

### Row 2 — Mixed metric block $G_{\mu A}$ (descended gauge precursor)

- **Object.** $G_{\mu A}$, the mixed 4D-internal block of the 13D metric (where $A$ runs over internal coordinates of $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$).
- **Layer.** $\times$ classically, descending to $\otimes$ as a 4D gauge connection actor per Paper 2 C-FF6 (gauge-origin discipline).
- **Classical source.** Mixed metric block of $G_{MN}$ on the active branch; descends under Kaluza-Klein-type expansion in the internal directions to a tower whose zero mode lives on $\mathcal E_{\rm gauge}$.
- **Quantum object.** Zero-mode 4D gauge connections $A_\mu^a$ for the descended Lie algebras: $\mathfrak{su}(3)_c$ from $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ (strong sector), $\mathfrak{su}(2)_L$ from $S^2$ spin-cover structure (weak sector left-handed piece), $\mathfrak{u}(1)_Y$ from $S^1_Y$ (hypercharge), with $U(1)_{\rm em}$ emerging post-EWSB per C-FF8. KK tower above the zero mode (Row 9) is bounded by main-manuscript-certificate authority.
- **Required test.** Correct gauge algebra ($SU(3)_c$, $SU(2)_L$, $U(1)_Y$) at the zero mode; descended-actor discipline (gauge fields are not primitive 13D bosons, per C-FF6); no double counting with Row 3 or Row 4 (per C-FF5); correct polarization count for the resulting 4D gauge bosons (Row 4 sub-rows).
- **Route-to-UQF-gate.** UQF-6 (gauge-boson certificate, primary); UQF-1 (ledger discipline — this row is the load-bearing layer-discipline row that prevents conflation of gravity with gauge); UQF-10 (compactification stability, for KK-mode bounds).
- **Status at Phase-1 close.** **CANDIDATE** (the descent is defined by Paper 2; the *quantum* descent — i.e., that zero modes survive at the quantum level with correct algebra — depends on UQF-10).
- **Failure-mode summary.** Wrong gauge algebra at the zero mode (e.g., extra $U(1)$ surviving from $K_6$ or wrong $SU(2)_L$ representation) drops UQF-6 to INTERFACE for the affected sector.

### Row 3 — Compact internal metric block $G_{AB}$ (moduli sector)

- **Object.** $G_{AB}$, the internal-internal block of the 13D metric on $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$.
- **Layer.** $\times$.
- **Classical source.** Internal metric on the compact factors of the active branch. Carries the compactification volumes (radion-like moduli) and any internal-shape moduli compatible with the active branch's $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ quotient.
- **Quantum object.** Moduli scalars (radion-type and shape-type) plus the KK tower (Row 9) of the compact factors. At the zero mode, each modulus is a 4D scalar that classically corresponds to a deformation of the compactification.
- **Required test.** No light moduli below current direct-test (fifth-force, equivalence-principle) bounds; declared-order effective potential with stable minimum at the inherited compactification volumes; no tachyonic directions.
- **Route-to-UQF-gate.** UQF-10 (compactification stability, primary); UQF-15 (no-hidden-force leakage, secondary — light moduli would mediate a fifth force); UQF-5 (graviton, secondary — instability of the moduli would destabilize the gravitational background).
- **Status at Phase-1 close.** **AUDIT** (depends on UQF-9 UV-completion; without UV control the moduli effective potential at higher loops is not controllable).
- **Failure-mode summary.** Tachyonic moduli direction means the active branch is not a stable vacuum at the quantum level, forcing UQF-10 to AUDIT and removing the compactification-stability claim from the paper.

### Row 4 — Descended 4D gauge connections $A_\mu^a$

- **Object.** $A_\mu^a$, the 4D gauge connections at the zero mode, for each descended Lie algebra $a$.
- **Layer.** $\otimes$ (field / operator bundle). Per C-FF6, these are descended actors, not primitive 13D fields.
- **Classical source.** Zero mode of Row 2's KK-expanded mixed metric block, organized by the descended gauge algebras: $A_\mu^a$ for $a = 1,\ldots,8$ (gluons, $SU(3)_c$); $A_\mu^I$ for $I = 1,2,3$ ($SU(2)_L$); $B_\mu$ ($U(1)_Y$); post-EWSB, the latter two mix into $W^\pm, Z^0, A_\mu^{\rm em}$.
- **Quantum object.** Per sub-sector:
  - **Gluons.** Eight massless gauge bosons $g_\mu^a$, two transverse polarizations each, color algebra $\mathfrak{su}(3)_c$.
  - **$W^\pm, Z^0$.** Three massive electroweak gauge bosons, three polarizations each (two transverse + one longitudinal from eaten Goldstone per Row 6), EWSB-determined masses.
  - **Photon.** One massless gauge boson $\gamma$, two transverse polarizations, $U(1)_{\rm em}$ post-EWSB.
- **Required test.** Per sub-sector: correct polarization count; correct mass; BRST-positive physical states; descended-actor discipline preserved (per C-FF6); shared charge convention $Q = T_3 + Y$ (per C-FF4) on matter coupling.
- **Route-to-UQF-gate.** UQF-6 (gauge-boson certificate, primary, per sub-sector); UQF-8 (Higgs / Goldstone, for $W^\pm/Z^0$ longitudinals); UQF-11 (nonperturbative QCD, for gluons in the IR); UQF-14 (unitarity, $WW$ scattering).
- **Status at Phase-1 close.** **CANDIDATE** per sub-sector at perturbative level; CERTIFICATE conditional on UQF-8 (for $W^\pm/Z^0$) and UQF-11 (for full QCD picture of gluons).
- **Failure-mode summary.** Wrong polarization count → corresponding UQF-6 sub-row drops. Surviving longitudinal photon would mean photon mass and is a hard fail. Surviving transverse $W^\pm/Z^0$ as massless would mean EWSB failure.

### Row 5 — Matter bundle $\Psi$ (chiral fermions)

- **Object.** $\Psi \in \mathcal E_{\rm matter}$, the inherited matter bundle of one full generation of left-handed Weyl fermions.
- **Layer.** $\otimes$.
- **Classical source.** Matter bundle from Paper 1, restricted to the active branch and carried through the four projection maps. Fermion content per Paper 1: $Q_L \sim (\mathbf 3, \mathbf 2, +\tfrac 1 6)$, $u_R^c \sim (\bar{\mathbf 3}, \mathbf 1, -\tfrac 2 3)$, $d_R^c \sim (\bar{\mathbf 3}, \mathbf 1, +\tfrac 1 3)$, $L \sim (\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2, -\tfrac 1 2)$, $e_R^c \sim (\mathbf 1, \mathbf 1, +1)$ in $Q = T_3 + Y$ normalization (per C-FF4). One generation is load-bearing; additional generations are inherited as a flavor structure from Paper 1 (Row 5 covers one representative generation; the flavor structure is consumed by UQF-13).
- **Quantum object.** Quantized chiral Weyl fermion fields $\psi_L^{(i)}$ for each representation $i$, with fermionic (Grassmann) statistics and Dirac/Weyl spinor structure. In path-integral terms, Grassmann-valued integration variables; in canonical terms, anticommuting field operators with $\{\psi(x), \psi^\dagger(y)\}_{\rm ET} = \delta^{(3)}(x - y)$ (equal-time anticommutator).
- **Required test.** No surviving mirror partners (i.e., no light right-handed pair for any left-handed Weyl arising from the KK expansion or the $S^2$ spin-cover); spin-statistics theorem satisfied; anomaly closure of UQF-4 survives the quantization (per C-FF10).
- **Route-to-UQF-gate.** UQF-7 (fermion quantization, primary); UQF-4 (BRST/BV anomaly closure, primary); UQF-3 (physical Hilbert space, positivity); UQF-13 (precision-force phenomenology, for flavor structure consumed at UQF-13 Tier-1 specification).
- **Status at Phase-1 close.** **AUDIT** (Paper 1 anomaly ledger is closed; demonstrating that the 4D-descent from the active branch preserves chirality at the quantum level without light mirror partners requires explicit Phase-3 verification).
- **Failure-mode summary.** Surviving light mirror pair → UQF-7 drops to INTERFACE; the unified-completion claim downgrades to "non-chiral candidate"; the matter content no longer matches the observed Standard Model.

### Row 6 — Higgs doublet $H$ (physical Higgs + eaten Goldstones)

- **Object.** $H \in \mathcal E_{\rm Higgs}$, the Higgs doublet field.
- **Layer.** $\otimes$.
- **Classical source.** Higgs bundle from Paper 1, with the Paper-2 weak-sector interface (the $S^2$ spin-cover + $S^1_Y$ hypercharge organize the doublet structure). Post-EWSB the doublet decomposes as $H = (\pi^+,\ (v + h + i\pi^0)/\sqrt 2)$ with $v$ the EWSB scale, $h$ the physical Higgs scalar, and $\pi^\pm, \pi^0$ the three Goldstones.
- **Quantum object.** One physical real scalar $h$ (the Higgs boson) plus three Goldstones $\pi^\pm, \pi^0$ that are removed from the physical Hilbert space by BRST gauge fixing (eaten by $W^\pm, Z^0$ to become their longitudinal polarizations per Row 4).
- **Required test.** Physical scalar $h$ with positive norm and correct (post-EWSB) mass and couplings to fermions (Yukawa) and gauge bosons; three Goldstones absent from $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$ after BRST; tree-level vacuum stable at $\langle H \rangle = v$; higher-order vacuum stability invoked by reference to Paper 1 Appendix-H authority (C-FF13).
- **Route-to-UQF-gate.** UQF-8 (Higgs / Goldstone certificate, primary); UQF-6 (gauge-boson certificate, for $W^\pm/Z^0$ getting their longitudinal modes from this row); UQF-3 (positivity of physical Higgs); UQF-13 (Higgs-coupling precision).
- **Status at Phase-1 close.** **CANDIDATE** at tree level; **AUDIT** at higher loop order (pending main-manuscript Appendix-H invocation).
- **Failure-mode summary.** Surviving physical Goldstone → UQF-6 weak-sector certificate drops; vacuum instability at higher order without an Appendix-H reference → UQF-8 drops to AUDIT.

### Row 7 — KK tower (compact-mode excitations)

- **Object.** KK modes of $G_{\mu A}$ (Row 2 tower), $G_{AB}$ (Row 3 tower), $A_\mu^a$ (Row 4 tower above zero mode), $\Psi$ (Row 5 tower), $H$ (Row 6 tower) on the compact factors $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$.
- **Layer.** $\times$ for metric-tower modes; $\otimes$ for matter/gauge/Higgs-tower modes — layer per parent object.
- **Classical source.** Nonzero-mode harmonic expansions of each field on the compact factors. KK mass scale set by the inverse compactification radii inherited from Paper 1 (main-manuscript-certificate authority for the specific values; this row treats the scale as $M_{\rm KK} \gtrsim$ TeV by interface).
- **Quantum object.** Massive 4D tower of states for each parent field, organized by harmonic mode and compactification factor. For each parent field, the tower is bounded below by $M_{\rm KK}$ and has couplings to the zero modes (gauge-boson + matter sectors) suppressed by appropriate powers of $M_{\rm KK}$ at low energy.
- **Required test.** No KK mode produces a non-Standard-Model state below current direct-test bounds; KK threshold structure feeds UQF-13 precision likelihood per C-FF11 sanity targets; KK tower contributions to graviton loops are bounded per UQF-9 / UQF-10.
- **Route-to-UQF-gate.** UQF-10 (compactification stability, primary); UQF-15 (no-hidden-force leakage, secondary — any KK mode below current bounds would mediate observable physics); UQF-13 (precision-force phenomenology, KK-threshold sub-row); UQF-1 (ledger discipline — distinguishes KK modes from zero modes to prevent silent double counting per C-FF5).
- **Status at Phase-1 close.** **AUDIT** (the KK threshold structure is bounded by interface but the explicit per-mode contributions to precision observables are deferred to UQF-13 partner work).
- **Failure-mode summary.** A KK mode falsifiably observable below current direct-test bounds → UQF-15 drops, UQF-13 reports a Tier-1 hit, and the compactification-stability claim downgrades.

### Row 8 — Ghost fields $c^\mu, c^a$

- **Object.** Faddeev-Popov / BRST ghost fields, one per gauge symmetry of the unified theory.
- **Layer.** $\oplus$/$\otimes$ — the ghost lives at the intersection of the finite-rule discipline (gauge redundancy is a rule constraint) and the field bundle (the ghost is a Grassmann field actor).
- **Classical source.** Each gauge symmetry of the unified theory contributes one ghost field: diffeomorphism ghost $c^\mu$ (for graviton gauge symmetry); Yang-Mills ghosts $c^a$ for $\mathfrak{su}(3)_c$ ($a = 1,\ldots,8$), $\mathfrak{su}(2)_L$ ($a = 1,2,3$), $\mathfrak{u}(1)_Y$ ($a = 1$). Per BRST construction, each ghost is paired with an antighost $\bar c$ and a Nakanishi-Lautrup auxiliary $B$ on the BRST-extended phase space.
- **Quantum object.** Grassmann-valued scalar fields $c^\mu, c^a$ with wrong-statistics (anticommuting where their tensor structure would suggest commuting). Removed from $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$ by BRST: physical states sit in $\ker(s)/\mathrm{im}(s)$, which excludes the ghosts by construction.
- **Required test.** Ghosts cancel unphysical (longitudinal/temporal/timelike) gauge-boson and graviton polarizations in the BRST cohomology; ghost contributions in path-integral measure restore unitarity; ghosts do not appear in $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$.
- **Route-to-UQF-gate.** UQF-4 (BRST nilpotency / anomaly closure, primary — ghosts are the load-bearing object for $s^2 = 0$); UQF-3 (physical Hilbert space — ghosts are removed by cohomology); UQF-5, UQF-6 (graviton and gauge certificates depend on ghosts cancelling the unphysical polarizations); UQF-14 (unitarity — ghost-loop contributions restore optical-theorem unitarity).
- **Status at Phase-1 close.** **CANDIDATE** (BRST ghost formalism is standard; the inherited application to the descended gauge symmetries of the active branch is straightforward at the tree/one-loop level).
- **Failure-mode summary.** Ghosts failing to cancel unphysical polarizations → UQF-4 fails → cascade per §3.4.2. Ghosts appearing in $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$ would mean negative-norm physical states and UQF-3 fails.

### Row 9 — Antifields $\Phi^*$

- **Object.** BV antifields, one per field-and-ghost in the BV-BRST construction.
- **Layer.** $\oplus$/$\otimes$ — antifields are formal BV doubling of the field content, living conceptually at the layer of the rule (BV master equation) that they encode.
- **Classical source.** For each field $\Phi \in \{h_{\mu\nu}, A_\mu^a, \psi, H, c^\mu, c^a\}$ (Rows 1, 2/4, 5, 6, 8 respectively), the BV construction introduces an antifield $\Phi^*$ of opposite Grassmann parity and ghost-number shifted by $-1$. Antifields couple to the gauge-symmetry transformations of their fields in the BV action.
- **Quantum object.** Formal partners in the BV action: $S_{\rm BV} = S_0 + \sum_\Phi \Phi^* \, s\Phi + \ldots$ where $s$ is the BRST operator. In a fully-gauge-fixed action, antifields can be eliminated by a gauge-fixing fermion; they are kept here as the load-bearing structure for canonical-vs-path-integral equivalence (UQF-2) and for nilpotency of $s$ (UQF-4).
- **Required test.** BV master equation $(S_{\rm BV}, S_{\rm BV}) = 0$ at classical level; quantum master equation $\hbar \Delta S_{\rm BV} - \tfrac 1 2 (S_{\rm BV}, S_{\rm BV}) = i \hbar \, \mathcal A$ has $\mathcal A = 0$ (anomaly closure, per UQF-4); antifields decouple from physical observables after gauge fixing.
- **Route-to-UQF-gate.** UQF-2 (canonical/path-integral equivalence, primary — antifields are the bridge between canonical-Hamiltonian and path-integral-Lagrangian descriptions); UQF-4 (BRST/BV nilpotency); UQF-1 (ledger discipline — without an antifield row, the BV formalism would silently introduce objects that are not in the ledger).
- **Status at Phase-1 close.** **CANDIDATE** (BV formalism is standard; the inherited application to the active branch is a Phase-2 build).
- **Failure-mode summary.** BV master equation violation at the classical level means the unified action is not gauge-invariant on the BV-extended phase space → UQF-4 fails. Quantum master equation anomaly $\mathcal A \neq 0$ means the gauge symmetry is anomalous at the quantum level → UQF-4 cascade.

## 4.3 Ledger summary table

| # | Object | Layer | Classical source | Quantum object | Required test | UQF route | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | $G_{\mu\nu}$ | $\times$ | 13D metric, $\pi_{\rm grav}$ | linearized graviton $h_{\mu\nu}$, spin-2 | positive-norm spin-2, 2 polarizations, Newtonian limit | UQF-5, UQF-3, UQF-9, UQF-14 | CANDIDATE |
| 2 | $G_{\mu A}$ | $\times \to \otimes$ | mixed metric, KK descent | 4D connections $A_\mu^a$ (zero mode) | correct gauge algebra, descended-actor discipline | UQF-6, UQF-1, UQF-10 | CANDIDATE |
| 3 | $G_{AB}$ | $\times$ | internal metric on $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$ | moduli scalars + tower | no light moduli, stable potential, no tachyons | UQF-10, UQF-15, UQF-5 | AUDIT |
| 4 | $A_\mu^a$ | $\otimes$ | descended zero modes of Row 2 | gluons, $W^\pm/Z^0$, photon | correct polarization counts, BRST-positive | UQF-6, UQF-8, UQF-11, UQF-14 | CANDIDATE |
| 5 | $\Psi$ | $\otimes$ | $\mathcal E_{\rm matter}$, one generation | chiral Weyl fermions $\psi_L^{(i)}$ | no mirrors, anomaly-free, spin-statistics | UQF-7, UQF-4, UQF-3, UQF-13 | AUDIT |
| 6 | $H$ | $\otimes$ | $\mathcal E_{\rm Higgs}$ doublet | physical Higgs $h$ + eaten Goldstones | physical scalar separated, Goldstones eaten, vacuum stable | UQF-8, UQF-6, UQF-3, UQF-13 | CANDIDATE (tree); AUDIT (higher loop) |
| 7 | KK tower | $\times$/$\otimes$ | nonzero harmonics of Rows 1-6 on compact factors | massive 4D tower per parent field | no observable KK mode below current bounds; threshold structure to UQF-13 | UQF-10, UQF-15, UQF-13, UQF-1 | AUDIT |
| 8 | $c^\mu, c^a$ | $\oplus$/$\otimes$ | gauge redundancy of every gauge symmetry | ghost fields, anti-Grassmann | cancel unphysical polarizations, not in $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$ | UQF-4, UQF-3, UQF-5, UQF-6, UQF-14 | CANDIDATE |
| 9 | $\Phi^*$ | $\oplus$/$\otimes$ | BV doubling of every field and ghost | BV antifields | classical master equation, no quantum-master anomaly | UQF-2, UQF-4, UQF-1 | CANDIDATE |

**Row count: 9 quantum objects.** Seven base rows from the handoff §3 template (G_MN, G_μA, G_AB, A_μ^a, Ψ, H, ghosts); two additional rows (KK tower, antifields) added because they are quantized downstream and would otherwise be silently introduced.

## 4.4 Closure under §3 UQF rows

The ledger is *closed under* the UQF stack of §3 in the following sense: every UQF row from §3 references at least one ledger row (its primary consumed object), and every ledger row is consumed by at least one UQF row (its primary route-to-UQF-gate).

The UQF → ledger consumption map:

| UQF row | Ledger rows consumed |
|---|---|
| UQF-0 (active-branch inheritance) | all (defines the branch every row lives on) |
| UQF-1 (this section) | all (this section *is* UQF-1) |
| UQF-2 (canonical/path-integral) | Row 9 (antifields) primary; all field rows secondary |
| UQF-3 (physical Hilbert space) | Rows 1, 4, 5, 6 (each must sit in positive-norm sector); Rows 8, 9 (must not) |
| UQF-4 (BRST/BV + anomaly) | Rows 5 (anomaly closure); Rows 8, 9 (BRST formalism) |
| UQF-5 (graviton) | Row 1 (primary); Rows 3 (background stability), 7 (KK loop contributions), 8 (ghost cancellation) |
| UQF-6 (gauge bosons) | Row 4 (primary); Rows 2 (descended-actor discipline), 6 (longitudinal modes), 8 (ghost cancellation) |
| UQF-7 (fermion) | Row 5 (primary) |
| UQF-8 (Higgs / Goldstone) | Row 6 (primary); Row 4 (longitudinal $W^\pm/Z^0$) |
| UQF-9 (UV completion) | Row 1 (graviton UV); Rows 4, 5, 6 (force-sector UV) |
| UQF-10 (compactification stability) | Row 3 (primary); Row 7 (KK tower) |
| UQF-11 (nonperturbative QCD) | Row 4 (gluon sub-row primary); Row 5 (quark fermions) |
| UQF-12 (strong CP) | Row 4 (gauge $\bar\theta$ angle); Row 5 (CKM phase contribution) |
| UQF-13 (precision phenomenology) | Rows 4, 5, 6, 7 (every observable sector) |
| UQF-14 (unitarity / causality / locality) | Rows 1, 4 (high-energy scattering); Row 8 (ghost-loop cancellation in optical theorem) |
| UQF-15 (no-hidden-force leakage) | Rows 3, 7 (silent residual moduli or KK modes); Rows 4, 5, 6 (declared residuals) |
| UQF-16 (final downgrade map) | all (downgrade map covers every row) |

Every ledger row appears in the right column at least once. Every UQF row appears in the left column at least once. The bipartite graph is connected: there is no orphan ledger row and no UQF row with empty consumption.

## 4.5 The ledger amendment rule

If during Phases 2 through 7 a quantization section needs to introduce an object not covered here, the discipline is:

1. **Pause** the downstream section.
2. **Amend** this ledger with a new row carrying all eight column entries.
3. **Update** §3 if the new row requires a UQF route not currently consuming it.
4. **Continue** the downstream section only after both updates are in place.

The amendment rule is the operational form of UQF-1 (quantum object ledger as a CERTIFICATE-tier deliverable). The current Phase-1 close represents nine rows; the rule expects that Phases 2–4 will not require silent additions, but if they do, the discipline above is the only honest path.

## 4.6 What is **not** in this ledger (deferred to Paper 4)

For symmetric clarity, the following classical objects are present in the corpus but are explicitly **not** ledger rows of this paper, because their quantization is deferred to Paper 4:

- $\mathcal E_{\rm proton}$ proton-decay operator bundle from Paper 1. *Not* quantized here as a separate row because (a) the proton-safety certificate is Paper 1's responsibility (C-FF13), and (b) proton-decay observables route through UQF-13 (precision-force phenomenology) as a Tier-1 specification, not through a separate ledger row. If at any later phase a quantized $\mathcal E_{\rm proton}$ object is needed standalone, the amendment rule of §4.5 applies.
- Cosmological background field(s) / inflaton candidate. Paper 4 reserve.
- Hidden-sector candidate field(s) underlying any dark-matter candidate. Paper 4 reserve.
- Boundary-parity data on $S^1_Y / \mathbb Z_2$. Inherited from Paper 1 as a constraint (consumed by UQF-12 strong-CP candidate) but not quantized in this paper as a separate dynamical object. If Paper 4 promotes the boundary-parity data to a dynamical mechanism, that paper will need its own ledger row.

The non-rows are listed not because they are unimportant but because a reviewer should be able to confirm that the paper does not silently quantize anything that should be deferred.

## 4.7 Bottom line for §4

- 9 quantum-object rows, each load-bearing.
- Every UQF row from §3 consumes at least one ledger row; every ledger row is consumed by at least one UQF row.
- Per-row status at Phase-1 close: 5 CANDIDATE, 3 AUDIT, 1 mixed (Higgs: tree CANDIDATE / higher-loop AUDIT). Aggregate by min-rule: **AUDIT**.
- Ledger amendment rule (§4.5) preserves CERTIFICATE-tier status of UQF-1 going forward.
- Cosmological / dark-sector / proton-decay-operator objects are explicitly deferred (§4.6), preserving the Paper-3 claim boundary.

Phase 1 closes with this ledger. Phase 2 begins by consuming Rows 8 and 9 (ghosts and antifields) to build the BV-BRST framework, then Rows 1, 4, 5, 6 to define the physical Hilbert space.

# 5. Quantization Framework: Canonical + BV-BRST + Path Integral
* · gate UQF-2 · drafted 2026-06-08*

> **Gate card — UQF-2: Canonical / path-integral equivalence** *(auto-derived from §3.3 / §4.4, the single source of truth per §3.0; any discrepancy with this chapter is a drafting bug)*
>
> | Field | Value |
> |---|---|
> | Tier | **CANDIDATE** *(phase-close reconciliation, §3.8: the §5 framework build — three-formulation equivalence on the free/perturbative overlap, §5.5/§5.8 — discharges the Phase-2 target; CERTIFICATE on interacting sectors per declared scheme remains open).* Original Phase-1 entry: INTERFACE. |
