## 9.1 Gluon certificate (UQF-6A)

The gluon certificate verifies that the eight massless color gauge bosons descend with exactly two transverse physical polarizations each and BRST-positive states. The subsections fix the object and its projection from the $K_6 = SU(3)/U(1)^2$ isometry sector (§9.1.1), state the layer discipline that keeps the color connection in the ⊗-bundle, and record the polarization count and positivity that constitute the certificate.

### 9.1.1 Object and projection

The carriers are the eight gluon fields $A^a_\mu(x)$, $a=1,\ldots,8$, taking values in $\mathfrak{su}(3)$. The underlying Paper 2 §7 projection is

$$\pi_{\rm strong}:\mathfrak B_{\rm active}\to\mathrm{EFT}_{SU(3)_c},$$

with the surviving color symmetry sourced by the left $SU(3)$ action on $K_6=SU(3)/T^2$ (Paper 2 §7.11.1–§7.11.3) and the gluon defined as the corresponding 4D gauge connection (§7.11.4):

$$A_\mu(x) = A^a_\mu(x)\,T^a,\qquad T^a\in\mathfrak{su}(3),\qquad [T^a,T^b] = i f^{abc} T^c.$$

The geometric chain: the $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ flag manifold carries an $SU(3)$ left action whose Killing vectors live in the mixed-block $G_{\mu A}$ sector; Bridge A (Paper 2 §5.4) maps the zero modes of this mixed-block content along the isometry directions to 4D gauge connections in $\mathcal E_{\rm gauge}$.

### 9.1.2 Layer discipline

Paper 2 §7.10 fixes:

- **$\times$-layer:** $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$, compact spectrum, color geometry.
- **$\oplus$-layer:** center/charge rules, color-singlet admissibility, BRST gauge-fixing rule, regulator/freeze discipline, $\theta$-scope rule.
- **$\otimes$-layer:** gluon connection $A^a_\mu$ in $\mathcal E_{\rm gauge}$, field strength $G^a_{\mu\nu}$, Faddeev–Popov ghost/antighost fields $c^a, \bar c^a$, Nakanishi–Lautrup auxiliary $B^a$, quark color modules $V_{SU(3)}$, BRST domain.

This satisfies C-FF6 (gauge-origin): the 4D gluon connection is *not* a primitive 13D boson; it is the descended/effective bundle actor obtained from the mixed-block route of Bridge A, repackaged at the $\otimes$ layer over the surviving $K_6$ color isometry. C-FF7 (gravity/gauge separation) is enforced by the §8.2 KK decomposition (UQFC-8): the gluon comes from $h_{\mu A}^{(0)}$ projected onto $SU(3)_c$ isometry directions of $K_6$, *not* from $h_{\mu\nu}^{(0)}$ (which is the graviton row).

### 9.1.3 Quantization

**Free-field expansion.** In a Lorenz / BRST gauge $\partial^\mu A^a_\mu = 0$, each gluon is expanded in helicity modes

$$A^a_\mu(x) = \sum_{\lambda=\pm}\int\frac{d^3 k}{(2\pi)^3\,2\omega_k}\Big[\varepsilon^\lambda_\mu(k)\,a^a_\lambda(k)\,e^{-ik\cdot x} + \varepsilon^{\lambda*}_\mu(k)\,a^{a\dagger}_\lambda(k)\,e^{ik\cdot x}\Big],$$

with $k^2 = 0$, $\omega_k = |\vec k|$, $k^\mu\varepsilon^\lambda_\mu(k) = 0$, and creation/annihilation algebra

$$[a^a_\lambda(k),\,a^{b\dagger}_{\lambda'}(k')] = (2\pi)^3 2\omega_k\,\delta^{ab}\delta_{\lambda\lambda'}\delta^3(k-k').$$

**Non-abelian gauge fixing.** The BRST charge $Q_{\rm BRST}$ generates

$$s\,A^a_\mu = D_\mu c^a,\qquad s\,c^a = -\tfrac12 g_s f^{abc} c^b c^c,\qquad s\,\bar c^a = i B^a,\qquad s\,B^a = 0,$$

with $D_\mu c^a = \partial_\mu c^a + g_s f^{abc} A^b_\mu c^c$, and is nilpotent: $s^2 = 0$, equivalently $\{Q_{\rm BRST},Q_{\rm BRST}\}=0$. The gauge-fixed action is

$$S_{\rm gf} = \int d^4 x\Big[-\tfrac14 G^a_{\mu\nu}G^{a\mu\nu} + B^a\partial^\mu A^a_\mu + \tfrac{\xi}{2}B^a B^a + \bar c^a\,\partial^\mu D_\mu c^a\Big],$$

with $G^a_{\mu\nu}=\partial_\mu A^a_\nu - \partial_\nu A^a_\mu + g_s f^{abc}A^b_\mu A^c_\nu$ (Paper 2 §7.11.5).

### 9.1.4 Polarization counting

Each massless gluon has $4$ Lorentz components; the BRST physical-state condition $Q_{\rm BRST}|\mathrm{phys}\rangle = 0$ together with the gauge-fixing constraint removes the timelike and longitudinal modes (or, equivalently, the FP ghost / antighost contribution cancels them in physical amplitudes). Each gluon retains $2$ transverse helicity-$\pm 1$ polarizations. Total over color: $8\times 2 = 16$ physical polarization–color states.

### 9.1.5 Norm positivity (Kugo–Ojima)

BRST cohomology selects the physical subspace:

$$\mathcal H_{\rm phys}^{\rm QCD} = \ker Q_{\rm BRST}/\operatorname{im} Q_{\rm BRST},$$

with positive-definite inner product on the cohomology classes (Kugo–Ojima construction). Perturbatively, gluon states with negative or zero norm are exact or cohomologically trivial and drop out of physical observables.

**Tier:** **CERTIFICATE-tier** perturbatively. The nonperturbative completion (where the cohomology is reorganized by the confining vacuum) is the load-bearing content of UQF-11 and is routed to §12.

### 9.1.6 Coupling to quark matter

Standard QCD covariant derivative (Paper 2 §7.11.6):

$$D_\mu = \partial_\mu - i g_s A^a_\mu T^a,$$
$$S_{\rm QCD} = \int d^4 x\,\sqrt{-g_4}\,\Big[-\tfrac14 G^a_{\mu\nu}G^{a\mu\nu} + \sum_f \bar q_f(i\gamma^\mu D_\mu - m_f) q_f\Big],$$

with quark color representations fixed by the matter ledger Paper 2 §7.12 / §7.12a. The quark color content per generation is $Q_L: (3,2)_{1/6}$, $u^c_L: (\bar 3,1)_{-2/3}$, $d^c_L: (\bar 3,1)_{1/3}$ (Paper 2 §8.4 / §8.5). Color anomaly cancellation is enforced per generation: the cubic $SU(3)^3$ anomaly vanishes because $\mathrm{tr}_3 T^aT^bT^c + \mathrm{tr}_{\bar 3} T^aT^bT^c = 0$ for the $Q_L + u^c_L + d^c_L$ content.

### 9.1.7 Vacuum and mass (perturbative)

At tree / perturbative level $\langle A^a_\mu\rangle = 0$ and the gluon is massless: no $m^2 A^a_\mu A^{a\mu}$ term is gauge invariant. At low energy the QCD vacuum is *not* the perturbative vacuum; the confining vacuum and the dynamical mass gap are the load-bearing content of **UQF-11** and are routed to §12.

### 9.1.8 Asymptotic freedom — low-energy sanity

The one-loop $\beta$-function (Paper 2 §7.11.7),

$$\beta(g_s) = -\frac{g_s^3}{16\pi^2}\Big(11 - \tfrac{2}{3}n_f\Big) + \cdots,$$

gives the correct asymptotically-free RG sign for the active SM flavor count, and the strong scale $\Lambda_{\rm QCD}$ is defined as the dimensional-transmutation scale of this flow. The asymptotic-freedom recovery is the **C-FF11 low-energy sanity target** for the gluon sub-row.

### 9.1.9 Gluon sub-row tier

| UQF row | Tier | Status |
|---|---|---|
| UQF-6A — Perturbative gluon quantization: $8$ colored vector bosons, $2$ transverse polarizations each, BRST physical states, standard quark coupling, color anomaly cancellation per generation, perturbative asymptotic freedom | **CERTIFICATE** | Closed at the level standard perturbative QCD supports after Paper 2 §7 is accepted. |
| UQF-6A* — Confinement, mass gap, hadron spectrum, chiral symmetry breaking | **DEFERRED** | Routed to UQF-11 (§12). Downgrade if §12 not earned: UQF-6A* drops to *Open / Diagnostic*; UQF-6A remains **CERTIFICATE** at the perturbative level. |
| UQF-6A** — Strong CP, $\bar\theta$ suppression | **DEFERRED** | Routed to UQF-12 (§13). |

---

## 9.2 Weak boson certificate (UQF-6B): $W^\pm, Z^0$

The weak-boson certificate handles the massive case: each of $W^\pm, Z^0$ must carry two transverse polarizations plus one longitudinal mode supplied by an eaten Goldstone, with BRST-positive physical states after electroweak breaking. The subsections fix the object and its projection (§9.2.1), state the layer discipline, and record the three-polarization count and positivity — the point where this certificate couples to the Higgs/Goldstone certificate of §10.

### 9.2.1 Object and projection

The carriers are the massive vector bosons $W^\pm_\mu, Z^0_\mu$ obtained after the electroweak breaking step (Paper 2 §8.5b, §8.11.5)

$$SU(2)_L\times U(1)_Y \to U(1)_{\rm em}.$$

In the unbroken basis the carriers are $W^a_\mu$ ($a=1,2,3$) and $B_\mu$. After breaking,

$$W^\pm_\mu = \tfrac{1}{\sqrt 2}(W^1_\mu \mp i W^2_\mu),\qquad Z_\mu = \cos\theta_W\,W^3_\mu - \sin\theta_W\,B_\mu,$$

with the photon $A_\mu = \sin\theta_W\,W^3_\mu + \cos\theta_W\,B_\mu$ split off into the QED certificate of §9.3. The Weinberg angle $\theta_W$ is fixed by $\cos\theta_W = g/\sqrt{g^2+g'^2}$.

The §8 projection $\pi_{\rm weak}:\mathfrak B_{\rm active}\to\mathrm{EFT}_{\rm EW}$ sources $SU(2)_L$ from the $S^2$ spin-cover (Paper 2 §8.11.1–§8.11.2) and $U(1)_Y$ from the $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ hypercharge interval (§8.11.3). Both descend through Bridge A from the mixed metric block $G_{\mu A}$ projected onto the $S^2$ and $S^1_Y$ isometry directions.

### 9.2.2 Layer discipline

Paper 2 §8.10 fixes:

- **$\times$-layer:** $S^2$ (weak-isospin carrier), $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ (hypercharge with parity identification), compact spectra.
- **$\oplus$-layer:** chirality/parity rules, $\mathbb Z_2$ and $\mathbb Z_6$ projectors, $Q = T_3 + Y$ rule, freeze protocol, EW-breaking selection.
- **$\otimes$-layer:** weak gauge fields $W^a_\mu, B_\mu$, Higgs/Wilson-line doublet operator $H$, matter doublets/singlets, lepton/quark domains, eaten-Goldstone modes, BRST ghost/antighost content.

C-FF4 (charge-normalization, $Q = T_3 + Y$), C-FF6 (gauge-origin, descended-not-primitive), C-FF7 (gravity/gauge separation, $S^2$ and $S^1_Y$ are *compact internal*, not part of $\mathcal M_4$), and C-FF8 (QED downstream of EW) all run through this row.

### 9.2.3 Quantization

**Free-field expansion in $R_\xi$ gauge.** After EW breaking, $W^\pm$ and $Z$ are massive vector bosons with three physical polarizations each:

$$W^\pm_\mu(x) = \sum_{\lambda=0,\pm 1}\int\frac{d^3 k}{(2\pi)^3\,2\omega_k}\Big[\varepsilon^\lambda_\mu(k)\,a^\pm_\lambda(k)\,e^{-ik\cdot x} + \mathrm{h.c.}\Big],\qquad \omega_k = \sqrt{|\vec k|^2 + m_W^2},$$

and similarly for $Z_\mu$ with $\omega_k = \sqrt{|\vec k|^2 + m_Z^2}$. The $R_\xi$-gauge action contains gauge-fixing terms

$$\mathcal L_{\rm gf} = -\tfrac{1}{2\xi}|F^a|^2,$$

with $F^a$ chosen to cancel the mixing between the broken gauge field and the would-be Goldstone bosons. The Faddeev–Popov sector contains $SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$ ghost / antighost fields whose masses are also $\xi$-dependent.

**BRST.** The full electroweak BRST charge is nilpotent ($s^2 = 0$); the longitudinal mode of $W$ and $Z$, the would-be Goldstones, and the FP ghosts have $\xi$-dependent masses but cancel as a whole in physical S-matrix elements (Slavnov–Taylor identities).

### 9.2.4 Polarization counting and Goldstone bookkeeping

Goldstone counting follows Paper 2 §8.5b: the breaking $SU(2)_L\times U(1)_Y\to U(1)_{\rm em}$ removes $3$ broken generators, so the minimal Higgs doublet supplies $3$ Goldstone modes that are *eaten* by $W^\pm, Z$.

| Stage | $W^a_\mu, B_\mu$ | Higgs doublet | Photon | Total |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Before breaking | $4 \times 2 = 8$ massless polarizations | $4$ real scalar modes | — | $12$ |
| After breaking | $W^\pm: 3+3 = 6$, $Z: 3$, total $9$ massive polarizations | $1$ physical Higgs ($h$) | $2$ transverse | $12$ |

The closure $8 + 4 = 9 + 2 + 1 = 12$ is the visible witness for the C-FF5 no-double-counting constraint at the EW-breaking step. UQFC-9 inherits this bookkeeping from UQC-2 §2.4.4 and Paper 2 §8.5b verbatim.

### 9.2.5 Norm positivity

In $R_\xi$ gauge the unphysical scalar (longitudinal) modes, would-be Goldstones, and FP ghosts have negative-norm contributions that cancel in BRST cohomology / physical S-matrix elements. The **Goldstone-equivalence theorem** at high energy $E \gg m_W$ reproduces longitudinal $W,Z$ scattering amplitudes by the eaten-Goldstone scalar amplitudes, providing a direct unitarity check up to the Higgs scale. Above $E \sim m_H$, longitudinal $WW$ scattering is unitarized by the Higgs, which is the load-bearing reason a Higgs (or some unitarizing scalar sector) is required for EW completion at the perturbative level.

**Tier:** **CERTIFICATE-tier** at the level standard EW QFT supports.

### 9.2.6 Coupling to matter

Charged-current and neutral-current couplings inherit from Paper 2 §8.11.6 mixing and §8.11.7 Fermi reduction:

$$\mathcal L_{\rm cc} = \frac{g}{\sqrt 2}\,W^+_\mu\,J^{+\mu}_{\rm cc} + \mathrm{h.c.},\qquad \mathcal L_{\rm nc} = \frac{g}{\cos\theta_W}\,Z_\mu\,J^\mu_{\rm nc},$$

with $J^{+\mu}_{\rm cc} = \bar u_L \gamma^\mu d_L + \bar \nu_L \gamma^\mu e_L + \ldots$ (the left-handed charged-current built from the $S^2$ spin-cover doublets of Paper 2 §8.11.2) and $J^\mu_{\rm nc} = J^{3\mu} - \sin^2\theta_W J^\mu_{\rm em}$. The left-handed structure is what implements parity violation: only the $S^2$-doublet-projected (left-handed) sectors couple to the charged current. At energies $E\ll m_W$ the charged-current sector reduces to the Fermi interaction

$$\mathcal L_{\rm Fermi} = -\frac{G_F}{\sqrt 2}\,J^{\mu}_{\rm cc}\,J_\mu^{\rm cc},\qquad \frac{G_F}{\sqrt 2} = \frac{g^2}{8\,m_W^2}.$$

The Fermi limit is the **C-FF11 low-energy sanity target** for the weak sub-row.

### 9.2.7 Vacuum and mass

The vacuum is the Higgs VEV

$$\langle H\rangle = \begin{pmatrix}0\\v/\sqrt 2\end{pmatrix},\qquad v \simeq 246~\mathrm{GeV},$$

descended from the §8.5a doublet representation. Tree-level masses (Paper 2 §8.5c):

$$m_W = \tfrac12 g v,\qquad m_Z = \tfrac12\sqrt{g^2+g'^2}\,v,\qquad \cos\theta_W = \frac{g}{\sqrt{g^2+g'^2}},$$

$$\rho \equiv \frac{m_W^2}{m_Z^2 \cos^2\theta_W} = 1\ \text{at tree level}.$$

The tree-level $\rho = 1$ identity is a binding consistency check; failure falsifies the EW interface (Paper 2 §8.5c). Loop-level corrections to $\rho$ (e.g., from the top-quark Yukawa coupling) are part of the EW precision sector and are routed to UQF-13 (§16).

### 9.2.8 Weak sub-row tier

| UQF row | Tier | Status |
|---|---|---|
| UQF-6B — Post-breaking quantization of $W^\pm$ and $Z^0$: massive vector boson quantization, three physical polarizations each, $R_\xi$-gauge norm positivity via Slavnov–Taylor, charged- and neutral-current matter couplings, tree-level mass relations, tree-level $\rho = 1$, Fermi limit | **CERTIFICATE** | Closed at the level standard EW QFT supports after Paper 2 §8 is accepted. |
| UQF-6B* — Full EW precision fit ($S, T, U$ at loop precision, flavor anomalies, oblique-parameter closure) | **DEFERRED** | Routed to UQF-13 (§16). |
| UQF-6B** — EW vacuum stability beyond tree-level, vacuum-decay lifetime | **DEFERRED** | Routed to UQF-8 (§10) + UQF-9 (§14). |

---

## 9.3 Photon certificate (UQF-6C)

The photon certificate closes the gauge-boson trio with the unbroken $U(1)_{\rm em}$ case: a single massless vector with two transverse polarizations, defined as the $\sin\theta_W\,W^3 + \cos\theta_W\,B$ combination that survives electroweak breaking. The subsections fix the composite projection (§9.3.1), state the layer discipline, and record that the massless count and positivity match the gluon case exactly, completing UQF-6.

### 9.3.1 Object and projection

The photon $A_\mu$ is the unbroken Abelian combination

$$A_\mu = \sin\theta_W\,W^3_\mu + \cos\theta_W\,B_\mu.$$

The Paper 2 §9 projection is **composite**:

$$\pi_{\rm QED}\circ\pi_{\rm weak}:\mathfrak B_{\rm active}\to\mathrm{EFT}_{U(1)_{\rm em}},$$

reflecting **C-FF8**: QED is *not* an independent parent reduction of the 13D backbone; it is the post-EW-breaking remnant of $SU(2)_L\times U(1)_Y$. The photon does *not* introduce a new compact factor in $\mathfrak B_{\rm active}$; it inherits the $S^2 \times S^1_Y$ carriers from the weak sector.

### 9.3.2 Layer discipline

Paper 2 §9.10 fixes:

- **$\times$-layer:** $\mathcal M_4$, electroweak compact carriers $S^2, S^1_Y$ (carried over from the weak sector; no new compact factor).
- **$\oplus$-layer:** charge rule $Q = T_3 + Y$, $U(1)_{\rm em}$ selection from the EW breaking pattern, gauge-fixing rule, static-limit rule, local charge-conservation rule.
- **$\otimes$-layer:** photon field $A_\mu$ in $\mathcal E_{\rm gauge}$, charged matter, electric current $J^\mu$, field strength $F_{\mu\nu} = \partial_\mu A_\nu - \partial_\nu A_\mu$, photon stress-energy contribution to $T_{\mu\nu}$.

### 9.3.3 Quantization

Standard QED in Lorenz / BRST gauge $\partial^\mu A_\mu = 0$:

$$A_\mu(x) = \sum_{\lambda=\pm}\int\frac{d^3 k}{(2\pi)^3\,2\omega_k}\Big[\varepsilon^\lambda_\mu(k)\,a_\lambda(k)\,e^{-ik\cdot x} + \varepsilon^{\lambda*}_\mu(k)\,a^\dagger_\lambda(k)\,e^{ik\cdot x}\Big],\qquad \omega_k = |\vec k|,$$

with creation/annihilation algebra $[a_\lambda(k),a^\dagger_{\lambda'}(k')] = (2\pi)^3\,2\omega_k\,\delta_{\lambda\lambda'}\delta^3(k-k')$, and Gupta–Bleuler / BRST physical-state condition selecting the transverse subspace.

### 9.3.4 Polarization counting

Four Lorentz components, $-2$ from gauge fixing + physical-state condition, leaves $2$ transverse helicity-$\pm 1$ polarizations. Standard photon polarization vectors satisfy

$$k^\mu \varepsilon^\lambda_\mu(k) = 0,\qquad \varepsilon^\lambda_\mu(k)\varepsilon^{\lambda'*\mu}(k) = -\delta^{\lambda\lambda'},$$

on shell.

### 9.3.5 Norm positivity — photon-mass ledger

The photon-mass ledger of Paper 2 §9.12 must pass every row:

| Requirement | Pass condition |
|---|---|
| $U(1)_{\rm em}$ unbroken | photon has no gauge-invariant mass term |
| charge generator preserved | $Q = T_3 + Y$ commutes with the EW vacuum / Wilson-line sector |
| no boundary mass | orbifold / boundary terms on $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ do not generate a photon mass |
| Ward identity | charge conservation $\partial_\mu J^\mu = 0$ holds |

Together with the Gupta–Bleuler / BRST physical-state condition, the four-row ledger certifies that the photon Hilbert space is positive-norm and the photon is exactly massless. The falsifier of Paper 2 §9.13 is binding: any nonzero $m_\gamma^2 A_\mu A^\mu$ from EW breaking, orbifold boundary terms, or compactification corrections fails the QED interface.

**Tier:** **CERTIFICATE-tier** perturbatively.

### 9.3.6 Coupling to matter

Standard minimal coupling:

$$D_\mu = \partial_\mu - i e\,Q\,A_\mu,\qquad S_{\rm QED} = \int d^4 x\,\sqrt{-g_4}\,\Big[-\tfrac14 F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu} + \bar\psi(i\gamma^\mu D_\mu - m)\psi\Big],$$

with $F_{\mu\nu} = \partial_\mu A_\nu - \partial_\nu A_\mu$ (Abelian — no commutator term, Paper 2 §9.11.5) and the Ward identity $\partial_\mu J^\mu = 0$ (§9.11.6). Electric charges are read off the charge-normalization table (Paper 2 §9.14), using $Q = T_3 + Y$ on the matter ledger Paper 2 §8.4:

| Field | $T_3$ | $Y$ | $Q$ |
|---|---|---|---|
| $\nu_L$ | $+1/2$ | $-1/2$ | $0$ |
| $e_L$ | $-1/2$ | $-1/2$ | $-1$ |
| $u_L$ | $+1/2$ | $+1/6$ | $+2/3$ |
| $d_L$ | $-1/2$ | $+1/6$ | $-1/3$ |
| $u^c_L$ | $0$ | $-2/3$ | $-2/3$ |
| $d^c_L$ | $0$ | $+1/3$ | $+1/3$ |
| $e^c_L$ | $0$ | $+1$ | $+1$ |

The standard SM electric charges are recovered exactly.

### 9.3.7 Vacuum and mass

$\langle A_\mu\rangle = 0$. $m_\gamma = 0$ enforced by the unbroken-$U(1)_{\rm em}$ remnant of EW breaking; the §9.12 ledger is the binding witness. The static Coulomb limit (Paper 2 §9.11.8–§9.11.9) is the **C-FF11 low-energy sanity target** for the photon sub-row:

$$\nabla^2 \Phi = -\rho_{\rm el}/\epsilon_0,\qquad \Phi(r) = \frac{Q_{\rm tot}}{4\pi\epsilon_0\,r}.$$

### 9.3.8 Photon sub-row tier — no Landau-pole overclaim

| UQF row | Tier | Status |
|---|---|---|
| UQF-6C — Perturbative quantized photon: $2$ transverse polarizations, Gupta–Bleuler / BRST physical-state norm positivity, exact masslessness via Paper 2 §9.12 ledger, standard QED matter coupling, Ward identity, recovered Maxwell equations, recovered static Coulomb limit, $Q = T_3 + Y$ charge assignments | **CERTIFICATE** | Closed at the level standard perturbative QED supports after Paper 2 §9 is accepted. |
| UQF-6C* — QED Landau-pole resolution beyond the EFT statement; full nonperturbative QED theorem package | **AUDIT / DEFERRED** | Routed to UQF-9 (§14). UQFC-9 does *not* claim Landau-pole resolution; the perturbative certificate is valid within the EFT validity domain $E \ll \Lambda_{\rm Landau}$, where $\Lambda_{\rm Landau}$ is far above the relevant SM scales. Above that EFT cutoff, the theory either UV-completes via the §14 route or downgrades to an EFT-only statement. |

---

## 9.4 Cross-carrier consistency for the gauge-boson row

The three sub-rows above must satisfy the C-FF backbone *as a set*. The single load-bearing cross-constraint is the **C-FF5 + C-FF6 + C-FF7 triple** of Paper 2: the mixed-block $G_{\mu A}$ zero modes are claimed *exactly once*, as the geometric origin of the 4D gauge connections in $\mathcal E_{\rm gauge}$ (Bridge A), and are partitioned by the surviving isometry-direction subgroups into the gluon (from $SU(3)_c$ on $K_6$), the weak bosons (from $SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$ on $S^2 \times S^1_Y$), and — composite — the photon (from the unbroken EW combination). They are *not* re-counted as gravitons (UQFC-8) and are *not* re-counted as moduli (UQFC-15).

### 9.4.1 Backbone compliance table — gauge sub-rows

| Constraint | Gluon (UQF-6A) | $W/Z$ (UQF-6B) | Photon (UQF-6C) |
|---|---|---|---|
| **C-FF0** one-parent-geometry | $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ subset of $\mathfrak B_{\rm active}$ | $S^2 \times S^1_Y$ subset of $\mathfrak B_{\rm active}$ | composite — no new compact factor |
| **C-FF1** layer discipline | §9.1.2 | §9.2.2 | §9.3.2 |
| **C-FF2** projection-specification | §7.0 of Paper 2 | §8.0 of Paper 2 | §9.0 of Paper 2 (composite) |
| **C-FF3** shared matter-bundle | quarks per §7.12 | leptons + quarks per §8.4 | all charged matter per §8.4, charges via $Q = T_3 + Y$ |
| **C-FF4** charge-normalization | color reps from §7.12; no $T_3, Y$ | $Q = T_3 + Y$ used throughout | $Q = T_3 + Y$ used exclusively for $\gamma$ couplings |
| **C-FF5** no-double-counting | gluon = $h_{\mu A}^{(0)}$ projected on $K_6$ isometry; not graviton, not moduli | $W^a, B$ = $h_{\mu A}^{(0)}$ projected on $S^2, S^1_Y$ isometries; not graviton, not moduli; Goldstones eaten cleanly | $A_\mu$ = unbroken EW combination; not separately added $U(1)$ primitive |
| **C-FF6** gauge-origin | descended bundle actor, not primitive 13D boson | descended, not primitive | descended via composite map, not primitive |
| **C-FF7** gravity/gauge separation | gluon from $G_{\mu A}$, not $G_{\mu\nu}$ | $W^a, B$ from $G_{\mu A}$, not $G_{\mu\nu}$ | $A$ from $G_{\mu A}$ via EW combination, not $G_{\mu\nu}$ |
| **C-FF8** QED-downstream-of-EW | n/a | source of the downstream branching | binding constraint — photon is downstream remnant, not parent |

| **C-FF10** anomaly-compatibility | color anomaly cancels per generation (§9.1.6) | full EW anomaly ledger of Paper 2 §8.5 | photon couples to anomaly-free $Q = T_3 + Y$ charges |
| **C-FF11** low-energy sanity | asymptotic freedom (§9.1.8) | Fermi limit (§9.2.6) + $\rho = 1$ (§9.2.7) | Coulomb law (§9.3.7) |
| **C-FF12** scope-boundary | confinement to §12; strong CP to §13 | EW precision to §16; vacuum stability to §10, §14 | Landau-pole to §14 |
| **C-FF13** main-manuscript authority | Wilson-line / freeze / gate authority not directly invoked here; flavor structure routed to Paper 1 | Higgs Wilson-line authority via Paper 1 Appendix H (invoked by §10) | no main-manuscript authority directly invoked |
| **C-FF14** falsification-path | Paper 2 §7.15 carried over | Paper 2 §8.15 carried over | Paper 2 §9.13 + §9.19 carried over |

### 9.4.2 Visible witness of cross-row consistency

The single visible witness for the cross-row C-FF5+6+7 triple is the polarization-bookkeeping table of §9.2.4: $8 + 4 = 9 + 2 + 1 = 12$ across the EW-breaking step. The gluon sub-row sits at $8 \times 2 = 16$ physical color polarizations *separately* from this count (the gluons descend from a different compact-factor isometry $K_6$, not $S^2 \times S^1_Y$). The graviton sub-row of UQFC-8 sits at $2$ physical helicities, *separately* from both. If any sub-row ever "borrowed" modes from another, the visible witness — total physical polarization count — would shift.

---

## 9.5 Falsifiers (all three sub-rows)

The gauge-boson row is falsified by any of the following:

1. A gluon mass term $m_g^2 A^a_\mu A^{a\mu}$ surviving the BRST gauge fixing perturbatively (would falsify UQF-6A masslessness).
2. A $\beta$-function sign change in the perturbative QCD coupling — i.e., loss of asymptotic freedom for the SM active flavor count (would falsify UQF-6A low-energy sanity).
3. Failure of the color cubic anomaly cancellation per generation (would falsify UQF-6A C-FF10).
4. Tree-level $\rho \neq 1$ for the SM Higgs doublet (would falsify UQF-6B EW interface).
5. A propagating Goldstone mode that fails to be eaten by $W^\pm$ or $Z$ (would falsify UQF-6B Goldstone bookkeeping).
6. A non-vanishing electric charge for the photon, or $A_\mu$ failing to be the unbroken combination $\sin\theta_W W^3 + \cos\theta_W B$ (would falsify UQF-6C C-FF8).
7. A photon mass $m_\gamma \neq 0$ from EW breaking, orbifold boundary terms, or compactification corrections (would falsify UQF-6C via the Paper 2 §9.12 ledger).
8. A Ward-identity violation $\partial_\mu J^\mu \neq 0$ for the electric current (would falsify UQF-6C and the QED gauge fixing).
9. Failure of either the Fermi limit (low-$E$ EW) or the Coulomb limit (low-$E$ QED) at leading order (would falsify the §9.2 / §9.3 C-FF11 low-energy sanity targets).

---

|---|---|---|---|
| UQF-6A | gluons | **CERTIFICATE** (perturbative) | nonperturbative → §12 (UQF-11); strong CP → §13 (UQF-12) |
| UQF-6B | $W^\pm, Z$ | **CERTIFICATE** (EW-broken perturbative) | precision fit → §16 (UQF-13); vacuum stability → §10 + §14 |
| UQF-6C | photon | **CERTIFICATE** (perturbative QED) | Landau-pole / nonpert QED → §14 (UQF-9) |

The single most 13D-specific subtlety across the three sub-rows is **the C-FF5+6+7 triple at the mixed-block-zero-mode level**: the same $G_{\mu A}$ zero modes have to partition cleanly across the three sub-rows (via the surviving compact-factor isometries $SU(3)$ on $K_6$, $SU(2)_L$ on $S^2$, $U(1)_Y$ on $S^1_Y$) without overlapping the graviton row (UQFC-8) or the moduli row (UQFC-15). If this partition fails, the three sub-row certificates cannot be simultaneously closed.

## 9.7 Boundary statement

UQFC-9 *certifies* the perturbative quantized gauge bosons at UQF-6A / B / C tier:

- 8 gluons with 2 transverse polarizations each, BRST physical states (Kugo–Ojima), standard quark coupling, color anomaly cancellation per generation, asymptotic freedom for the SM active flavor count;
- $W^\pm$ and $Z$ as massive vector bosons after EW breaking with 3 polarizations each, $R_\xi$ gauge fixing with Slavnov–Taylor identities, charged- and neutral-current matter couplings, tree-level masses $m_W = gv/2$, $m_Z = \sqrt{g^2+g'^2}\,v/2$, tree-level $\rho = 1$, Goldstone-equivalence theorem at high energy, Fermi limit at low energy;
- the photon as the unbroken EW combination with $2$ transverse polarizations, Gupta–Bleuler / BRST physical-state condition, exact masslessness via the four-row §9.12 ledger, standard $Q = T_3 + Y$ matter coupling, Ward identity, Maxwell equations, Coulomb law.

UQFC-9 does *not* claim:

- confinement, the QCD mass gap, hadron spectroscopy, chiral symmetry breaking (routed to UQF-11 / §12),
- strong-CP resolution / $\bar\theta$ suppression (routed to UQF-12 / §13),
- the full EW precision fit, $S, T, U$ at loop precision, oblique-parameter closure (routed to UQF-13 / §16),
- EW vacuum stability beyond tree level, vacuum-decay lifetime (routed to UQF-8 / §10 + UQF-9 / §14),
- QED Landau-pole nonperturbative resolution (routed to UQF-9 / §14),
- the KK gauge-boson tower spectrum or quantum compactification stability under gauge-boson loops (routed to UQF-10 / §15).

## 10.0 Purpose and boundary

The Higgs / Goldstone / vacuum row of the UQF certificate stack is **UQF-8**:

> *Higgs / Goldstone quantum certificate.* Separate the physical Higgs scalar from the three eaten Goldstone modes; identify the electroweak vacuum $\langle H\rangle = (0, v/\sqrt 2)^\top$, $v \simeq 246~\mathrm{GeV}$; quantize the Higgs as a canonical scalar around that vacuum with mass $m_h^2 = 2\lambda v^2$; record the Yukawa coupling structure to fermions; verify that the photon stays massless after EW breaking (joint with UQF-6C); state the radiative-stability and vacuum-stability boundary explicitly.

UQF-8 is structurally the most 13D-specific of the four force-carrier certificates in Phase 3. The Higgs *quantization* (a canonical massive scalar with $m_h^2 = 2\lambda v^2$) is textbook; the Higgs *origin* (a Wilson-line / compactified scalar on $S^1_Y$, descended from the 13D framework) is the load-bearing 13D-specific subtlety. This is the AUDIT-tier flag on the row.

This section makes the split explicit:

- **CERTIFICATE-tier sub-row** (UQF-8A): tree-level canonical scalar quantization around the EW vacuum, Goldstone separation, $W^\pm / Z$ mass generation, photon-stays-massless joint check, tree-level Yukawa coupling structure, tree-level relation $m_h^2 = 2\lambda v^2$.
- **AUDIT-tier sub-row** (UQF-8B): the Wilson-line origin of $H$ on $S^1_Y$, the vacuum-selection mechanism in the 13D compactified geometry, and the radiative-stability protection (whether it is exact, parametric, or downgraded). Authority routed to Paper 1 Appendix H.
- **DEFERRED sub-row** (UQF-8C): full radiative stability under SM running plus 13D KK corrections, and the vacuum metastability / lifetime calculation. Routed to §14 (UQF-9) and §15 (UQF-10).

**Scope and outside-scope.**

```
+--------------------------------------------------------------------+
|  Inside UQFC-10:                                                   |
|    - origin of the Higgs mode (Wilson-line / compactified scalar,  |
|      cross-referenced to Paper 1 Appendix H)                       |
|    - tree-level potential structure                                 |
|    - vacuum selection (tree-level)                                  |
|    - Goldstone separation (3 modes eaten by W^+/-, Z; photon stays |
|      massless)                                                      |
|    - W/Z mass generation (tree-level)                              |
|    - fermion-mass coupling via Yukawas (structural)                 |
|    - radiative stability — AUDIT-tier boundary statement only      |
|    - vacuum metastability — AUDIT-tier boundary statement only     |
|    - certificate table: v, m_H, lambda, Goldstones, photon,        |
|      vacuum status, hierarchy                                       |
|    - C-FF backbone compliance table for the Higgs row              |
|    - tier declaration and downgrade rule                            |
|    - cross-reference index to Paper 2 §8 and Paper 1 Appendix H    |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------+
```

Outside this section (named, routed):

| Outside-scope item | Routed to |
|---|---|
| Compactification-independent Higgs theorem (no Wilson-line origin) | Not claimed — UQFC-10 is explicit that the Higgs *needs* its Wilson-line origin from Paper 1 Appendix H |
| Full radiative Higgs spectrum at all loop orders with the 13D KK content | UQF-9 (§14) + UQF-10 (§15) |
| Electroweak vacuum-decay lifetime (absolute lifetime number) | UQF-9 (§14) — uses the SM RG running of $\lambda(\mu)$ plus 13D KK corrections |
| Hierarchy-problem resolution beyond "protected by Wilson-line origin" | Paper 1 Appendix H — UQFC-10 invokes the protection by interface only |
| Detailed flavor structure (CKM, PMNS, hierarchies, mixing angles) | Paper 1 (flavor sector) — UQFC-10 certifies the *structure* of the Yukawa couplings, not the numerical values |
| Neutrino mass mechanism (Dirac vs Majorana, see-saw) | UQFC-11 §11.7 + Paper 1 Appendix K |

---

## 10.1 Origin of the Higgs mode — Wilson line on $S^1_Y$

The Higgs is *not* postulated as an independent fundamental scalar in the 13D framework. It is derived as a Wilson-line / compactified-scalar mode on the hypercharge interval $S^1_Y$.

The carrier is the electroweak Higgs doublet

$$H \sim (\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2)_{1/2}\ \text{under}\ SU(3)_c \times SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y,$$

with the convention $Q = T_3 + Y$. In the 13D compactification on $S^2 \times S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$, $H$ arises as the zero-mode component of a 5D gauge / scalar field along the hypercharge interval direction:

$$H(x) = \int_{S^1_Y} dy_Y\ Z(y_Y)\ \Phi(x, y_Y),$$

where $\Phi(x, y_Y)$ is the appropriate 5D scalar (Wilson-line component of an extended hypercharge connection, after the $\mathbb Z_2$ projection) and $Z(y_Y)$ is the normalized zero-mode profile selected by the boundary conditions.

**Authority.** The detailed gate certificate for the Wilson-line / Higgs protection — including:

- the precise 13D field whose Wilson-line component descends to $H$,
- the $\mathbb Z_2$ projection rule that produces the doublet structure $(\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2)_{1/2}$,
- the boundary conditions on $S^1_Y$ that select the zero-mode profile $Z(y_Y)$,
- the loop-level protection that keeps the Higgs mass parametrically light,
- the freeze record for this construction —

lives in **Paper 1 Appendix H** ("Wilson-line / Higgs protection certificate"). UQFC-10 invokes Appendix H by interface only and does *not* claim a compactification-independent Higgs theorem. This is the C-FF13 (main-manuscript authority) compliance for the Higgs row.

**Visible witness for UQFC-10 reviewers.** The minimum observable consequence the UQFC-10 row *does* claim is:

- $H$ transforms as $(\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2)_{1/2}$ (Paper 2 §8.5a),
- the SM doublet $H$ is the *only* scalar in the active 13D zero-mode content that couples to $SU(2)_L$ doublets with $Y = 1/2$,
- there is no independent fundamental 4D scalar postulated.

If Paper 1 Appendix H is ever downgraded — e.g., the Wilson-line construction is found to lose its loop-level protection — UQFC-10's UQF-8 row downgrades correspondingly. The downgrade ladder is in §10.10 below.

---

## 10.2 Wilson-line potential and tree-level structure

After dimensional reduction, the 4D effective potential for the doublet $H$ takes the standard Mexican-hat form

$$V(H) = -\mu^2\,H^\dagger H + \lambda\,(H^\dagger H)^2,$$

with $\mu^2 > 0$ and $\lambda > 0$ for electroweak breaking. The signs and the magnitude of $\mu^2$ and $\lambda$ are inputs from the 13D effective theory: $\lambda$ from the dimensional-reduction structure of the Wilson-line action, and $\mu^2$ from the radiative-/orbifold-boundary contributions that generate the negative mass-squared on $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$.

The minimum of $V$ is at $H^\dagger H = \mu^2 / (2\lambda)$, equivalently

$$v^2 = \mu^2 / \lambda,\qquad v \simeq 246~\mathrm{GeV},$$

with $v$ identified with the measured EW VEV. The tree-level Higgs mass is

$$m_h^2 = 2\lambda\,v^2,\qquad m_h \simeq 125~\mathrm{GeV}\implies \lambda \simeq 0.13.$$

UQFC-10 takes $v$ and $m_h$ from observation; the 13D framework provides the *structure* (Wilson-line origin, gauge representation, doublet structure, sign of $\mu^2$) but inherits the numerical values from the SM fit, as Paper 2 §8.5a–§8.5c does at interface level.

---

## 10.3 Vacuum selection

The EW vacuum is the minimum of $V(H)$, conventionally chosen as

$$\langle H\rangle = \frac{1}{\sqrt 2}\begin{pmatrix}0\\v\end{pmatrix},\qquad v = \mu/\sqrt\lambda \simeq 246~\mathrm{GeV}.$$

The choice of vacuum direction in the 2-dimensional complex doublet (a 3-sphere of minima before gauge fixing) is fixed by gauge choice; in unitary gauge the upper component is set to zero and the lower component is real. The *physical* vacuum is gauge-equivalent across this 3-sphere; the gauge-fixing choice is what makes the polarization-bookkeeping table of §10.5 unambiguous.

**Vacuum stability — tree-level statement.** $V(H)$ is bounded below for $\lambda > 0$. The tree-level EW vacuum is stable. Loop corrections to $\lambda$ from the top-Yukawa coupling drive $\lambda(\mu)$ downward at high RG scale; whether the running $\lambda(\mu)$ stays positive up to the cutoff is the load-bearing content of **UQF-9** (§14). UQFC-10 records only the tree-level statement and the explicit deferral.

---

## 10.4 Goldstone separation

The breaking $SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y \to U(1)_{\rm em}$ removes $3$ generators, so the minimal Higgs doublet supplies $3$ Goldstone modes. In the parametrization

$$H(x) = \frac{1}{\sqrt 2}\begin{pmatrix}\phi_1(x) + i\phi_2(x)\\ v + h(x) + i\phi_3(x)\end{pmatrix},$$

the three real fields $\{\phi_1, \phi_2, \phi_3\}$ are the Goldstone modes, and $h(x)$ is the physical Higgs.

**Eaten-Goldstone assignment.** Each Goldstone is absorbed by the longitudinal mode of a broken-symmetry gauge boson:

- $\phi^+ \equiv \tfrac{1}{\sqrt 2}(\phi_1 - i\phi_2)$ → eaten by $W^+_\mu$ (longitudinal polarization),
- $\phi^- \equiv \tfrac{1}{\sqrt 2}(\phi_1 + i\phi_2)$ → eaten by $W^-_\mu$,
- $\phi^0 \equiv \phi_3$ → eaten by $Z^0_\mu$.

The photon $A_\mu$ — the unbroken $U(1)_{\rm em}$ combination — has *no* Goldstone partner and stays massless. This is the joint check with UQFC-9 §9.3 (photon-mass ledger). The photon-stays-massless condition is the visible witness that the breaking pattern is exactly $SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y \to U(1)_{\rm em}$ and not, e.g., $SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y \to \emptyset$.

**Polarization bookkeeping** (cross-reference to UQFC-9 §9.2.4):

| Stage | $W^a, B$ polarizations | Higgs doublet real components | Photon polarizations | Total |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Before EW breaking | $4 \times 2 = 8$ | $4$ ($\phi_1, \phi_2, h, \phi_3$ + the VEV shift) | — | $12$ |
| After EW breaking | $W^\pm: 6$, $Z: 3$ → $9$ (three from Goldstones) | $1$ ($h$) | $2$ | $12$ |

The closure $8 + 4 = 9 + 2 + 1 = 12$ is the visible witness for C-FF5 (no double counting) across the Higgs ↔ gauge-boson partition. UQFC-10 inherits this bookkeeping from Paper 2 §8.5b and UQC-2 §2.4.4 verbatim.

---

## 10.5 $W/Z$ mass generation

From the gauge-covariant kinetic term $|D_\mu H|^2$ evaluated at the vacuum, with

$$D_\mu H = \Big(\partial_\mu - i\tfrac{g}{2}\tau^a W^a_\mu - i\tfrac{g'}{2}\,Y_H\,B_\mu\Big)H,\qquad Y_H = 1/2,$$

the bilinear gauge-boson mass term reads

$$\mathcal L_{\rm mass} = \frac{v^2}{8}\Big[g^2(W^1_\mu W^{1\,\mu} + W^2_\mu W^{2\,\mu}) + (g\,W^3_\mu - g'\,B_\mu)^2\Big].$$

Diagonalizing the $(W^3, B)$ block by the Weinberg rotation,

$$Z_\mu = \cos\theta_W\,W^3_\mu - \sin\theta_W\,B_\mu,\qquad A_\mu = \sin\theta_W\,W^3_\mu + \cos\theta_W\,B_\mu,\qquad \tan\theta_W = g'/g,$$

gives the tree-level mass spectrum:

$$\boxed{\quad m_W = \tfrac12\,g\,v,\qquad m_Z = \tfrac12\,\sqrt{g^2 + g'^2}\,v,\qquad m_\gamma = 0.\quad}$$

The tree-level $\rho$-parameter is

$$\rho \equiv \frac{m_W^2}{m_Z^2 \cos^2\theta_W} = 1,$$

the same identity used by UQFC-9 §9.2.7 as the binding consistency check for the EW interface. Loop corrections to $\rho$ are routed to UQF-13 (§16).

**UQFC-10 cross-check with UQFC-9.** UQFC-9 §9.2.7 reads off the same masses from the broken-EW sector; UQFC-10 §10.5 derives them from the Higgs side via the gauge-covariant kinetic term. The two should agree exactly at tree level — and they do — which is the cross-row consistency check inside Phase 3 of UQFC.

---

## 10.6 Fermion-mass coupling — Yukawa structure

The Yukawa coupling Lagrangian (left-handed Weyl notation matching Paper 2 §7.12a / §8.12) is

$$\mathcal L_Y = -y^e_{ij}\,\bar L_{Li}\,H\,e_{Rj}\ -\ y^d_{ij}\,\bar Q_{Li}\,H\,d_{Rj}\ -\ y^u_{ij}\,\bar Q_{Li}\,\tilde H\,u_{Rj}\ +\ \mathrm{h.c.},$$

with $\tilde H = i\sigma_2 H^*$ and $i,j$ running over the three generations. After EW breaking, $H \to (0, v/\sqrt 2)^\top$ supplies the tree-level fermion masses

$$m_f = \frac{y_f\,v}{\sqrt 2},$$

for each fermion species $f$ (with the $y_f$ matrices diagonalized in the mass basis; the mismatch between the gauge basis and the mass basis supplies CKM / PMNS mixing).

**Boundary statement (what UQFC-10 claims and does not claim).** UQFC-10 certifies that the Yukawa coupling structure is consistent with:

- doublet $H \sim (\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2)_{1/2}$ acting on left-handed quark and lepton doublets,
- right-handed singlets per generation,
- the gauge-invariance pattern of the SM Yukawa terms.

UQFC-10 does *not* claim numerical values for the Yukawa matrices $y^e, y^u, y^d$, does *not* derive the CKM / PMNS angles from first principles, and does *not* close the flavor / hierarchy puzzle. Numerical flavor structure is sourced from Paper 1 (flavor sector) and is not litigated here. The Yukawa numerical fit is part of the precision phenomenology of UQF-13 (§16).

---

## 10.7 Radiative stability — AUDIT-tier boundary statement

The tree-level Higgs sector is described by the parameters $\{v, m_h, \lambda\}$ with $\lambda \simeq 0.13$ at the EW scale. Under RG flow:

- $\lambda(\mu)$ runs downward at high scales due to the top-Yukawa contribution,
- the running can drive $\lambda(\mu_*) = 0$ at some scale $\mu_*$ (instability scale) and turn negative above $\mu_*$ (in the SM, $\mu_* \sim 10^{10}$ GeV in the standard fit),
- the EW vacuum can become metastable (long-lived but not absolutely stable).

**SM-level statement (textbook).** The SM RG analysis, with the measured top-quark and Higgs masses, places the EW vacuum in the *metastable* region: $\lambda(\mu_*) = 0$ at $\mu_* \sim 10^{10}$ GeV, and the calculated tunneling lifetime $\tau_{\rm vac}$ exceeds the age of the Universe by many orders of magnitude. UQFC-10 inherits this status as a baseline.

**13D-specific addition (AUDIT-tier).** The 13D KK corrections — thresholds from the $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$ KK towers crossing the running — can shift $\mu_*$ and $\tau_{\rm vac}$. The shifts depend on:

- the compactification scales $1/R_{K_6}, 1/R_{S^2}, 1/R_{S^1_Y}$,
- the KK content that couples to the Higgs sector (relevant: gauge bosons, top quark, scalar moduli),
- the loop threshold structure at each KK level.

UQFC-10 does *not* compute these shifts. The full radiative-stability audit with the 13D KK content is the load-bearing content of UQF-9 (§14) and UQF-10 (§15). UQFC-10 records the AUDIT-tier status:

| Sub-claim | Tier in UQFC-10 | Routed to |
|---|---|---|
| Tree-level $V(H)$ bounded below for $\lambda > 0$ | **CERTIFICATE** | this section |
| EW vacuum at $\langle H\rangle = (0, v/\sqrt 2)^\top$ | **CERTIFICATE** | this section |
| SM-level $\lambda(\mu)$ running and SM instability-scale estimate | **CERTIFICATE** (textbook SM result, inherited) | this section |
| SM-level metastable-vacuum lifetime estimate ($\tau_{\rm vac} \gg t_{\rm Hubble}$) | **CERTIFICATE** (textbook SM result, inherited) | this section |
| Full radiative stability under SM + 13D KK corrections | **AUDIT / DEFERRED** | UQF-9 (§14) + UQF-10 (§15) |
| Absolute / quantitative vacuum-decay lifetime with 13D corrections | **AUDIT / DEFERRED** | UQF-9 (§14) |
| Hierarchy-problem protection (Wilson-line / compactification origin) | **AUDIT** | Paper 1 Appendix H |

---

## 10.8 Quantization of the physical Higgs scalar

Standard canonical scalar quantization around the EW vacuum:

$$h(x) = \int\frac{d^3 k}{(2\pi)^3\,2\omega_k}\Big[a(k)\,e^{-ik\cdot x} + a^\dagger(k)\,e^{ik\cdot x}\Big],\qquad \omega_k = \sqrt{|\vec k|^2 + m_h^2},$$

with canonical commutator $[a(k), a^\dagger(k')] = (2\pi)^3\,2\omega_k\,\delta^3(k - k')$ and unique vacuum $a(k)|0\rangle = 0$. The Hilbert space is standard scalar Fock space; positivity is manifest. There is no gauge redundancy on the Higgs mode itself; the gauge fixing for the broken gauge bosons handles the eaten Goldstone modes ($\phi_1, \phi_2, \phi_3$) without modifying the Higgs canonical commutators.

**Tier:** **CERTIFICATE-tier** at tree level. The Higgs is a textbook canonical scalar around the EW vacuum.

---

## 10.10 Tier declaration and downgrade ladder

| UQF row | Carrier | Tier (this section) | Downgrade if higher-tier work fails |
|---|---|---|---|
| **UQF-8A** — Tree-level Higgs / Goldstone / vacuum | physical scalar $h$, 3 eaten Goldstones, photon stays massless, $m_W = gv/2$, $m_Z = \sqrt{g^2+g'^2}\,v/2$, $\rho = 1$, $m_h^2 = 2\lambda v^2$, Yukawa coupling structure | **CERTIFICATE** | n/a — this row is closed at the level standard EW QFT supports |
| **UQF-8B** — Wilson-line origin and Appendix H protection | $H$ from $S^1_Y$ Wilson line, doublet structure $(\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2)_{1/2}$, loop-level protection | **AUDIT** (cited via Paper 1 Appendix H) | If Paper 1 Appendix H is ever downgraded — e.g., the Wilson-line protection is lost — UQF-8B drops to *Open / Diagnostic*. UQF-8A retains its CERTIFICATE tier (tree-level statements are independent of the origin question). |
| **UQF-8C** — Full radiative stability + vacuum lifetime under SM + 13D KK | running $\lambda(\mu)$ with 13D KK thresholds; vacuum-decay lifetime with 13D corrections | **DEFERRED** | Routed to UQF-9 (§14) and UQF-10 (§15). If §14 / §15 do not earn their certificates: UQF-8C drops to *Diagnostic*; the SM-level estimate in §10.7 retains CERTIFICATE tier; the 13D-corrected statement is not made. |

**The single load-bearing 13D-specific subtlety for UQFC-10** is **the Wilson-line origin of $H$ on $S^1_Y$**. Every other piece of the row — the canonical scalar quantization, the Goldstone bookkeeping, the $W/Z$ mass generation, the photon staying massless, the Yukawa structure, the tree-level $\rho = 1$ — is standard EW QFT once the doublet $(\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2)_{1/2}$ is granted. The doublet *is granted* by Paper 1 Appendix H's Wilson-line construction, but the construction is the audit surface. This is the row where UQFC-10 most explicitly hands the load to Paper 1 Appendix H rather than re-closing the gate inside UQFC.

---

## 10.11 Certificate-backbone compliance table for the Higgs row

Mirroring the C-FF compliance structure of Paper 2 §8, the Higgs row's compliance with the four-force constraint backbone (C-FF0..C-FF14) is:

| Constraint | Higgs-row provision in UQFC-10 |
|---|---|
| **C-FF0** one-parent-geometry | $H$ descends from $\mathfrak B_{\rm active}$ as a Wilson-line / compactified scalar on $S^1_Y$ inside $\mathfrak B_{\rm active}$; no private parent geometry. (§10.1) |
| **C-FF1** layer discipline | $S^2 \times S^1_Y$ on the $\times$ layer (compact carrier); EW vacuum-admissibility rule, $Q = T_3 + Y$, doublet-structure rule, freeze protocol on the $\oplus$ layer; $\hat H$, $\hat h$, eaten Goldstones, Yukawa operators $y_f \bar\psi_L H \psi_R$ on the $\otimes$ layer. |
| **C-FF2** projection-specification | Routes to Paper 2 §8.0 operational projection $\pi_{\rm weak}$ + §8.5a–§8.5c (Higgs doublet representation, Goldstone counting, tree-level masses) + §8.6 (Higgs-like mode from geometry, with Paper 1 Appendix H authority). |
| **C-FF3** shared matter-bundle | Yukawa couplings act on the same $\mathcal E_{\rm matter}$ assignments fixed by Paper 2 §7.12 / §7.12a / §8.12 — the same matter content used by UQFC-9 (gauge couplings) and UQFC-11 (fermion quantization). |
| **C-FF4** charge-normalization | $H$ carries $Y = 1/2$; $Q = T_3 + Y$ used throughout. The doublet entries $H^+$ and $H^0$ have $Q = 1$ and $Q = 0$, consistent with the standard EW charge assignment. |
| **C-FF5** no-double-counting | The 3 Goldstones are counted as longitudinal $W^\pm, Z$ polarizations in UQFC-9 §9.2.4 and are *not* re-counted as physical scalars here. The physical Higgs $h$ is counted once. The polarization bookkeeping $8 + 4 = 9 + 2 + 1 = 12$ across the EW-breaking step is the visible witness. (§10.4) |
| **C-FF6** gauge-origin | Not directly applicable — $H$ is a scalar, not a gauge boson. The Wilson-line origin on $S^1_Y$ is a *scalar* descended bundle actor, distinct from the gauge-descendant route of UQFC-9. (§10.1) |
| **C-FF7** gravity/gauge separation | $H$ comes from a different compact-factor structure ($S^1_Y$ Wilson-line) than the graviton ($G_{\mu\nu}$ block, UQFC-8) or the gauge bosons ($G_{\mu A}$ mixed block, UQFC-9). No conflation. |
| **C-FF8** QED-downstream-of-EW | The photon-stays-massless joint check is the binding cross-constraint with UQFC-9 §9.3. (§10.4) |
| **C-FF9** regulator/RG compatibility | Tree-level statements only inside UQFC-10. SM RG running of $\lambda(\mu)$ inherited at SM-textbook level; 13D KK threshold corrections routed to §14. |
| **C-FF10** anomaly-compatibility | The Yukawa coupling structure does not introduce a new chiral asymmetry; the per-generation anomaly ledger of Paper 2 §8.5 is unaffected by adding the Higgs doublet (which is non-chiral). |
| **C-FF11** low-energy sanity | $W/Z$ masses (§10.5) match the Fermi-limit constraint via $G_F/\sqrt 2 = g^2/(8 m_W^2) = 1/(\sqrt 2 v^2)$; this is the C-FF11 low-energy sanity check for the EW + Higgs joint sector. |
| **C-FF12** scope-boundary | Routes radiative stability + vacuum lifetime to §14 + §15; routes flavor numerics to Paper 1 + §16; does not use any deferred sector to upgrade UQFC-10's certificate. |
| **C-FF13** main-manuscript authority | Paper 1 Appendix H is invoked explicitly for the Wilson-line origin and the loop-level protection; UQFC-10 does *not* re-close Appendix H. |
| **C-FF14** falsification-path | Falsifiers listed in §10.12 below; Paper 2 §8.15 falsifiers carried over for the EW interface. |

---

## 10.12 Falsifiers

The Higgs row is falsified by any of the following:

1. A vacuum expectation value $\langle H\rangle \neq (0, v/\sqrt 2)^\top$ with $v \neq 246~\mathrm{GeV}$ at the EW scale (would falsify the §10.3 vacuum identification).
2. Failure of the tree-level relation $m_h^2 = 2\lambda v^2$ at $m_h \simeq 125~\mathrm{GeV}, v \simeq 246~\mathrm{GeV}$ — equivalently, $\lambda \neq 0.13$ (would falsify §10.2).
3. Tree-level $\rho \neq 1$ (would falsify §10.5 — joint with UQFC-9 §9.2.7).
4. Fewer or more than $3$ Goldstone modes after $SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y \to U(1)_{\rm em}$ (would falsify the §10.4 breaking-pattern identification).
5. The photon failing to remain massless after EW breaking (would falsify the §10.4 + UQFC-9 §9.3 joint check).
6. The Higgs doublet failing to be $(\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2)_{1/2}$ under $SU(3)_c \times SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$ (would falsify the §10.1 doublet structure and the C-FF4 charge-normalization).
7. The Wilson-line origin of $H$ on $S^1_Y$ being inconsistent with Paper 1 Appendix H (would downgrade UQF-8B to *Diagnostic*; UQF-8A retains CERTIFICATE tier as long as the doublet itself is granted by some other Paper 1 mechanism).
8. The Yukawa coupling structure failing to be gauge-invariant under $SU(3)_c \times SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$ — e.g., a term that requires the wrong $Y$ assignment on a fermion (would falsify §10.6).

Failures 1–6 are direct EW-interface failures and falsify UQF-8A. Failure 7 is the Wilson-line / Appendix H surface (UQF-8B). Failure 8 is a structural Yukawa failure that would also falsify the matter ledger of Paper 2 §8.12.

---

## 10.13 Boundary statement

UQFC-10 *certifies* the tree-level Higgs / Goldstone / vacuum sector at UQF-8A tier:

- physical Higgs scalar $h$ with one polarization, canonical scalar quantization around the EW vacuum,
- three Goldstone modes exactly eaten by $W^\pm$ and $Z$,
- photon stays massless (joint with UQFC-9 §9.3),
- tree-level masses $m_W = gv/2$, $m_Z = \sqrt{g^2+g'^2}\,v/2$, $m_\gamma = 0$, $\rho = 1$,
- EW vacuum at $\langle H\rangle = (0, v/\sqrt 2)^\top$ with $v \simeq 246~\mathrm{GeV}$,
- tree-level Higgs self-coupling $\lambda \simeq 0.13$ from $m_h^2 = 2\lambda v^2$,
- Yukawa coupling structure compatible with the per-generation matter ledger,
- SM-level metastable-vacuum status (with $\tau_{\rm vac} \gg t_{\rm Hubble}$) inherited as a baseline.

UQFC-10 records the AUDIT-tier statement for UQF-8B:

- $H$ originates as a Wilson-line / compactified scalar on $S^1_Y$,
- the doublet structure $(\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2)_{1/2}$ is inherited from the Paper 1 Appendix H Wilson-line / Higgs protection certificate,
- the loop-level hierarchy-problem protection lives in Appendix H and is invoked by interface only.

UQFC-10 does *not* claim:

- a compactification-independent Higgs theorem,
- full radiative stability under SM + 13D KK corrections at all loop orders,
- the quantitative vacuum-decay lifetime with 13D corrections,
- the numerical Yukawa values, CKM / PMNS angles, or hierarchies,
- the neutrino mass mechanism (which is the joint content of UQFC-11 §11.7 + Paper 1 Appendix K).

The radiative-stability + vacuum-lifetime content is routed to **UQF-9** (§14) and **UQF-10** (§15). The Wilson-line origin is sourced from **Paper 1 Appendix H** by interface only.

---

| §10.9 certificate table | §8.5a–§8.5c, §8.12 | Appendix H | UQC-2 §2.6 (synthesizes) |
| §10.11 C-FF compliance | C-FF0..C-FF14 (Paper 2 §2.6) | — | UQC-2 §2.7 (mapped to Higgs row) |
| §10.12 falsifiers | §8.15 (EW falsifiers) | — | UQC-2 §2.6.8 boundary |

## 11.0 Purpose and boundary

The fermion row of the UQF certificate stack is **UQF-7**:

> *Fermion quantization.* Quantize the Standard-Model chiral matter — three generations of left-handed Weyl spinors $\{Q_L, u^c_L, d^c_L, L_L, e^c_L\}$ — on the 13D active branch, with (a) correct chirality after compactification (left-handed only, no mirror fermions), (b) correct fermionic statistics (anti-commuting, not bosonic), (c) anomaly leak prevention (the per-generation anomaly ledger inherited from Paper 2 §8.5 and Paper 1's main anomaly tables remains closed under quantization), (d) three families from the $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ spin-c index, (e) Yukawa coupling structure to the Higgs Wilson line of UQFC-10, and (f) neutrino-sector boundary statement (Dirac vs Majorana; right-handed neutrinos in $\mathcal E_{\rm matter}$; mass mechanism flagged AUDIT-tier with the Paper 1 Appendix K route).

UQF-7 is structurally the most "matter-side" of the four Phase-3 carrier certificates. The previous three rows (UQFC-8 graviton, UQFC-9 gauge bosons, UQFC-10 Higgs) all dealt with *bosonic* excitations of the geometry. UQFC-11 deals with the fermionic content — the matter bundle $\mathcal E_{\rm matter}$ — and the question is whether the standard chiral-fermion quantization route (anti-commuting Dirac / Weyl spinors with the spin-statistics theorem) is *compatible* with the 13D geometric origin of those fermions.

The answer is yes, at the level standard QFT supports after Paper 2 §8 (chirality routing through the $S^2$ spin-cover and the $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ boundary parity) and Paper 2 §7.4 (three families from the $K_6$ spin-c index) are accepted. UQFC-11 makes this compatibility explicit and writes it as a certificate row.

The single load-bearing 13D-specific subtlety for UQFC-11 is the **chirality survival under compactification**: the 13D parent spinor decomposes after compactification into 4D left-handed *and* right-handed pieces, and the $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ boundary parity must project out the right-handed mirrors to leave only the SM left-handed chiral content. This is the "no mirror fermions" certificate, and it is the binding consistency check for UQF-7. Without this projection, the 4D theory would contain unwanted mirror-doublet states, the anomaly ledger would not close, and parity violation would not be structural.

**Scope and outside-scope.**

## 11.1 Chiral matter from 13D — geometric origin

The Standard-Model matter content per generation, in left-handed Weyl notation, is the five-multiplet:

$$Q_L: (\mathbf 3, \mathbf 2)_{1/6},\qquad u^c_L: (\bar{\mathbf 3}, \mathbf 1)_{-2/3},\qquad d^c_L: (\bar{\mathbf 3}, \mathbf 1)_{1/3},$$
$$L_L: (\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2)_{-1/2},\qquad e^c_L: (\mathbf 1, \mathbf 1)_{1}.$$

This is the selected five-bundle SM table of Paper 2 §8.4, with $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ supplying color triplets, the $S^2$ spin-cover supplying $SU(2)_L$ doublets, and $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ supplying the hypercharge labels.

### 11.1.1 13D parent spinor

The 13D parent fermion is a spinor of the 13D Lorentz group $\mathrm{Spin}(1,12)$ — equivalently, a section of an appropriate spinor bundle over the active 13D background $M_{13} = \mathcal M_4 \times K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$. The spinor's degrees of freedom split, after compactification on $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$, into 4D Weyl components organized by:

- 4D Lorentz $\mathrm{Spin}(1,3) = SL(2,\mathbb C)$ — supplies the 4D Weyl chirality label (left vs right);
- internal $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ — supplies the color representation through the spin-c index on the flag manifold;
- internal $S^2$ — supplies the $SU(2)_L$ doublet structure via the standard spin cover;
- internal $S^1_Y / \mathbb Z_2$ — supplies the hypercharge label and the $\mathbb Z_2$ boundary parity that projects out the mirror partner.

### 11.1.2 4D Weyl chirality from compactification

A 4D Weyl spinor $\psi_L(x)$ is sourced from the 13D parent spinor $\Psi(x, y)$ by

$$\psi_L(x) = \int_X d^9 y\,\sqrt{g_X(y)}\,\eta_L(y)\,\Psi(x, y),$$

with $\eta_L(y)$ the zero-mode profile on $X = K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y$ that (a) is left-handed under 4D Lorentz, (b) carries the chosen color / weak-isospin / hypercharge labels, and (c) survives the $\mathbb Z_2$ boundary projection on $S^1_Y$.

The 4D Lagrangian for the surviving Weyl mode is the standard

$$\mathcal L_{\rm Weyl} = i\,\psi_L^\dagger\,\bar\sigma^\mu\,\partial_\mu\,\psi_L,$$

plus gauge-covariantization (next subsection). The dimensional reduction is the standard KK reduction applied to a parent spinor on a compact internal space, with the standard Atiyah–Singer index theorem governing the zero-mode count on each compact factor.

### 11.1.3 Gauge-covariant kinetic term

The kinetic term for each 4D Weyl multiplet, with the appropriate gauge connections inserted, is

$$\mathcal L_{\rm fermion}^{(\rm 4D)} = \sum_{f \in \{Q_L, u^c_L, d^c_L, L_L, e^c_L\}} i\,\bar f\,\gamma^\mu\,D_\mu\,f,$$

with $D_\mu$ assembled from the gluon, $W^a$, and $B$ gauge connections of UQFC-9 acting on the appropriate representations:

$$D_\mu Q_L = (\partial_\mu - i g_s A^a_\mu T^a - i\tfrac{g}{2}\tau^b W^b_\mu - i\tfrac{g'}{2}\cdot\tfrac{1}{6}\,B_\mu)\,Q_L,$$

and analogously for $u^c_L, d^c_L, L_L, e^c_L$ with their representation-appropriate generators and hypercharges. The covariant derivative reuses the gauge connections of UQFC-9 verbatim; no new gauge content is introduced here.

---

## 11.2 No mirror fermions — $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ boundary parity

The "no mirror fermions" certificate is the binding 13D-specific consistency check for UQFC-11.

**Statement.** After compactification on $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$, the 4D Weyl content is the SM five-multiplet $\{Q_L, u^c_L, d^c_L, L_L, e^c_L\}$ per generation, with *no* right-handed partners $\{Q_R, u^c_R, d^c_R, L_R, e^c_R\}$ surviving as physical zero modes. The right-handed partners are projected out by the $\mathbb Z_2$ boundary parity on $S^1_Y$.

### 11.2.1 The $\mathbb Z_2$ projection rule

The interval $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ identifies points $\theta \sim -\theta$ on the circle (Paper 2 §8.3, §8.4). The action on the 13D parent spinor $\Psi$ takes the form

$$\mathbb Z_2:\quad \Psi(x, y_Y) \to P_Y\,\Psi(x, -y_Y),$$

with $P_Y$ a chirality / parity projector on the spinor indices. The projector is chosen (as recorded in Paper 1's compactification gate certificates) such that:

- left-handed 4D Weyl modes with the chosen $Y$ assignments survive,
- right-handed 4D Weyl modes with the same $Y$ assignments are projected out,
- and the surviving zero-mode content is exactly the SM five-multiplet per generation.

### 11.2.2 Visible witness — parity violation is structural

If $P_Y$ failed — e.g., if the $\mathbb Z_2$ projection let through both left- and right-handed partners — the 4D theory would be vector-like in $SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$ at each generation. The observed parity violation of the weak interaction would *not* be structural; it would require an additional fine-tuning to suppress the right-handed couplings.

UQFC-11's "no mirror fermions" certificate asserts that the $\mathbb Z_2$ projection on $S^1_Y$ is the structural mechanism that makes parity violation automatic. This is the **C-FF11 low-energy sanity target** for the fermion row: the absence of right-handed weak doublets at the 4D zero-mode level.

### 11.2.3 Right-handed singlets and the matter bundle

The "no mirror fermions" certificate does *not* exclude *singlet* right-handed fermions — in particular, right-handed neutrinos $\nu_R$ (singlet under $SU(2)_L$) — from the matter bundle $\mathcal E_{\rm matter}$. The boundary projection only forbids *partners* to the surviving left-handed doublets. Singlet right-handed states (color singlets, weak singlets) can in principle survive if the $\mathbb Z_2$ projection allows them. This is the route through which a right-handed neutrino enters in §11.7 below; its quantization is well-defined, but its mass-generation mechanism (Dirac vs Majorana) is the AUDIT-tier flag.

### 11.2.4 Falsification of the no-mirror certificate

A surviving right-handed $SU(2)_L$ doublet (e.g., $Q_R: (\mathbf 3, \mathbf 2)_{1/6}$) at the 4D zero-mode level would falsify UQFC-11's no-mirror certificate. The visible signature would be vector-like quark or lepton multiplets accessible at low energy, or non-$V$–$A$ structure in the charged-current sector at leading order. Neither is observed.

---

## 11.3 Wrong-statistics exclusion

A separate but related consistency check is the **wrong-statistics exclusion**: the 4D descendants of a 13D spinor must obey Fermi-Dirac statistics (anti-commuting operators, $\{\psi(x), \psi(y)\} =$ standard), not Bose-Einstein statistics. This is the spin-statistics theorem applied to the 13D parent and transmitted to the 4D descendants.

### 11.3.1 Spin-statistics on the 13D parent

The 13D parent spinor $\Psi$ has half-integer spin under $\mathrm{Spin}(1,12)$ and is quantized as an anti-commuting field by the standard spin-statistics theorem. The 13D anti-commutator

$$\{\Psi_\alpha(X), \bar\Psi_\beta(X')\}_+ = i (\gamma^M)_{\alpha\beta}\,\partial_M\,\Delta(X-X')$$

is the standard fermionic algebra on $M_{13}$.

### 11.3.2 Transmission to 4D Weyl descendants

After KK reduction, the zero-mode profile $\eta_L(y)$ is a c-number on the compact internal space; it does not modify the anti-commutator structure of $\Psi$. The induced 4D anti-commutator for the Weyl descendant is

$$\{\psi_L(x), \psi_L^\dagger(x')\}_+ = i\,\sigma^\mu\,\partial_\mu\,\Delta_4(x - x')\,\Big(\int_X d^9 y\,\sqrt{g_X}\,|\eta_L(y)|^2\Big),$$

with the bracketed normalization factor canonically set to unity. The 4D Weyl operator $\psi_L(x)$ is thus a standard anti-commuting field; it is *not* a bosonic field. This is the wrong-statistics exclusion: a 13D spinor parent does not produce a bosonic 4D descendant, and the SM chiral fermions inherit the standard fermionic statistics.

### 11.3.3 Why this is non-trivial

The wrong-statistics exclusion sounds tautological, but it is the load-bearing reason that the SM chiral fermions can be quantized at all. If the 13D framework forced (e.g., via an exotic compactification rule or a spin-statistics-violating boundary condition) the 4D Weyl descendants to anti-commute on some compact-factor components and commute on others, the 4D theory would not have a well-defined Hilbert space — gauge-invariant operators would mix bosonic and fermionic statistics, the spin-statistics theorem would fail at the 4D level, and the SM matter sector would not quantize consistently.

UQFC-11 certifies that the standard 13D spinor → 4D Weyl reduction *preserves* the spin-statistics theorem at both levels.

---

## 11.4 Anomaly-leak prevention

The Standard-Model per-generation anomaly cancellation is the load-bearing consistency check for the chiral matter sector. UQFC-11 reuses, without modification, the anomaly ledger of Paper 2 §8.5 (electroweak anomaly audit) and Paper 1's main anomaly tables.

### 11.4.1 Per-generation anomaly ledger (Paper 2 §8.5)

The per-generation Weyl content $(\mathbf 3, \mathbf 2)_{1/6} \oplus (\bar{\mathbf 3}, \mathbf 1)_{-2/3} \oplus (\bar{\mathbf 3}, \mathbf 1)_{1/3} \oplus (\mathbf 1, \mathbf 2)_{-1/2} \oplus (\mathbf 1, \mathbf 1)_{1}$ supplies the following anomaly coefficients, all of which vanish:

$$A_{SU(3)^3} = 0,\qquad A_{SU(3)^2 U(1)_Y} = 0,\qquad A_{SU(2)^2 U(1)_Y} = 0,$$
$$A_{U(1)_Y^3} = 0,\qquad A_{\mathrm{grav}^2 U(1)_Y} = 0.$$

For $SU(2)^2 U(1)$, one generation gives

$$3 \cdot Y(Q_L) + 1 \cdot Y(L_L) = 3 \cdot \tfrac{1}{6} - \tfrac{1}{2} = 0,$$

the minimal visible witness for the hypercharge normalization. The global $SU(2)$ Witten anomaly also vanishes because the total number of left-handed $SU(2)$ doublets per generation is even (4 quark doublets from the color triplet $Q_L$ + 1 lepton doublet $L_L$ = 5, but only the left-handed doublets count in the parity ledger; the global anomaly cancels per-generation by the standard SM count).

### 11.4.2 Quantization preserves the anomaly closure

UQFC-11 certifies that the standard 4D chiral-fermion quantization route preserves these anomaly cancellations. The argument is:

1. The 4D anomaly coefficients are determined by the *chiral content* — i.e., by which 4D Weyl multiplets survive compactification.
2. The 13D → 4D reduction selects exactly the SM five-multiplet per generation (via the §11.1, §11.2 chirality + no-mirror certificate).
3. Therefore the 4D anomaly coefficients are exactly the SM per-generation values, which all vanish.
4. The quantization measure (the standard chiral fermion path-integral measure, regularized via dimensional or Pauli–Villars regularization with the appropriate spectator-fermion content) does not introduce additional anomalies.

This is the "anomaly leak prevention" certificate. The 13D parent does not introduce additional anomaly contributions beyond the standard SM per-generation ledger.

### 11.4.3 Authority

Paper 1's main anomaly tables (in the GUT manuscript) record the per-generation closure with frozen artifact and freeze hash. UQFC-11 invokes Paper 1's anomaly tables by interface only and does *not* re-close them. C-FF10 (anomaly compatibility) and C-FF13 (main-manuscript authority) compliance is satisfied by this routing.

---

## 11.5 Three families from $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ spin-c index

Paper 2 §7.4 fixes the three-generation structure of the SM matter content as a consequence of the $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ spin-c index. The index theorem on the flag manifold $K_6$ acting on the chosen matter bundle produces three families at factor-level.

### 11.5.1 Spin-c index on $K_6$

The flag manifold $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$ is a 6-dimensional Kähler manifold. With the chosen spin-c structure and the chosen line bundles (selected by the active 13D theory in Paper 1's branch-selection ledger), the Atiyah–Singer spin-c index theorem applied to the Dirac operator on $K_6$ gives

$$\mathrm{ind}\,D_{K_6} = 3,$$

producing three zero-mode multiplets, identified with three families of SM matter. The detailed bundle choice and the index calculation live in Paper 1; UQFC-11 invokes Paper 1's spin-c index calculation as the freeze record. **Governing corpus authority (§11.2, EXTERNAL):** this index count is a *load-bearing closed* result in TOE_FINAL v6 §I/§II — the APS zero-mode inventory is $(+3, 0)$, twice-derived (ASP +3 and the BWB scan with $|\mathrm{index}|=3$ confirmed against the frozen row), and the corpus reads the three families as *the spin-structure witness* (zero modes exist iff the KK towers are integer-moded iff the fermion spin structure is PERIODIC). The classical chiral count is therefore **closed** and is not UQF-7's open item; UQFC-11 inherits it as the classical input (see §11.5.4 and the open-item narrowing in the gate card).

### 11.5.2 No-mirror lift and family structure

The three families surviving the $K_6$ index theorem are then *each* subject to the $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ no-mirror projection of §11.2. The result is three generations of left-handed-only SM matter, each with the five-multiplet content $\{Q_L, u^c_L, d^c_L, L_L, e^c_L\}$.

### 11.5.3 Visible witness — three generations, not more or fewer

The visible witness is that the observed SM has exactly three generations with the per-generation content listed above. UQFC-11 inherits this count from Paper 2 §7.4 / Paper 1; it does *not* re-derive the family-number-three statement here. The "three families" certificate is sourced authority, not new content.

### 11.5.4 What if the count failed?

If the $K_6$ spin-c index produced a different number — e.g., $\mathrm{ind}\,D_{K_6} = 2$ or $\mathrm{ind}\,D_{K_6} = 4$ — UQFC-11 would have to be downgraded along with Paper 2 §7.4 and Paper 1's spin-c calculation. The downgrade ladder is: UQF-7's family-count sub-claim drops to *Diagnostic*; the per-family quantization, no-mirror, and anomaly-leak-prevention certificates of §11.1–§11.4 retain their CERTIFICATE tier (they are per-generation statements, valid for whatever family count survives).

**Where UQF-7's AUDIT obligation actually sits (open-item narrowing; §11.2).** It is worth stating precisely, because the corpus reconciliation sharpens it. The *classical* chiral inventory — the index count $\mathrm{ind}\,D_{K_6}=3$, the no-mirror structure at the zero-mode level (§11.2), and the spin-statistics transmission (§11.3) — is **closed** at the level the corpus banks it (TOE_FINAL v6 APS $(+3,0)$, EXTERNAL; twice-derived). The reason UQF-7 nonetheless sits at AUDIT rather than CERTIFICATE in the §3.3 stack is **not** that the family count is in doubt; it is the residual **quantum-descent** question: whether the full 4D BV-BRST quantization of the 13D→4D descent — including KK-tower loops, the $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ quotient measure, and the boundary-parity projector at the quantum level — introduces a *light mirror* not present in the classical zero-mode count. That is the narrow open obligation this paper owns; it is a statement about the quantized descent measure, not about the index theorem, and the corpus's classical APS certificate does not by itself discharge it. (This is the same split the campaign reconciliation records: index count closed, quantum descent open.)

---

## 11.6 Yukawa couplings to the Higgs Wilson line

The quark-mass and lepton-mass coupling structure is the Yukawa Lagrangian of UQFC-10 §10.6:

$$\mathcal L_Y = -y^e_{ij}\,\bar L_{Li}\,H\,e_{Rj} - y^d_{ij}\,\bar Q_{Li}\,H\,d_{Rj} - y^u_{ij}\,\bar Q_{Li}\,\tilde H\,u_{Rj} + \mathrm{h.c.},$$

with $\tilde H = i\sigma_2 H^*$, $i,j$ running over the three generations, and the right-handed singlet fields $e_R \equiv (e^c_L)^c$, $d_R \equiv (d^c_L)^c$, $u_R \equiv (u^c_L)^c$ identified with the charge conjugates of the left-handed singlet entries in the SM five-multiplet.

### 11.6.1 Structural statement

UQFC-11 certifies the *structure* of the Yukawa couplings:

- gauge invariance under $SU(3)_c \times SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$,
- correct hypercharge assignment ($Y_H = 1/2$ for $H$, $Y_{\tilde H} = -1/2$ for $\tilde H$),
- correct color contraction ($Q_L: \mathbf 3$, $u^c_L, d^c_L: \bar{\mathbf 3}$),
- correct $SU(2)_L$ contraction ($\bar L_L H$ is a singlet, $\bar Q_L H$ is a $\bar{\mathbf 3}$, $\bar Q_L \tilde H$ is a $\bar{\mathbf 3}$).

The Yukawa terms are the unique dimension-4 gauge-invariant couplings between the SM five-multiplet and the Higgs doublet.

### 11.6.2 After EW breaking

After EW breaking, $\langle H\rangle = (0, v/\sqrt 2)^\top$ supplies the tree-level fermion masses

$$m_f = \frac{y_f\,v}{\sqrt 2},$$

for each species. The Yukawa matrices $y^e, y^u, y^d$ are diagonalized in the mass basis; the mismatch between the gauge basis and the mass basis supplies the CKM (quarks) and PMNS (leptons) mixing.

### 11.6.3 What is *not* claimed

UQFC-11 does *not* claim:

- numerical values for the Yukawa matrices,
- the CKM / PMNS angle values,
- a first-principles derivation of the flavor hierarchy ($m_t \gg m_b \gg m_c \gg \ldots$),
- the resolution of the flavor puzzle.

Numerical flavor structure is routed to Paper 1 (flavor sector) and to §16 (UQF-13). UQFC-11 closes only the structural / consistency layer.

---

## 11.7 Neutrino sector — Dirac vs Majorana boundary statement

The neutrino sector is the AUDIT-tier flag inside UQFC-11. The reason is that the SM five-multiplet (the per-generation content of §11.1) does *not* include a right-handed neutrino singlet $\nu_R$ as a fundamental zero mode. Whether neutrino masses are Dirac (requiring a $\nu_R$ in the matter bundle) or Majorana (built from $\nu_L$ alone with lepton-number violation) is a load-bearing question for the matter ledger.

### 11.7.1 Three options at the matter-bundle level

The 13D framework can accommodate three logically distinct neutrino-mass mechanisms:

| Option | $\nu_R$ in $\mathcal E_{\rm matter}$? | Mass type | Coupling | Lepton number |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| (i) Dirac | Yes — added as a singlet zero mode | Dirac mass $m^D \bar\nu_L H \nu_R$ | Tiny Yukawa $y_\nu \sim 10^{-12}$ | Conserved |
| (ii) Majorana from $\nu_L$ only | No | Majorana mass via dim-5 Weinberg operator $\frac{(L_L H)^2}{\Lambda}$ | Suppressed by high scale $\Lambda$ | Violated by 2 units |
| (iii) See-saw (Dirac + Majorana on $\nu_R$) | Yes, with a large Majorana mass $M_R$ for $\nu_R$ | Light Majorana on $\nu_L$ via see-saw $m_\nu \sim m^D_\nu{}^2 / M_R$ | Yukawa $\sim O(1)$, $M_R$ at high scale | Violated by 2 units via $\nu_R$ Majorana |

Each option is consistent with the SM matter content and with the §11.4 anomaly ledger ($\nu_R$ is a singlet under $SU(3)_c \times SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$ with $Y = 0$, so adding it does not change any anomaly coefficient). The choice between (i), (ii), (iii) is determined by *Paper 1 Appendix K* (lepton / neutrino sector) and the active matter-bundle selection.

### 11.7.2 What UQFC-11 certifies

UQFC-11 certifies:

- the quantization of $\nu_L$ as a standard chiral Weyl spinor (covered by §11.1 + §11.3),
- if $\nu_R$ is in the matter bundle, the quantization of $\nu_R$ as a chiral singlet Weyl spinor (the no-mirror certificate of §11.2 allows singlet right-handed states),
- the structural consistency of any of options (i), (ii), (iii) with the §11.4 anomaly closure,
- the lepton-number-violation status: conserved (option (i)) or violated by 2 units (options (ii) and (iii)).

UQFC-11 does *not* certify which option is realized in the 13D framework. The choice is the load-bearing content of Paper 1 Appendix K.

### 11.7.3 Boundary

The neutrino-mass mechanism, the values of the active neutrino masses, the PMNS mixing angles, the CP-violating phase, and the see-saw scale $M_R$ (if option (iii) is realized) are *all* outside the scope of UQFC-11. They are routed to:

- Paper 1 Appendix K — for the structural mechanism and the matter-bundle selection;
- §16 (UQF-13, precision phenomenology) — for the numerical fit to the observed $\Delta m^2_{ij}$ and mixing angles.

UQFC-11 status for the neutrino row is **AUDIT-tier** with the named research path.

---

## 11.8 Certificate table — per family per chirality

| Field | $SU(3)_c$ | $SU(2)_L$ | $U(1)_Y$ | $Q = T_3 + Y$ | Chirality | Source | Tier |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| $Q_L$ (per gen) | $\mathbf 3$ | $\mathbf 2$ | $+1/6$ | $u: +2/3,\ d: -1/3$ | L | $K_6$ + $S^2$ doublet + $S^1_Y$ projection | **CERTIFICATE** |
| $u^c_L$ (per gen) | $\bar{\mathbf 3}$ | $\mathbf 1$ | $-2/3$ | $-2/3$ | L (charge conj of $u_R$) | $K_6$ + $S^2$ singlet + $S^1_Y$ projection | **CERTIFICATE** |
| $d^c_L$ (per gen) | $\bar{\mathbf 3}$ | $\mathbf 1$ | $+1/3$ | $+1/3$ | L (charge conj of $d_R$) | $K_6$ + $S^2$ singlet + $S^1_Y$ projection | **CERTIFICATE** |
| $L_L$ (per gen) | $\mathbf 1$ | $\mathbf 2$ | $-1/2$ | $\nu: 0,\ e: -1$ | L | color singlet + $S^2$ doublet + $S^1_Y$ projection | **CERTIFICATE** |
| $e^c_L$ (per gen) | $\mathbf 1$ | $\mathbf 1$ | $+1$ | $+1$ | L (charge conj of $e_R$) | color singlet + $S^2$ singlet + $S^1_Y$ projection | **CERTIFICATE** |
| $\nu^c_L \equiv \nu_R$ charge-conjugate (per gen, *if present*) | $\mathbf 1$ | $\mathbf 1$ | $0$ | $0$ | L (charge conj of $\nu_R$) | singlet under everything | **AUDIT** (presence / mechanism depends on Paper 1 Appendix K) |
| Mirror $Q_R, u_R, d_R, L_R, e_R$ partners | — | — | — | — | R — *forbidden as zero mode* | projected out by $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ boundary parity | **CERTIFICATE — projected out** |

Total per generation: $3 \cdot 2 + \bar 3 + \bar 3 + 2 + 1 = 15$ left-handed Weyl states (the standard SM count); with $\nu_R$ added, 16 states; with no $\nu_R$ and Majorana mass via Weinberg dim-5 operator, still 15.

The mirror row is the visible witness for the no-mirror certificate of §11.2: it explicitly records that the right-handed partners exist *as 13D spinor components* but do *not* survive as 4D zero modes.

Mirroring the C-FF compliance structure of Paper 2 §7 and §8, the fermion row's compliance with the four-force constraint backbone (C-FF0..C-FF14) is:

| **C-FF1** layer discipline | $K_6, S^2, S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ on the $\times$ layer; chirality/parity rules, $\mathbb Z_2$ projection, $Q = T_3 + Y$ rule, freeze protocol on the $\oplus$ layer; 4D Weyl operators $\{Q_L, u^c_L, d^c_L, L_L, e^c_L\}$ on the $\otimes$ layer. |

| **C-FF5** no-double-counting | The 4D Weyl zero modes are counted once per generation; the mirror states are explicitly projected out (not double-counted as additional matter). The right-handed singlets ($u^c_L, d^c_L, e^c_L$) are counted as charge-conjugates of the right-handed entries — *not* as additional states beyond the five-multiplet. |

| **C-FF7** gravity/gauge separation | The fermion multiplets live in $\mathcal E_{\rm matter}$ (a matter bundle), separate from the metric block ($G_{\mu\nu}$, UQFC-8) and the gauge bundle ($\mathcal E_{\rm gauge}$, UQFC-9). |
| **C-FF8** QED-downstream-of-EW | The electric charges of the fermions are read off via $Q = T_3 + Y$ after EW breaking; the assignment is downstream of the EW interface. (§11.8) |
| **C-FF9** regulator/RG compatibility | Standard chiral-fermion regularization (dimensional or Pauli–Villars with spectator-fermion content); no cross-sector RG comparison is upgraded by UQFC-11. |
| **C-FF10** anomaly-compatibility | Per-generation anomaly ledger inherited from Paper 2 §8.5 and Paper 1's main anomaly tables; UQFC-11 does *not* reopen any anomaly closure. (§11.4) |
| **C-FF11** low-energy sanity | Structural parity violation (§11.2) is the low-energy sanity target — no right-handed weak doublets at the 4D zero-mode level, matching the observed $V-A$ structure. |
| **C-FF12** scope-boundary | Routes flavor numerics to Paper 1 + §16; routes neutrino-mass mechanism to Paper 1 Appendix K; routes proton-decay numerics to Paper 1 (proton safety). UQFC-11 does *not* use these deferred sectors to upgrade the row. |
| **C-FF13** main-manuscript authority | Paper 1 main anomaly tables, Paper 1 $K_6$ spin-c index for family count, Paper 1 Appendix K for neutrino sector — all invoked by interface only. |
| **C-FF14** falsification-path | Falsifiers listed in §11.11 below. |

|---|---|---|---|
