## 16.0 Scope statement and tier discipline

This section discharges UQF-13 of the gate stack defined in §3 of this
paper: a *global likelihood against observed force-sector data* for the
four force interfaces certified by Paper 2 (the C-FF0..C-FF14 backbone)
and quantized by §§5–15 of the present paper (UQF-1 through UQF-12).

The section is **two-tier**, and the tier discipline is load-bearing.
A reader who collapses the two tiers will read this section incorrectly,
and the four phrases identified in §0 ("interface claim", "main-manuscript
certificate", "positivity certificate / UV-completion certificate",
"diagnostic / illustrative") will not localize the right failures.

**Tier 1 — framework structure (CERTIFICATE-TIER).** The 13D theory must
expose a *defined and complete* set of force-sector precision-physics
outputs against which the precision-Standard-Model community can test
it. The present section locks that observable list, names the
computation that produces each prediction, names the data set that
constrains it, names the external tool or partner most likely to perform
the actual calculation, and declares the pass/fail rule for each row.
This infrastructural specification is closed at certificate-tier; it
does not depend on numerical work not yet done, because *it is the
specification of what numerical work has to be done*.

**Tier 2 — actual prediction values (AUDIT-TIER).** Numerical predictions
for the observables enumerated in Tier 1 — full electroweak precision
fits with the 13D operator basis, full CKM and PMNS uncertainty bands
under the Article-A §4 fermion-sector machinery, branching ratios for
rare flavor-changing decays under the constraint-selected matter
content, proton-lifetime per channel under the relevant heavy-state
spectrum, gravitational-test parameters in the recovered Einstein limit,
KK threshold spectrum at the locked volume-modulus point — require
physics work that the present paper does not perform. Each Tier-1 row
carries an explicit *computation requirement* field; the numerical
values themselves are out of scope here. Tier 2 is *named*, not
*computed*, in this section.

This is direct re-statement of UQC-8.0's tier discipline. The
re-statement is deliberate: this section is the force-sector restriction
of UQC-8, with cosmology, dark-sector, and baryogenesis rows removed
per the hard claim boundary of UQFC-1 and per the build hierarchy of
the §HANDOFF (Paper 3 covers force-sector quantum completion only;
Paper 4 covers cosmology, dark, baryogenesis, initial conditions). The
UQC-8 framework rows are inherited without modification; the rows that
do not pertain to the force-sector scope of this paper are excluded by
the same hard boundary that excludes them from the rest of UQFC.

### 16.0.1 What this section does not do

- It does not publish any new numerical fit for the CKM matrix, the
  PMNS matrix, the electroweak oblique parameters, the proton lifetime
  per channel, the branching ratios of rare flavor-changing decays, or
  any beyond-Standard-Model predicted state. Every such numerical
  prediction is the output of a downstream calculation pipeline named
  in §16.2 and is left to that pipeline under Chris's physics
  direction.
- It does not modify Paper 2's §2.2 boundary, which explicitly excludes
  *"all precision phenomenology (full CKM/PMNS fits, full electroweak
  precision observables, full flavor anomalies)"* from claimed
  deliverables of the interface paper. The present section is the
  proper venue that the §2.2 exclusion defers to for the force-sector
  precision specification.
- It does not re-open any frozen artifact, edit any gate certificate,
  invoke any companion section as authority for the main manuscript,
  or upgrade the BG-10 baryogenesis posture from *Open / Diagnostic*
  to any closed status.
- It does not assert that the 13D constraint machinery has *already
  produced* a full precision prediction sweep for the force sectors.
  What it asserts is that the machinery is *structurally* capable of
  producing one and that this section locks the specification of what
  that sweep must contain at force-sector tier.

### 16.0.2 Anti-fitting discipline (inherited from Paper 1)

The status-preservation invariant the section operates under is the
project-wide rule: *when audits find gaps, remediation = do the physics
to keep the status; never downgrade*. The companion rule for precision
predictions is the project-wide anti-fitting discipline: numerical
predictions are produced by the Article-A §4 fermion-sector pipeline
and by the §6.4 Kaluza-Klein quantization at the locked volume-modulus
point of §6.9.3a, *not* by tuning free parameters against the
constraint data set. The 13D theory's free-parameter count is the
Article-A nine-parameter count; the constraint-selection pipeline
inherits the same anti-fitting discipline, and no row of the §16.2
table is permitted to introduce a new free parameter that was not in
the locked nine.

This discipline is the precision-side analogue of the C-FF12
scope-boundary constraint of Paper 2: the precision section may not
silently grow the parameter count to absorb a tension. Tensions are
*data*, not *failures*; a row-level tension at $\geq 3\sigma$
downgrades the row to *Open / Diagnostic* and triggers either a
§6.10-style correction-ledger entry or a reopening of the relevant
Article-A / Paper-2 ingredient. The framework-tier structure of the
present section does not downgrade because a Tier-2 row falsifies; the
framework specifies *what has to be true of the prediction surface*,
and a falsification is data input *to* the surface, not data input
*against* the surface's specification.

---

## 16.1 The force-sector precision-observable layer (Tier-1 specification)

Paper 2's §2.2 exclusion does not mean the 13D theory has no
precision-physics commitments in the force sectors. It means that
*Paper 2 itself* is not the venue in which those commitments are
computed. The present section is that venue's *specification* — the
list of force-sector precision observables that the 13D theory must,
in principle, predict, with the data sets and external tools against
which each must be checked. Each class below is phrased as a
*requirement on the 13D theory's prediction surface*, not as a claim
that the prediction has already been produced.

The layer is partitioned by force sector and matter-force coupling
class. Each class names its UQF-row inheritance (the gate of this
paper that supplies the underlying physics certificate) and its C-FF
inheritance (the Paper 2 interface constraint whose target the
prediction completes).

### 16.1.1 Gravity-sector precision targets

**UQF inheritance:** UQF-5 (graviton certificate), UQF-10 (compactification
stability).
**C-FF inheritance:** C-FF7 (gravity/gauge separation), C-FF11
(low-energy sanity target — Newtonian limit).

- The **short-distance inverse-square-law tests**. Torsion-balance
  experiments now reach down to roughly $52\ \mu\text{m}$ (Eöt-Wash
  group, Adelberger collaboration, current best result 2024) with no
  deviation from $1/r^2$. The 13D theory's compactification spectrum at
  the locked volume-modulus point fixes the scale at which a $1/r^{2+n}$
  correction would become visible; any such correction must be checked
  against the Eöt-Wash bound and against the Paper 2 §6.4 KK threshold.
- The **equivalence-principle tests**. MICROSCOPE has reported
  $\eta = (-1.5 \pm 2.3) \times 10^{-15}$, consistent with universality
  to $10^{-15}$. The Paper 2 §6.3a check guarantees a universal leading
  gravitational coupling in the 13D theory; the precision-observable
  layer requires that this universality survives at the next loop
  order under the §6.10 correction ledger.
- The **parametrized post-Newtonian (PPN) parameters**
  $\gamma, \beta, \xi, \alpha_{1,2,3}, \zeta_{1,2,3,4}$, currently
  constrained by Cassini ($|\gamma-1| < 2.3 \times 10^{-5}$), Lunar
  Laser Ranging ($|\beta-1| < 1.1 \times 10^{-4}$), and pulsar timing
  ($\alpha_3 \lesssim 4 \times 10^{-20}$). The 13D Einstein-limit
  reduction must reproduce GR's PPN signature within experimental
  band.
- The **gravitational-wave propagation tests**. Speed of GWs from
  GW170817+GRB170817A constrains $|c_g - c|/c < 10^{-15}$; polarization
  content is consistent with only the two GR tensor modes;
  inspiral-merger-ringdown waveform consistency in the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA
  O4 catalog further constrains modifications. The 13D theory must
  preserve all of these in the recovered Einstein limit; any predicted
  deviation (from a non-trivial KK graviton tower, for example) must
  be located in a frequency band not already excluded.

### 16.1.2 Strong-sector (QCD) precision targets

**UQF inheritance:** UQF-6 (gauge-boson certificate — gluon component),
UQF-11 (nonperturbative QCD).
**C-FF inheritance:** C-FF1, C-FF6, C-FF11 (asymptotic-freedom anchor).

- The **strong coupling $\alpha_s(M_Z)$**, currently determined to
  $\alpha_s(M_Z) = 0.1180 \pm 0.0009$ (PDG 2024 world average from
  lattice, $\tau$ decays, deep-inelastic scattering, jets at hadron
  colliders, and $Z$-pole event shapes). The 13D theory's prediction
  from §6.4 KK threshold corrections and the strong-sector projection
  of §5 (Paper 2) must remain within this band.
- The **hadronic spectrum and mass gap**. UQF-11 supplies the
  nonperturbative-QCD route; the precision-observable layer requires
  that the predicted mass gap is consistent with lattice-QCD inputs
  and that the lowest hadronic resonances reproduce experimental
  masses within the lattice-QCD uncertainty band.
- The **hadronic vacuum polarization** contribution to $(g-2)_\mu$.
  Currently dominated by the data-driven ($e^+e^- \to \text{hadrons}$)
  vs lattice-QCD (BMW collaboration) split. The 13D theory must
  either inherit the SM HVP value as a low-energy sanity inheritance
  (preserving C-FF11 of Paper 2) or supply an identifiable additional
  contribution whose magnitude is bracketed by the experiment-theory
  gap.

### 16.1.3 Electroweak-sector precision targets (EWPO)

**UQF inheritance:** UQF-6 (gauge-boson certificate — $W^\pm,Z$
components), UQF-8 (Higgs / Goldstone certificate).
**C-FF inheritance:** C-FF3, C-FF4, C-FF8, C-FF10 (anomaly compatibility).

- The **oblique parameters** $S, T, U$ of Peskin–Takeuchi. PDG global
  fit (2024) gives $S = -0.05 \pm 0.07$, $T = 0.00 \pm 0.06$,
  $U = 0.08 \pm 0.07$. Any new heavy state predicted by the 13D
  theory between the electroweak scale and the compactification scale
  must be re-checked against these bands.
- The **effective leptonic weak mixing angle**
  $\sin^2\theta_{\rm eff}^{\rm lep}$. Tevatron + LHC + LEP combination
  gives $\sin^2\theta_{\rm eff}^{\rm lep} = 0.23155 \pm 0.00004$.
- The **$W$-boson mass** $m_W$. The most active EWPO tension in the
  literature: PDG world average sits near
  $m_W = 80.3692 \pm 0.0133$ GeV after the post-CDF reanalyses
  (ATLAS 2024 update; LHCb 2025 result), while the SM prediction from
  the global EW fit is $m_W = 80.354 \pm 0.007$ GeV (Gfitter / HEPfit,
  current as of 2026).
- The **full $Z$-pole observable suite**: $\Gamma_Z$, $R_\ell$,
  $R_b$, $R_c$, $A_{\rm FB}^{0,b}$, $A_{\rm FB}^{0,c}$, $A_b$, $A_c$,
  $\sigma_{\rm had}^0$. The LEP-1 legacy data set fixes these to
  per-mille precision; the 13D theory must reproduce each within band.
- The **CKM matrix with full uncertainties** — Wolfenstein parameters
  $(\lambda, A, \bar\rho, \bar\eta)$ with covariance (CKMfitter 2024
  central values: $\lambda = 0.22501 \pm 0.00068$,
  $A = 0.826^{+0.018}_{-0.015}$, $\bar\rho = 0.1591 \pm 0.0094$,
  $\bar\eta = 0.3523^{+0.0073}_{-0.0071}$); Jarlskog invariant
  $J = (3.08^{+0.15}_{-0.13}) \times 10^{-5}$; unitarity-triangle
  angles $\alpha, \beta, \gamma$ (with $\gamma = (66.4^{+3.0}_{-3.5})^\circ$
  from LHCb 2024); the full $3\times 3$ CKM magnitude matrix. Article-B
  §8.2 supplies the HC-1 anchor (same $\omega^{(1,0)}$ implies $J$ at
  machine precision); the 13D theory must reproduce $J$ within the
  global-fit band under its §4 numerical pipeline.
- The **PMNS matrix** — mixing angles $\theta_{12}, \theta_{23},
  \theta_{13}$ (NuFIT 5.3 central values:
  $\sin^2\theta_{12} = 0.307^{+0.013}_{-0.012}$,
  $\sin^2\theta_{23} = 0.572^{+0.018}_{-0.023}$ NO,
  $\sin^2\theta_{13} = 0.02203^{+0.00056}_{-0.00059}$); Dirac CP phase
  $\delta_{\rm CP} = (197^{+27}_{-24})^\circ$ NO; Majorana phases
  $\alpha_{21}, \alpha_{31}$ (conditional on main-manuscript
  Appendix K mechanism); mass ordering (NO vs IO) and absolute mass
  scale (KATRIN $m_\beta < 0.45$ eV; Planck+BAO+DESI $\sum m_\nu$
  bound at the current cosmological release).

### 16.1.4 QED-sector precision targets

**UQF inheritance:** UQF-6 (gauge-boson certificate — photon component
post-EW breaking).
**C-FF inheritance:** C-FF8 (QED downstream of EW), C-FF11 (Coulomb
law, photon masslessness).

- The **fine-structure constant $\alpha_{\rm em}$** at zero
  momentum-transfer. Currently determined to
  $\alpha^{-1} = 137.035999084(21)$ from atomic recoil measurements
  (Berkeley 2018 / LKB 2020). The 13D theory's prediction must remain
  within this band; the photon-mass post-breaking remnant per C-FF8
  must remain compatible with the laboratory bound
  $m_\gamma < 10^{-18}$ eV.
- The **anomalous magnetic moment of the electron** $(g-2)_e$,
  currently the most precise consistency test of QED;
  $a_e^{\rm exp} - a_e^{\rm SM}$ at the $10^{-13}$ level.
- The **anomalous magnetic moment of the muon** $(g-2)_\mu$. The
  experimental world average from Fermilab E989 Run-6 (2025) combined
  with BNL E821 is $a_\mu^{\rm exp} = 116592061(41) \times 10^{-11}$;
  the SM prediction is dominated by the HVP split between data-driven
  and lattice (BMW collaboration) evaluations. This row appears under
  the EW-sector and QCD-sector classes as well; here it tests the
  QED-side contribution and the 13D theory's matching to it.

### 16.1.5 Matter-force coupling precision targets

**UQF inheritance:** UQF-7 (fermion quantization), UQF-8 (Higgs /
Goldstone).
**C-FF inheritance:** C-FF3 (shared matter bundle), C-FF4
(charge-normalization), C-FF10 (anomaly compatibility), C-FF11.

- The **rare flavor-changing decays**:
  - $B^0 \to K^{*0} \mu^+\mu^-$ and the angular observable $P_5'$;
    isospin-related $B^+ \to K^+ \mu^+\mu^-$ and $B^+ \to K^+ e^+e^-$;
    lepton-universality ratio $R_K$ (LHCb 2022 reanalysis: SM
    consistency). Any 13D modification of the dipole/scalar Wilson
    coefficients $C_7, C_9, C_{10}$ must remain consistent with the
    current global fit.
  - $B_s^0 \to \mu^+\mu^-$, measured at
    $\text{BR}(B_s \to \mu\mu) = (3.45 \pm 0.29) \times 10^{-9}$
    (LHCb+CMS+ATLAS combined 2024) versus the SM
    $\text{BR}_{\rm SM} = (3.66 \pm 0.14) \times 10^{-9}$.
  - $K^+ \to \pi^+ \nu\bar\nu$ (NA62 2024:
    $(10.6^{+4.0}_{-3.4}) \times 10^{-11}$ versus SM
    $(8.4 \pm 1.0) \times 10^{-11}$); $K_L \to \pi^0 \nu\bar\nu$
    (KOTO).
  - Charged-lepton-flavor-violating decays: $\mu \to e\gamma$ (MEG-II
    2024 bound $\text{BR} < 1.5 \times 10^{-13}$ at 90% CL);
    $\mu \to 3e$ (SINDRUM bound $< 10^{-12}$); $\mu \to e$ conversion
    (Mu2e / COMET projected sensitivity $\sim 10^{-17}$).

- The **Higgs sector** — mass $m_h = 125.20 \pm 0.11$ GeV (ATLAS+CMS
  Run-2 combination), couplings to gauge bosons and to third-generation
  fermions, signal-strengths $\mu_i$ in the standard production /
  decay channel grid (gluon-fusion, vector-boson-fusion, $V h$,
  $t\bar t h$; $h \to \gamma\gamma$, $h \to ZZ^*$, $h \to WW^*$,
  $h \to b\bar b$, $h \to \tau^+\tau^-$, $h \to \mu^+\mu^-$). The 13D
  Higgs / Wilson-line construction of §10 (UQF-8 certificate) must
  reproduce the SM Higgs coupling pattern within current Run-3
  precision.

### 16.1.6 Proton stability precision targets (most-consequential)

**UQF inheritance:** UQF-7 (fermion quantization — matter-bundle
assignments), UQF-9 (UV completion), UQF-10 (compactification stability).
**C-FF inheritance:** C-FF3, C-FF5 (no double-counting), C-FF11
(asymptotic-freedom anchor).

Proton stability is *the most stringent low-energy test of any GUT
embedding*, and the most consequential single observable for the 13D
theory's force-sector precision claim. The Paper-2 §5 strong-sector
and §8 weak-sector projections together with the §8.4 matter-bundle
conventions fix which dimension-six baryon-number-violating operators
are produced and at what scale they are generated.

- $p \to e^+ \pi^0$: current Super-Kamiokande bound
  $\tau/\text{BR} > 2.4 \times 10^{34}$ yr (90% CL, Super-K 2020);
  Hyper-K projection $\tau/\text{BR} > 1.3 \times 10^{35}$ yr after
  10 years of running.
- $p \to \mu^+ \pi^0$: current Super-K bound
  $\tau/\text{BR} > 1.6 \times 10^{34}$ yr.
- $p \to \nu K^+$ (canonical SUSY-favored channel): current Super-K
  bound $\tau/\text{BR} > 5.9 \times 10^{33}$ yr; DUNE far detector
  $\sim 1.3 \times 10^{34}$ yr after 10 years.
- $p \to e^+ K^0$: current bound $> 1.0 \times 10^{33}$ yr.
- $n \to \nu \pi^0$ and $n \to e^+ \pi^-$ channels.

The 13D theory must produce a per-channel lifetime prediction whose
shortest channel exceeds the current Super-K bound for that channel
and whose ordering between channels — the *signature pattern* — is a
falsifiable prediction distinguishable from the standard $SU(5)$,
$SO(10)$, flipped-$SU(5)$, and Pati–Salam alternatives.

Proton decay carries the highest *consequence-per-observation*: a
positive detection in any channel by Hyper-K or DUNE either confirms
the 13D theory's matter-bundle and matching-scale predictions or
falsifies them; a non-detection at Hyper-K's projected
$1.3 \times 10^{35}$ yr in $p \to e^+\pi^0$ pushes the matching scale
upward and either inherits to §6.9.3a's volume modulus or downgrades
the proton-stability prediction to *Open / Diagnostic*.

### 16.1.7 Strong-CP precision target

**UQF inheritance:** UQF-12 (strong CP).
**C-FF inheritance:** C-FF12 (scope-boundary: nonperturbative QCD
companion may not silently upgrade interface claims).

- The neutron electric dipole moment, currently bounded by PSI nEDM
  at $|d_n| < 1.8 \times 10^{-26}\ e\,\text{cm}$ (90% CL, 2020).
  The 13D theory's strong-CP candidate (UQF-12 of §13) must produce
  a prediction (or an explicit explanation for $\bar\theta \approx 0$)
  consistent with this bound; the prediction's falsification path is
  a future nEDM measurement at the $10^{-28}\ e\,\text{cm}$ level
  (n2EDM at PSI; SNS nEDM at Oak Ridge).

### 16.1.8 Beyond-SM force-sector predicted states (if any)

**UQF inheritance:** UQF-5 (graviton tower), UQF-6 (gauge KK partners),
UQF-10 (compactification stability).
**C-FF inheritance:** C-FF5 (no double-counting), C-FF12 (scope
boundary).

The 13D theory's matter-bundle assignments enumerate the SM fermion
content exactly. The question for the force sector is whether any
*additional state* is geometrically required at any scale between the
electroweak scale and $M_{\rm Pl}$. The precision-observable layer
requires:

- An explicit **state inventory** by scale: zero-mode SM force-carrier
  content (already locked), heavy KK partners (set by §6.4 quantization
  at the §6.9.3a volume-modulus point), any moduli below the
  compactification scale, any geometric scalar arising from the §6.3
  BV-BRST package, and any state required by anomaly inflow that is
  not already in the SM gauge content.
- For each predicted state: production cross-section at currently
  active and proposed colliders (HL-LHC at 14 TeV, FCC-hh at 100 TeV,
  ILC at 250–500 GeV, muon collider at 3–10 TeV), and discovery reach
  as a function of integrated luminosity.
- A negative result, if the inventory is *exhausted* by SM content
  plus the KK tower — that statement is itself a falsifiable
  prediction (no light dark-sector force carriers, no extended Higgs
  sector below compactification, no fourth family).

Hidden-sector force-leakage modes (which the next section, UQFC-18,
audits as UQF-15) are excluded from this row's positive inventory by
construction; they appear there as a *negative* (no-leakage) prediction.

---

## 16.2 Global force-sector precision table

Each row of the §16.1 precision-observable layer is reduced to its
predicted value (named, not computed), uncertainty (named), calibration
status, frozen-input status, comparison value, pull (named), pass/fail
rule, and authority. The table is the certificate-tier core of this
section: it locks the *infrastructure* for the force-sector precision
sweep. Numerical predicted values and pulls are *named*, not *populated*,
in this version; populating each row is the deliverable of the Tier-2
roadmap of §16.3.

| Observable | UQF row | C-FF row | Predicted value (13D) | Uncertainty | Calibration status | Frozen-input status | Comparison value (data) | Pull | Pass/fail rule | Authority (tool/partner) |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Gravity sector** | | | | | | | | | | |
| Short-distance gravity ($1/r^2$ to $\mu$m) | UQF-5, UQF-10 | C-FF7, C-FF11 | Predicted-$1/r^{2+n}$ correction or null | Locked by §6.9.3a KK mass | AUDIT | Frozen via §6.9.3a volume modulus | Eöt-Wash 2024: no deviation to $\sim 52\ \mu$m | TBC at sweep | $\geq 3\sigma$ deviation absent or located in band | Eöt-Wash (Adelberger); cold-neutron group |
| Equivalence principle $\eta$ | UQF-5 | C-FF7 | Predicted at next loop under §6.10 ledger | Locked by §6.10 | AUDIT | Frozen via §6.3a + §6.10 | MICROSCOPE: $\eta = (-1.5 \pm 2.3) \times 10^{-15}$ | TBC | $|\eta_{\rm pred}| <$ MICROSCOPE band | MICROSCOPE / STE-QUEST; Eöt-Wash |
| PPN parameters $\gamma, \beta$, et seq. | UQF-5 | C-FF7, C-FF11 | GR values at PN order 1, 2 | Locked by §6.9.4 reduction | AUDIT | Frozen via §6.9.4 | Cassini, LLR, pulsar timing | TBC | Within experimental band | Will PPN community; NANOGrav / EPTA / PPTA / IPTA |
| GW propagation ($c_g$, polarization, waveforms) | UQF-5 | C-FF7 | GR target; KK-tower correction at frequency $\geq M_{\rm KK}$ | Locked by §6.4 KK spectrum | AUDIT | Frozen via §6.4 + §6.9.3a | LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA O4; GW170817 + GRB170817A | TBC | Within current GW constraint envelope | LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA; LISA |
| **Strong sector (QCD)** | | | | | | | | | | |

| **EW sector (EWPO)** | | | | | | | | | | |
| $S, T, U$ (Peskin-Takeuchi) | UQF-6 ($W,Z$), UQF-8 | C-FF3, C-FF8, C-FF10 | Predicted from 13D oblique-parameter machinery + KK insertions | Locked by KK spectrum | AUDIT | Frozen via §6.4 + UQF-8 | PDG 2024: $S = -0.05 \pm 0.07$, $T = 0.00 \pm 0.06$, $U = 0.08 \pm 0.07$ | TBC | Within $3\sigma$ ellipse | HEPfit (de Blas, Ciuchini, Reina, Silvestrini); Gfitter |

| PMNS $\delta_{\rm CP}$ | UQF-7 | C-FF3 | Article-A §4 phase prediction | Locked | AUDIT | Frozen | NuFIT 5.3: $(197^{+27}_{-24})^\circ$ NO; T2K-NOvA tension | TBC | Within $3\sigma$ of one allowed configuration | NuFIT; T2K; NOvA; DUNE; Hyper-K |

The table is *complete* relative to Paper 2's §2.2 exclusion list,
restricted to the force-sector scope of this paper. Every observable
that Paper 2 §2.2 defers — full EWPO, full CKM/PMNS, full flavor
anomalies, proton stability, gravitational tests, $(g-2)_\mu$, $m_W$,
KK threshold, BSM force-carrier inventory, strong-CP — is re-listed
here as a framework row with named computation requirement (Tool /
partner), constraint experiment, and pass/fail rule. The four UQC-8
table rows that pertain to cosmology / dark sector / baryogenesis are
*not* re-listed: those are Paper 4 material per the §HANDOFF hierarchy.

There is no overlap between *what Paper 2 claims* and *what this
section requires the precision-observable layer to deliver for the
force sectors*; the two documents do not double-count.

---

## 16.3 Tier-2 roadmap (force-sector restriction of UQC-8.3)

The infrastructure of §16.1 and §16.2 is closed at certificate-tier in
this section. The Tier-2 actual prediction values are not. The roadmap
below is the force-sector restriction of UQC-8.3, with the cosmology /
dark / baryogenesis bullets removed.

**Year 0–1 (in-house + tool-partnership setup).**

- *In-house.* Lock the Article-A §4 fermion-sector machinery as the
  numerical input pipeline for the CKM, PMNS, and matter-force coupling
  rows. The §4 mass / mixing surface is already at machine-precision
  status for fermion masses and CKM magnitudes (per Article A); the
  present roadmap requires reading off Wolfenstein parameters with
  covariance, Jarlskog $J$, unitarity-triangle angles, PMNS angles,
  $\delta_{\rm CP}$, and (conditional on Appendix K) the Majorana
  extension.
- *Tool-partnership setup.* Establish working contact with HEPfit
  (de Blas, Ciuchini, Reina, Silvestrini), CKMfitter (Descotes-Genon,
  Monteil), and NuFIT (Gonzalez-Garcia, Maltoni). Deliverable for each:
  a wrapper that takes the 13D §4 prediction surface and feeds it
  through the partner's existing $\chi^2$ infrastructure.
- *In-house.* Write the 13D KK threshold-mass calculation at the
  locked volume-modulus point of §6.9.3a, producing the first row of
  the threshold spectrum at certificate-tier (rather than as a
  parametric one-liner).
- *In-house.* Write the dimension-six baryon-number-violating
  operator matching at the §8.4 matter-bundle level and obtain the
  matching-scale dependence per channel; preliminary lifetime
  estimates with RBC-UKQCD hadronic matrix elements as static input.

**Year 1–3 (partnership-led predictions + first observable comparisons).**

- *Partnership (HEPfit / Gfitter).* First full EWPO global fit with
  13D oblique-parameter insertions: numerical $S, T, U$ with covariance
  and a $\chi^2$ against the LEP+LHC EWPO data; $m_W$ prediction
  reconciled with the Gfitter/HEPfit SM-fit band and the PDG world
  average; $Z$-pole observable suite reproduced to per-mille.
- *Partnership (CKMfitter / UTfit + flavio).* Full CKM fit with 13D
  Yukawa textures from Article-A §4 fed through inclusive / exclusive
  semileptonic decay machinery, with loop-induced $\epsilon_K, \Delta
  m_d, \Delta m_s, \sin 2\beta, \gamma$. Lattice hadronic matrix
  elements from FLAG (Aoki et al.). Output: Wolfenstein parameters
  with covariance, Jarlskog $J$, unitarity-triangle closure test.
- *Partnership (FlavBit / flavio / SuperIso).* Rare-decay observable
  predictions for $B \to K^{(*)}\mu\mu$, $B_s \to \mu\mu$,
  $K \to \pi\nu\bar\nu$, $\mu \to e\gamma$. The Wilson-coefficient
  bases are well-established; the 13D matching at the compactification
  scale is the new input.
- *In-house.* Proton-decay rate calculation per channel, with lattice
  matrix elements from RBC-UKQCD (uncertainty $\sim 10\%$ on current
  $p \to e^+ \pi^0$ ME). Outcome: per-channel lifetime predictions to
  be compared against current Super-K bounds and Hyper-K projections.
- *Partnership (NuFIT / Bari / Valencia + JUNO theory).* First PMNS
  global fit with 13D §4 neutrino mass matrix. Outcome: predicted
  ordering, absolute scale, $\delta_{\rm CP}$ prediction with
  covariance, comparison against JUNO 2030 ordering sensitivity.
- *Partnership (LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA + LISA).* GW propagation row: speed,
  polarization, and waveform consistency tested against current O4
  catalog and projected O5 release; KK graviton tower (if any)
  inserted in propagation kernel.

**Year 3–5 (closure of the precision-observable layer's first sweep).**

- *In-house.* Write the synthesis: each row of the §16.2 table
  populated with a numerical prediction, its uncertainty, the data
  set against which it has been checked, and the residual to the
  global fit (or a pass/fail at $1\sigma, 2\sigma, 3\sigma$
  significance). At this point the section's audit-tier "Predicted
  value (13D)" column is replaced row-by-row with certificate-tier
  prediction outputs.
- *Field-wide.* Inherited progress on the data side: HL-LHC EWPO
  reaches design luminosity; Belle II completes 50 ab$^{-1}$; Hyper-K
  starts data taking; KATRIN reports final result; Fermilab E989
  reports final $a_\mu$; MEG-II reports final; Mu2e first physics
  data; LIGO O5 catalog; PSI n2EDM reports first result. The 13D
  prediction surface adjusts at each release; the *infrastructure*
  defined here does not change.

**Year 5–7 (next-generation experimental matching).**

- *Field-wide.* DUNE and Hyper-K reach full neutrino-physics
  programme; JUNO resolves mass ordering; nEXO and LEGEND-1000 push
  $0\nu\beta\beta$ sensitivity into the inverted-ordering window;
  HL-LHC completes; FCC-ee CDR enters decision phase; SNS nEDM
  reports. By this horizon, each row of the §16.2 table either has a
  confirmed prediction (consistent with all data) or a falsified
  prediction (rejected at $\geq 3\sigma$). Either outcome is
  informative: confirmation strengthens the framework, falsification
  localizes the failing row and points to the §6.10
  correction-ledger entry that has to be revisited.

**What no roadmap can promise.** None of the above promises that the
precision-observable sweep, when completed, will fully confirm the 13D
theory at every row. The honest expectation: the framework is
*structurally* compatible with the data we have today; the first sweep
will reveal which rows are *tight* (high diagnostic value), which are
*loose* (limited diagnostic value), and which are *in tension*
(requiring re-examination of the corresponding 13D ingredient).
Tension does not mean falsification — it means an active research
direction.

---

## 16.4 Falsification path summary (force-sector restriction)

A precision-row falsifier triggers when:

- An EWPO prediction lies outside the current global-fit band at
  $\geq 3\sigma$, with no identifiable §6.10 correction-ledger entry
  to absorb the deviation.
- A CKM or PMNS parameter prediction lies outside the global-fit band
  at $\geq 3\sigma$ under the locked Article-A §4 fermion-sector
  pipeline.
- A rare-decay rate prediction exceeds the relevant experimental upper
  bound (or falls below an observed signal) at $\geq 3\sigma$.
- A proton-decay channel's predicted lifetime is *shorter* than the
  Super-K bound, with no inheritance from the §6.9.3a volume modulus
  to push the matching scale higher.
- A short-distance gravity prediction predicts a $1/r^2$ deviation at
  a scale where current torsion-balance data rules it out.
- A PPN-parameter prediction deviates from the GR value at any order
  greater than the experimental constraint.
- A KK threshold prediction places the lowest mode at a mass already
  excluded by HL-LHC direct searches in the predicted channel.
- A neutron-EDM prediction exceeds the current PSI nEDM bound.
- The proton-decay *signature pattern* matches one of the standard
  alternative GUTs ($SU(5), SO(10)$, flipped-$SU(5)$, Pati-Salam)
  rather than the 13D-distinctive ordering, with no §6.10 entry to
  re-route.

Each falsifier above is *one row*. A row-level falsification downgrades
that row to *Open / Diagnostic* and triggers either a §6.10-style
correction-ledger entry or a reopening of the relevant Article-A /
Paper-2 / UQFC-precursor-gate ingredient. It does not downgrade the
framework-tier structure of the present section, because the framework
specifies *what has to be true of the prediction surface* — falsification
of a prediction is data input to the surface, not data input against
the surface's specification.

Among the rows in §16.2, the highest *consequence-per-observation* row
is the proton-stability row group: Hyper-K and DUNE will either confirm
or falsify the 13D matter-bundle and matching-scale predictions in the
$3\times 10^{34}$ yr to $1.3\times 10^{35}$ yr range, and a positive
detection or null at the Hyper-K projection will be the single most
diagnostic precision input the force-sector layer can receive. The
$m_W$ row is the highest-current-tension row, with the post-CDF
PDG world average and the Gfitter/HEPfit SM-fit band separated by
$\sim 1.5\sigma$; the 13D prediction must navigate this tension
honestly, naming the §8.3 EW-embedding or §6.10 correction-ledger
inheritance.

---

## 16.5 Tier-2 promotion conditions (row-level)

A row of §16.2 promotes from AUDIT-tier "Predicted value (13D)" to
CERTIFICATE-tier only when **all** of the following hold:

1. The Article-A §4 fermion-sector machinery, or the §6.4 KK
   quantization at the §6.9.3a modulus, or whichever 13D ingredient
   supplies the relevant input, has produced the numerical prediction
   with stated covariance.
2. The named external tool / partner from the §16.2 table has
   independently verified the prediction by running it through their
   existing global-fit infrastructure.
3. The prediction's $\chi^2$ against the relevant experimental data
   set is within the corresponding band, *or* the deviation is
   localized in a §6.10 correction-ledger entry that the main
   manuscript has approved.
4. The prediction's falsification path (per §16.4) has been
   operationalized — that is, a specific experimental result that
   would invalidate the prediction has been named and is within reach
   of an active or planned experiment.
5. The hard-gate vector and BG-10 status are not disturbed by the
   row's promotion.

Conditions (1)–(5) are *row-level*, not section-level. Different rows
will close at different times; this section's framework-tier status
does not require any single row to close. The framework-tier value of
the section is that it specifies a *complete and partitioned*
force-sector prediction surface, with every external tool and partner
named, and that this specification holds whether or not any individual
row has yet been numerically populated.

None of the row-level promotion conditions is *presently* met for any
row. Nothing in this section is to be cited as if any row has been
promoted to certificate-tier value status.

---

## 16.6 Cross-references

- **UQFC-3 (UQF gate stack).** This section discharges UQF-13. Every
  row of the §16.2 table inherits a UQF-row label and a C-FF-row label
  in the "UQF row" and "C-FF row" columns. A row whose prediction
  falsifies downgrades the named UQF row (and thereby the framework
  inheritance into §16) per the downgrade ladder of §3 and per the
  final downgrade map of §19.
- **UQFC-§5–15 (Phase 2 + 3 + 5 + 6 certificates).** Every row's
  "Predicted value (13D)" cell is the *output surface* of one or more
  of these gates. UQF-5 (graviton) feeds the gravity-sector rows;
  UQF-6 (gauge bosons) feeds the strong, EW, and QED rows; UQF-7
  (fermion quantization) feeds the CKM, PMNS, matter-force coupling,
  and proton-decay rows; UQF-8 (Higgs) feeds the Higgs and EW rows;
  UQF-9 (UV completion) and UQF-10 (compactification stability) feed
  the proton-decay matching scale and KK threshold rows; UQF-11
  (nonperturbative QCD) feeds the QCD spectrum, mass-gap, and HVP
  rows; UQF-12 (strong CP) feeds the nEDM row.
- **Paper 2 §2.2.** This section is the proper venue that Paper 2's
  §2.2 exclusion defers to for force-sector precision. The §2.2
  exclusion is *preserved* as the correct scope statement of Paper 2.
- **Paper 2 §6.4 (KK quantization), §6.9.3a (Einstein-frame caveat /
  volume-modulus stabilization), §6.9.4 (Einstein-Hilbert reduction),
  §6.9.6 (weak-field Newtonian limit), §6.10 (correction ledger).**
  These are the Paper-2 hooks for the gravity-sector and KK rows of
  §16.2.
- **C-FF11.** Every row of §16.2 is downstream of a C-FF11 anchor:
  EWPO and CKM/PMNS ride on the Fermi-limit anchor; gravity rows
  ride on the Newtonian-limit anchor; QED rows ride on Coulomb /
  photon-masslessness; the proton-decay row rides on the
  asymptotic-freedom anchor. C-FF11 is the *sanity floor* below
  which no §16.2 row can drop.
- **C-FF12.** The companion paper may not use excluded sectors —
  full QG UV completion, nonperturbative QCD, strong CP, cosmology,
  dark matter, dark energy, baryogenesis — to upgrade interface
  claims. This section is the *precision-phenomenology* section for
  the force sector, distinct from those categories. UQF-9 / UQF-10 /
  UQF-11 / UQF-12 each carry their own certificate inside this paper
  and do not borrow from any companion outside the paper.
- **C-FF13.** Detailed gate certificates, freeze records, and formal
  review vocabulary remain in the main GUT manuscript and in Article-A.
  This section invokes them by interface only and adds no new gate
  vocabulary.
- **C-FF14.** Every framework row of §16.2 carries an explicit
  falsifier in the "Pass/fail rule" column, enumerated in §16.4.
- **Main GUT manuscript Appendix K (neutrino sector).** The Majorana
  extension of the PMNS row is conditional on the Appendix K
  mechanism; this section does not anticipate Appendix K beyond noting
  the conditional.
- **Article A §4 (fermion-sector machinery).** Numerical pipeline for
  CKM, PMNS, Higgs-coupling, and rare-decay rows. The present section
  locks the *interface* through which the Article-A pipeline is
  queried for precision predictions; it does not modify Article A
  itself.
- **Article B §8.2 (Jarlskog HC-1 anchor).** The Jarlskog row inherits
  the HC-1 machine-precision statement from Article B §8.2.
- **UQC-8 (predecessor specification).** This section is the
  force-sector restriction of UQC-8. The cosmology / dark / baryogenesis
  rows of UQC-8 are excluded by Paper 3's hard claim boundary and
  defer to Paper 4. The UQC-8 hard-gate, BG-10, and SoT discipline
  is preserved.
- **UQFC-19 (falsification and downgrade map).** The §16.2 pass/fail
  rules feed the UQF-13 row of the §19 final downgrade map; failures
  there carry forward to the min-rule of §19.

# UQFC-17 — Unitarity / Causality / Locality Audit
*Phase 4 — Consistency certificates · gate UQF-14 · drafted 2026-06-08*

> **Gate card — UQF-14: Unitarity / causality / locality audit** *(auto-derived from §3.3 / §4.4, the single source of truth per §3.0; any discrepancy with this chapter is a drafting bug)*
>
> | Field | Value |
> |---|---|
> | Tier | **AUDIT** (per-sector bounds are routine where the sector is perturbative; the graviton sector's unitarity above the cutoff is conditional on UQF-9). |
> | Required certificate | Per-sector unitarity bound check (e.g., partial-wave unitarity on $WW \to WW$, gluon-gluon scattering, graviton-graviton scattering at perturbative scale); causality check via Lorentz-covariance and spectral conditions on physical states; locality check via cluster decomposition on $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$. |
> | Frozen inputs | UQF-3 (physical Hilbert space); UQF-4 (BRST); UQF-9 (UV completion for high-energy unitarity). |
> | Pass / fail | Pass: per-sector unitarity within declared cutoff; Lorentz covariance respected; cluster decomposition holds on $\mathcal H_{\rm phys}$. Fail: any negative probability, any superluminal signal, any cluster-decomposition violation. |
> | Downgrade | Per-sector. Unitarity violation in the graviton sector at scale $\Lambda_\star < M_{\rm Planck}$ → UQF-5 graviton certificate drops one tier; gauge-sector unitarity violation → corresponding UQF-6 sub-row drops. |
> | C-FF rows consumed | C-FF5 (no double counting). |
> | Ledger rows consumed (§4.4) | Rows 1, 4 (high-energy scattering); Row 8 (ghost-loop cancellation in optical theorem) |

## 17.0 Scope statement and tier discipline

This section discharges UQF-14 of the gate stack defined in §3 of this
paper: a *unitarity, causality, and locality audit* for the four force
sectors as quantized by §§5–15 of the present paper. The audit
operates on the BV-BRST construction of §5, the physical-Hilbert-space
construction of §6, the anomaly-and-measure closure of §7, the
graviton certificate of §8, the gauge-boson certificates of §9, the
Higgs / Goldstone certificate of §10, and the fermion certificate of
§11. It is the *structural discipline* layer that verifies that the
quantized force-sector content carries no negative probabilities, no
superluminal signaling, and no nonlocal failures of cluster
decomposition in the 4D low-energy limit.

The section is **two-tier**, and the tier discipline is load-bearing.

**Tier 1 — structural discipline (CERTIFICATE-TIER).** Where standard
QFT supports it, the audit can be discharged at certificate tier. This
covers: (i) perturbative S-matrix unitarity from BRST cohomology and
the positivity of the physical-Hilbert-space construction; (ii)
causality from microcausality of the free-field commutators in each
sector and from causal perturbation theory at each loop order;
(iii) locality from the local action principle, the cluster
decomposition for connected $n$-point functions, and the absence of
auxiliary fields with action outside the lightcone. These are
*structural* in the sense that the audit consists of checking that the
13D theory, after compactification and projection to the four force
sectors, does not violate the standard QFT consistency conditions that
hold for the Standard Model. Where it does not violate them, the
audit closes at certificate-tier; where it does, the row downgrades to
AUDIT-tier or *Open / Diagnostic* per §19.

**Tier 2 — nonperturbative subtleties (AUDIT-TIER).** Full
nonperturbative unitarity for the strong sector, full causality
under graviton-loop dressing, and full cluster decomposition under the
13D-to-4D projection in the presence of the §6.4 KK tower are
*open at the same level as QCD nonperturbative*. The audit names these
explicitly and routes them through UQF-9 (UV completion), UQF-10
(compactification stability), and UQF-11 (nonperturbative QCD), each
of which carries its own tier label inside this paper.

### 17.0.1 Anti-overclaim discipline

This section is *structural discipline*, not a deep proof. In
particular:

- This section does **not** claim a nonperturbative proof of unitarity
  for the strong sector beyond what UQF-11 supplies. The
  nonperturbative-QCD route of §12 (UQF-11) carries its own tier
  label, and the present section inherits it without modification.
- This section does **not** claim a full nonperturbative proof of
  causality under graviton self-coupling beyond what UQF-9 supplies.
  The UV-completion route of §14 (UQF-9) carries its own tier label,
  and the present section inherits it without modification.
- This section does **not** claim that the cluster-decomposition
  property is exact under the 13D compactification with all KK modes
  retained; the audit operates at the truncated mode expansion of
  §6.4 (Paper 2) and any failure beyond truncation is named.
- This section does **not** assert that the 13D theory's full
  S-matrix has been computed. What it asserts is that the *structural
  preconditions* for unitarity, causality, and locality are satisfied
  at the perturbative-plus-truncated-KK order at which the §§8–11
  certificates operate.

This is the same anti-overclaim discipline that runs through Paper 2
(C-FF12 scope-boundary constraint) and through Article A (anti-fitting
discipline). The present section preserves it explicitly: where
standard QFT supports a certificate, claim it; where nonperturbative
subtlety enters, name it and route to the corresponding UQF row.

---

## 17.1 Unitarity audit

Unitarity is the requirement that the S-matrix on the physical Hilbert
space satisfies $S^\dagger S = S S^\dagger = \mathbb{1}$, equivalently
that no scattering amplitude produces a negative probability and that
total probability is conserved. In a gauge theory it is the requirement
that unphysical states (longitudinal polarizations, Faddeev-Popov ghosts,
BRST-exact states) cancel from physical observables, leaving the
physical-state norms positive-definite and the S-matrix unitary on the
quotient $\mathcal{H}_{\rm phys} = \ker Q_{\rm BRST} / \mathrm{im}\,
Q_{\rm BRST}$.

### 17.1.1 Per-sector check

The audit proceeds sector by sector, in the order of the §§8–11
certificates.

**Gravity sector (UQF-5 inheritance).** The graviton certificate of
§8 extracts the physical spin-2 massless graviton modes from the 4D
metric block $g_{\mu\nu}$. Unitarity at perturbative order is the
statement that the two physical transverse-traceless polarizations
have positive norm and that the four BRST-exact (gauge-redundant)
polarizations cancel against the Faddeev-Popov ghost contributions
in the loop expansion. This is the standard textbook result for
linearized gravity around flat Minkowski background; the 13D theory
inherits it directly through the §6.4 (Paper 2) Kaluza-Klein
zero-mode reduction at the locked volume-modulus point of §6.9.3a.

The *KK graviton tower* adds a discrete spectrum of massive spin-2
modes. Massive spin-2 fields in flat space carry five physical
polarizations (helicities $\pm 2, \pm 1, 0$), and unitarity for the
free massive graviton is automatic in the Fierz-Pauli action; the
13D theory inherits this provided the KK mass spectrum from §6.4 is
real and positive (it is, by the §6.9.3a volume modulus). Unitarity
of *amplitudes involving* the KK graviton tower at high energy is
the Vainshtein / strong-coupling question for massive gravity; in the
13D theory this is routed through UQF-9 (UV completion) and UQF-10
(compactification stability), and the present audit does not claim
to resolve it nonperturbatively. At perturbative order with a finite
KK truncation, the audit closes at certificate-tier; beyond that, it
inherits the tier label of UQF-9 / UQF-10.

**Strong sector (UQF-6 gluon component inheritance, UQF-11
inheritance for nonperturbative).** The gluon certificate of §9
extracts $SU(3)_c$ Yang-Mills with eight physical color polarizations
per gluon at perturbative order. Unitarity at perturbative order
follows from standard BRST cohomology for Yang-Mills: the two
unphysical polarizations per gauge boson are BRST-exact and cancel
against the Faddeev-Popov ghost loop contributions, as guaranteed by
the Kugo-Ojima quartet mechanism. The 13D theory inherits this
directly through the §5 (Paper 2) projection of $K_6 = SU(3)/T^2$
to the surviving $SU(3)_c$ color action.

*Nonperturbative* unitarity for the strong sector is the statement
that the confined hadronic spectrum carries positive norms — equivalently,
that the BRST quartet mechanism continues to work in the
nonperturbative regime where colored states do not appear as
asymptotic scattering states. This is the Kugo-Ojima color
confinement criterion, and its nonperturbative status is the
*same open question as QCD nonperturbative*. The present audit
inherits the UQF-11 tier label: certificate-tier where the
UQF-11 nonperturbative-QCD route supplies a confinement /
mass-gap certificate (§12 of this paper); AUDIT-tier or
*Open / Diagnostic* where it does not. The present section does
not upgrade UQF-11.

**Weak sector (UQF-6 $W,Z$ components inheritance, UQF-8 inheritance
for vacuum).** The $W^\pm, Z$ certificate of §9 extracts the
massive electroweak gauge bosons after EW breaking. Massive gauge
bosons carry three physical polarizations (transverse $\pm$ and
longitudinal). Unitarity for massive gauge bosons is the Higgs
mechanism: the longitudinal polarization is the would-be Goldstone
boson eaten by the gauge field, and the Equivalence Theorem
(Cornwall–Levin–Tiktopoulos; Lee–Quigg–Thacker) guarantees that
high-energy amplitudes involving longitudinal $W, Z$ scattering are
unitarized by the Higgs propagator. The 13D theory's Higgs / Wilson-line
construction of §10 (UQF-8) is the inheritance pathway for this
mechanism; the §8 (Paper 2) weak-sector projection from $S^2$
spin-cover combined with $S^1_Y$ hypercharge fixes the gauge content
to $SU(2)_L \times U(1)_Y$, and the EW breaking pattern is the
standard one (charged-shell Coulomb sanity per §11 of Paper 2 is
preserved).

Unitarity at perturbative order in the EW sector closes at
certificate-tier. *Nonperturbative* unitarity for the EW sector
(electroweak instanton effects, sphaleron transitions, baryon-number
violation at high temperature) is **excluded from this paper's
scope by the hard claim boundary** — those questions feed Paper 4's
baryogenesis discussion, which is *Open / Diagnostic* (BG-10).
The present audit inherits the BG-10 status without modification:
where BG-10 is *Open / Diagnostic*, the corresponding EW
nonperturbative-unitarity row of the present audit is also
*Open / Diagnostic*.

**QED sector (UQF-6 photon component inheritance).** The photon
certificate of §9 extracts the unbroken $U(1)_{\rm em}$ massless
photon as the post-breaking remnant per C-FF8. Unitarity at
perturbative order is the standard QED result: the photon's two
transverse physical polarizations have positive norm; the
longitudinal and timelike polarizations are gauge-redundant and
cancel in physical amplitudes via Gupta-Bleuler or BRST. The 13D
theory inherits this directly through C-FF8.

Nonperturbative QED in the Landau-pole regime is an open question
in the same way for the 13D theory as for the Standard Model; the
present audit names it and routes it to UQF-9 (UV completion). The
UV-completion route of §14 (UQF-9) does not require a resolution of
the QED Landau pole separately from the broader 13D UV-completion
strategy.

**Fermion sector (UQF-7 inheritance).** The fermion certificate of
§11 quantizes the chiral matter content of the §8.4 (Paper 2)
matter bundle. Unitarity at perturbative order requires (i) no
wrong-statistics states (no fermionic ghosts of physical-state
nature) and (ii) no mirror fermions surviving the projection. Both
conditions are met by construction in the §11 certificate: the
matter bundle assigns left-handed Weyl content with no mirror
partners surviving the chirality projection on $S^1_Y$ per Paper 2
§8, and the spin-statistics theorem is satisfied for each Weyl
species. The audit closes at certificate-tier for the perturbative
sector.

### 17.1.2 BRST cohomology and positivity

The BV-BRST construction of §5 supplies a nilpotent BRST charge
$Q_{\rm BRST}^2 = 0$ at the level of the master action. The physical
Hilbert space of §6 is the BRST cohomology
$\mathcal{H}_{\rm phys} = \ker Q_{\rm BRST} / \mathrm{im}\,
Q_{\rm BRST}$, and the §6 positivity certificate is the statement
that this quotient carries a positive-definite inner product. The
audit closes at certificate-tier provided:

(a) The BRST charge defined in §5 is nilpotent (UQF-4 certificate).
(b) The inner product on $\mathcal{H}_{\rm phys}$ is positive-definite
    (UQF-3 certificate).
(c) The S-matrix preserves $\mathcal{H}_{\rm phys}$
    (BRST-cohomology preservation under time evolution, equivalent to
    gauge-independence of physical amplitudes).

Conditions (a) and (b) are discharged inside the respective UQF gates
of this paper; the present section assumes their closure and inherits
the corresponding tier labels. Condition (c) is the *unitarity
audit proper* and is the content of §17.1.1 above, sector by sector.

### 17.1.3 Negative-norm and ghost-state inventory

To make the unitarity audit explicit, the per-sector inventory below
records, for each force sector, the unphysical-state content that the
BRST mechanism is required to cancel.

| Sector | Unphysical polarizations | Ghost content | Cancellation mechanism | Certificate path |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Gravity (zero-mode) | 2 (longitudinal + timelike per graviton mode) | Faddeev-Popov diffeomorphism ghosts | Standard linearized-gravity BRST | UQF-4, UQF-5 |
| Gravity (KK tower) | per-mode: 3 (massive spin-2 unphysical polarizations) | Stückelberg / spin-2 ghosts | Truncated KK BRST at §6.9.3a modulus | UQF-5, UQF-10 |
| Strong (gluons, perturbative) | 2 per gluon (longitudinal + timelike) | $SU(3)_c$ Faddeev-Popov ghosts | Kugo-Ojima quartet | UQF-4, UQF-6 |
| Strong (nonperturbative) | colored asymptotic states | not applicable | Kugo-Ojima color confinement criterion | UQF-11 (inherited tier) |
| Weak ($W^\pm, Z$) | 2 per boson (transverse unphysical + longitudinal mode) | $SU(2)_L$ Faddeev-Popov ghosts | Higgs mechanism + Equivalence Theorem | UQF-4, UQF-6, UQF-8 |
| QED (photon) | 2 (longitudinal + timelike) | $U(1)_{\rm em}$ Faddeev-Popov ghost | Standard QED Gupta-Bleuler / BRST | UQF-4, UQF-6 |
| Fermion | wrong-statistics states (none); mirror Weyls (none) | not applicable | Spin-statistics + §8 chirality projection | UQF-7 |

Every row reads "cancellation mechanism" as the standard QFT result
that the 13D theory inherits without modification. The audit closes at
certificate-tier for the perturbative rows; the nonperturbative-QCD
row inherits the UQF-11 tier label.

### 17.1.4 Unitarity violation paths

A unitarity-violation row triggers when:

- The BRST charge defined in §5 fails to be nilpotent at some loop
  order (UQF-4 failure). This is a §5 certificate failure, not a
  §17 failure; it propagates here as inheritance.
- The §6 physical-state positivity certificate produces a negative-norm
  physical state (UQF-3 failure). Same propagation logic.
- A spin-2 KK graviton mode in the §6.4 (Paper 2) tower acquires a
  negative mass-squared eigenvalue under loop corrections from the
  §6.10 ledger. This would indicate that the §6.9.3a volume modulus
  is not perturbatively stable; the row inherits the UQF-10 tier
  label and downgrades to *Open / Diagnostic* on failure.
- The Higgs mechanism in §10 fails to unitarize longitudinal $W, Z$
  scattering — for example because the §10 Higgs construction does
  not reproduce the SM Higgs couplings to gauge bosons within the
  Run-3 precision band. This is a UQF-8 failure that propagates here.
- A nonperturbative strong-sector amplitude produces a negative
  probability. This is a UQF-11 failure that propagates here; the
  Kugo-Ojima color-confinement criterion has not yet been proven
  nonperturbatively at the level the Clay Millennium Yang-Mills
  problem requires, and the audit's nonperturbative-QCD row is
  *Open / Diagnostic* until UQF-11 closes.

Each path above is *one row*. A row-level violation downgrades the
corresponding UQF row (UQF-3, UQF-4, UQF-8, UQF-10, UQF-11) per the
final downgrade map of §19; the present section does not introduce
its own downgrade vocabulary.

---

## 17.2 Causality audit

Causality is the requirement that commutators (or anticommutators for
fermions) of physical fields vanish outside the lightcone, equivalently
that no measurement at spacelike separation from another can be
influenced by it. In a relativistic QFT this is microcausality:
$[\phi(x), \phi(y)] = 0$ for $(x-y)^2 > 0$ for bosonic fields,
$\{\psi(x), \bar\psi(y)\} = 0$ for spacelike separation for fermionic
fields. At the macroscopic level it is the absence of superluminal
signaling, which the LSZ reduction connects to the analyticity and
crossing-symmetry properties of the S-matrix.

### 17.2.1 Per-carrier check

The 13D theory's force carriers are the graviton (UQF-5), the gluon /
$W^\pm$ / $Z$ / photon (UQF-6), the Higgs (UQF-8), and the KK partners
of each. The chiral matter content (UQF-7) is governed by the same
microcausality, with the appropriate fermionic anticommutator
replacement.

**Graviton (zero-mode).** The free linearized-gravity propagator is
the standard de Donder-gauge propagator on flat Minkowski background,
and the free-field commutator is the Pauli-Jordan function for a
massless spin-2 field. This vanishes outside the lightcone by
construction; microcausality is automatic. The 13D theory inherits
this directly through the §6.4 (Paper 2) zero-mode reduction. The
audit closes at certificate-tier.

**Graviton (KK tower).** Each massive KK graviton mode satisfies
its own Klein-Gordon-type equation with mass set by the §6.4
spectrum at the §6.9.3a volume-modulus point. The free-field
commutator for each KK mode is the Pauli-Jordan function for a
massive spin-2 field, which also vanishes outside the lightcone.
Microcausality is automatic at the level of free fields. *Causality
under interaction* (graviton self-coupling + KK-tower exchange) is
the Vainshtein / strong-coupling question, routed through UQF-9 /
UQF-10; the audit inherits the corresponding tier labels.

**Gluon (perturbative).** The free $SU(3)_c$ gluon propagator is
the standard Yang-Mills propagator in covariant gauge, and the free
gluon commutator vanishes outside the lightcone. The Faddeev-Popov
ghost satisfies the same microcausality (with the appropriate sign
from the ghost statistics). At interaction order, causal
perturbation theory (Epstein-Glaser) extends microcausality to
arbitrary loop order. The audit closes at certificate-tier for the
perturbative sector.

**Gluon (nonperturbative).** Causality in the confined phase is the
statement that nucleon-nucleon scattering amplitudes (the
hadron-level S-matrix) respect microcausality. This is supported by
hadronic-physics phenomenology — no measured nucleon scattering
amplitude has shown superluminal signaling — but a rigorous proof
from first-principles QCD is not available beyond what UQF-11
supplies. The audit inherits the UQF-11 tier label.

**$W^\pm, Z$.** Free massive gauge-boson propagators in unitary
gauge satisfy microcausality with the appropriate massive Pauli-Jordan
function. Causal perturbation theory extends to all orders. At
nonperturbative order (electroweak instantons, sphalerons), causality
is unaffected by the standard mechanisms (these contribute exponentially
suppressed amplitudes, not superluminal signaling). The audit closes
at certificate-tier for the perturbative sector; the nonperturbative-EW
sector inherits BG-10 status per the hard claim boundary.

**Photon.** Free QED propagator microcausality is the textbook
result; the 13D theory inherits it through C-FF8. The audit closes at
certificate-tier.

**Higgs.** The Higgs is a scalar with mass $m_h = 125.20 \pm 0.11$
GeV. Microcausality for a free massive scalar is automatic. At
interaction order, the Higgs self-coupling and Yukawa couplings are
local and produce causal amplitudes by standard Epstein-Glaser
construction. The audit closes at certificate-tier.

**KK partners of each carrier.** Each KK partner has a real positive
mass-squared from §6.4 at the §6.9.3a modulus and satisfies its own
free-field Klein-Gordon / Dirac / Proca equation in 4D. Microcausality
for each free KK partner is automatic. Causality of the full
13D-to-4D projection at all energies is the *causal-cluster* question
addressed in §17.3 (locality).

### 17.2.2 Commutator vanishing outside lightcone

To make the per-carrier audit explicit, the inventory below records,
for each force carrier, the form of the free-field commutator and the
guarantee that it vanishes outside the lightcone.

| Carrier | Mass | Free commutator | Vanishes outside lightcone? | Certificate path |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Graviton (zero-mode) | 0 | Pauli-Jordan, massless spin-2 | Yes (textbook) | UQF-5 |
| Graviton (KK $n$) | $M_{\rm KK}^{(n)}$ from §6.4 | Pauli-Jordan, massive spin-2 | Yes (textbook) for each $n$ | UQF-5, UQF-10 |
| Gluon | 0 | Pauli-Jordan, massless spin-1 | Yes (textbook) | UQF-6 |
| Gluon KK | $M_{\rm KK}^{(K_6, n)}$ | Pauli-Jordan, massive spin-1 | Yes (textbook) | UQF-6, UQF-10 |
| $W^\pm$ | $m_W \approx 80.37$ GeV | Massive Proca, unitary gauge | Yes (textbook) | UQF-6, UQF-8 |
| $Z$ | $m_Z \approx 91.19$ GeV | Massive Proca | Yes (textbook) | UQF-6, UQF-8 |
| EW KK | $M_{\rm KK}^{(S^2, n)}$, $M_{\rm KK}^{(S^1, n)}$ | Massive Proca | Yes (textbook) | UQF-6, UQF-10 |
| Photon | 0 | Pauli-Jordan, massless spin-1 | Yes (textbook) | UQF-6 |
| Higgs | $m_h \approx 125.20$ GeV | Klein-Gordon | Yes (textbook) | UQF-8 |
| Fermion species (each) | as in §11 | Dirac anticommutator | Yes (textbook) | UQF-7 |

Every row reads "Yes (textbook)" because the 13D theory's projection
to 4D force carriers does not introduce new field types beyond the
standard catalog (scalars, spinors, massless and massive vectors,
massless and massive spin-2). The microcausality property is inherited
for each row.

### 17.2.3 Causal-perturbation-theory extension

Microcausality of free fields extends to the S-matrix at all loop
orders by causal perturbation theory (Epstein-Glaser, Bogoliubov,
Steinmann). The standard QFT construction works without modification
in the 13D theory's 4D projection. The audit closes at certificate-tier
for the perturbative sector.

*Nonperturbative* causality — for example, causality of the
gravitational S-matrix under graviton self-coupling at all loop
orders — is the *same open question as nonperturbative quantum
gravity*, routed through UQF-9 and UQF-10. The present audit inherits
the corresponding tier labels.

### 17.2.4 No-superluminal-signaling check

The post-graviton-coupling propagation of gravitational waves is
constrained to $|c_g - c|/c < 10^{-15}$ by GW170817 + GRB170817A
multi-messenger observation. The 13D theory inherits this constraint
through the §UQFC-16.1.1 gravity-sector row. No carrier in the 13D
theory's spectrum propagates with a phase velocity greater than $c$
in the recovered Einstein limit; the KK graviton tower (if any) has
phase velocity at-most $c$ in the high-frequency limit.

For the gauge sector and matter sector, no analogous superluminal
window has been observed in the LHC or precision-experiment catalog.
The 13D theory's force-carrier dispersion relations are the standard
relativistic ones; no Lorentz-violating term is added at any loop
order accessible to the §6.4 truncation.

### 17.2.5 Causality violation paths

A causality-violation row triggers when:

- A KK graviton mode acquires a tachyonic ($M^2 < 0$) mass eigenvalue
  under loop corrections from §6.10. This is a §6.9.3a volume-modulus
  failure and inherits the UQF-10 tier label.
- A gauge boson, Higgs, or fermion KK partner acquires a tachyonic
  mass eigenvalue. Same logic, UQF-10 inheritance.
- The Equivalence-Theorem unitarity for longitudinal $W, Z$ scattering
  fails at high energy because the §10 Higgs construction does not
  reproduce the SM Higgs couplings within the Run-3 precision band.
  This is a UQF-8 failure that propagates here.
- A KK-tower exchange amplitude at high energy violates the
  Froissart bound (a sufficient condition for analyticity / crossing /
  causality of the S-matrix). This is a UQF-9 (UV completion) failure
  that propagates here.
- Gravitational-wave propagation deviates from $c_g = c$ at the level
  ruled out by GW170817+GRB170817A. This is a §UQFC-16.1.1 row
  falsification that propagates here.

Each path above is *one row*. A row-level violation downgrades the
corresponding UQF row per the §19 final downgrade map.

---

## 17.3 Locality audit

Locality is the requirement that (i) the action is built from local
operators — products of fields and their derivatives at a single
spacetime point — and (ii) cluster decomposition holds: connected
$n$-point functions factorize when one subset of arguments is taken
to spatial infinity from another. The first is the *local-action
principle*; the second is the *cluster decomposition principle*.

### 17.3.1 Local-action principle

The 13D action of §5 is, at the BV-BRST level, a sum of local terms in
the 13D fields. Local in 13D means at a single 13D spacetime point.
After compactification on $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1$ to the 4D
spacetime $M_{3,1}$, the 4D effective action is obtained by integrating
the 13D action over the compact factors at each 4D point. The result
is a 4D action that is local in 4D *at the level of any finite KK
truncation*: each truncated mode produces a finite-derivative local
operator in 4D.

The 4D effective action is *not* local in 4D if all KK modes are
retained: an infinite tower of massive modes integrated out at low
energy produces an effective action with non-local (form-factor-type)
operators suppressed by inverse powers of the KK mass. This is the
*standard* feature of Kaluza-Klein reduction and is not a pathology;
the 4D effective theory at energies $E \ll M_{\rm KK}$ is local up to
exponentially suppressed non-localities, and the non-localities are
controlled by the KK threshold spectrum from §6.4.

The audit closes at certificate-tier provided:

(a) The 13D action of §5 is local in 13D (UQF-2 certificate).
(b) The §6.4 KK truncation produces a local 4D effective action at
    each truncation level (geometric inheritance).
(c) The infinite-truncation limit produces an effective action whose
    non-localities are bounded by the KK threshold scale (UQF-10
    inheritance).

Conditions (a) and (c) are discharged inside UQF-2 and UQF-10
respectively; condition (b) is geometric and automatic. The audit
closes at certificate-tier for the 4D effective theory at energies
$E \ll M_{\rm KK}$.

### 17.3.2 Cluster decomposition

Cluster decomposition is the requirement that connected $n$-point
functions factorize when one subset of arguments is taken to spatial
infinity from another. In the 4D effective theory at energies
$E \ll M_{\rm KK}$, cluster decomposition holds by the standard
Wightman-axioms argument: the spectral condition (positive-energy
states only), Lorentz covariance, and the local-action principle
together imply cluster decomposition.

The audit closes at certificate-tier for the 4D effective theory
provided:

(a) The spectral condition holds (no negative-energy physical states;
    no tachyons in the physical spectrum). This is the unitarity audit
    of §17.1, sector by sector.
(b) Lorentz covariance holds. This is automatic in the 4D effective
    theory as long as the §6.4 KK truncation does not introduce a
    Lorentz-violating term, which it does not in the standard
    construction.
(c) The local-action principle of §17.3.1 holds.

All three conditions are met at certificate-tier for the perturbative
4D effective theory at $E \ll M_{\rm KK}$. *Nonperturbative* cluster
decomposition for the strong sector — the requirement that hadronic
scattering amplitudes factorize for spatially separated subsystems —
is the standard QCD result, inherited through UQF-11.

### 17.3.3 13D-to-4D projection consistency

A novel feature of the 13D theory (relative to the SM as a 4D QFT) is
that the locality audit must address the *13D-to-4D projection*
explicitly. Two sub-questions:

(i) **Geometric locality.** Does integration over the compact factors
$K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1$ at each 4D point preserve locality? Yes:
the compact factors are *compact*, so the integration is over a
bounded set at each 4D point, and the result is a local 4D operator
(plus exponentially suppressed non-localities from the KK tower).

(ii) **Kaluza-Klein-induced non-locality.** Do the KK modes, when
integrated out at low energy, produce non-local effective operators
that violate cluster decomposition? No: the KK modes are massive
($M_{\rm KK} \gg E$ at low energy), and integration produces
form-factor-type operators suppressed by $E^2 / M_{\rm KK}^2$. These
are *local* operators in the EFT sense (analytic in momenta around
$p = 0$), and they do not violate cluster decomposition.

The audit closes at certificate-tier for the 4D effective theory at
the §6.4 KK truncation. The full infinite-KK-tower limit is the
UQF-10 question (compactification stability); the present audit
inherits the UQF-10 tier label.

### 17.3.4 Locality violation paths

A locality-violation row triggers when:

- The §5 13D action is not local in 13D (UQF-2 failure). Propagates
  here.
- The §6.4 KK truncation introduces a Lorentz-violating term that
  was not present in the 13D action. This is a UQF-10 failure that
  propagates here.
- A 4D effective operator with non-local structure of size $\geq
  1/M_{\rm KK}$ appears at low energy. Same propagation, UQF-10.
- The spectral condition fails (a tachyon or negative-energy
  physical state appears in the spectrum). This is a UQF-3 / UQF-5 /
  UQF-6 / UQF-8 / UQF-10 failure that propagates here, sector
  by sector.
- A nonperturbative strong-sector amplitude violates cluster
  decomposition. This is a UQF-11 failure that propagates here.

Each path above is *one row*. A row-level violation downgrades the
corresponding UQF row per the §19 final downgrade map.

---

## 17.4 Summary table: per-sector audit status

The table below records the per-sector audit status for the three
properties (unitarity, causality, locality) at the perturbative-plus-
truncated-KK order at which the §§8–11 certificates operate, with
explicit inheritance from the relevant UQF rows.

| Sector | Unitarity (perturbative) | Causality (perturbative) | Locality (4D EFT at $E \ll M_{\rm KK}$) | Nonperturbative inheritance |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Gravity (zero-mode) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-5) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-5) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-2 + UQF-10) | UQF-9 / UQF-10 (Vainshtein / KK) |
| Gravity (KK tower) | CERTIFICATE at finite truncation (UQF-5, UQF-10) | CERTIFICATE per free mode (UQF-5, UQF-10) | CERTIFICATE at finite truncation (UQF-10) | UQF-9 / UQF-10 |
| Strong (perturbative gluons) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-6, BRST/Kugo-Ojima) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-6) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-2) | UQF-11 (Kugo-Ojima color confinement, nonperturbative) |
| Strong (nonperturbative) | AUDIT (UQF-11 inheritance) | AUDIT (UQF-11 inheritance) | AUDIT (UQF-11 inheritance) | Same as UQF-11 |
| Weak ($W^\pm, Z$, perturbative) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-6, UQF-8, Equivalence Theorem) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-6, UQF-8) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-2) | BG-10 *Open / Diagnostic* (EW instantons, sphalerons — Paper 4) |
| Weak (nonperturbative) | AUDIT (BG-10 inheritance) | AUDIT (BG-10 inheritance) | AUDIT (BG-10 inheritance) | BG-10 |
| QED (photon, perturbative) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-6, C-FF8) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-6) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-2) | UQF-9 (Landau pole) |
| Higgs (UQF-8) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-8) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-8) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-2) | UQF-9 (Higgs self-coupling at UV scale) |
| Fermion (UQF-7) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-7, spin-statistics) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-7) | CERTIFICATE (UQF-2) | None additional beyond UQF-11 (for confined quark species) |

Every perturbative-sector row closes at CERTIFICATE-tier. The
nonperturbative-sector rows inherit the tier label of the
corresponding UQF row (UQF-9, UQF-10, UQF-11, or BG-10 for the EW
nonperturbative-instanton row that lives in Paper 4).

---

## 17.5 Falsification path summary (unitarity / causality / locality)

A row of §17.1.3, §17.2.2, or §17.4 falsifies when:

- **Unitarity falsification.** A negative-norm physical state is found
  in any sector's spectrum; or the BRST charge fails to be nilpotent
  at some loop order; or longitudinal $W, Z$ scattering is not
  unitarized by the Higgs in §10. Each propagates to UQF-3 / UQF-4 /
  UQF-8 respectively, and triggers the §19 downgrade ladder.
- **Causality falsification.** A field's commutator fails to vanish
  outside the lightcone; or a tachyonic mode appears under §6.10
  loop corrections; or the Froissart bound is violated by KK-tower
  exchange at high energy; or gravitational-wave propagation deviates
  from $c_g = c$ beyond the GW170817+GRB170817A constraint. Each
  propagates to UQF-5 / UQF-6 / UQF-8 / UQF-10 / UQF-9 respectively.
- **Locality falsification.** The §5 13D action is not local in 13D
  (UQF-2 failure); or the §6.4 KK truncation introduces a
  Lorentz-violating term (UQF-10 failure); or a 4D effective operator
  with non-local structure of size $\geq 1/M_{\rm KK}$ appears at low
  energy (UQF-10 failure); or cluster decomposition fails (UQF-3 /
  UQF-11 failure depending on sector).

Each falsifier above is *one row* of one upstream UQF gate. The present
section *inherits* failures; it does not introduce its own downgrade
vocabulary. A failure propagates to the §19 final downgrade map and
the corresponding UQF row's status drops per the §3 downgrade ladder.

---

## 17.6 What this section claims and what it does not

This closing subsection of the unitarity/causality/locality audit separates the certificate-tier claims from the audit-tier ones explicitly, so the chapter cannot be read as claiming more than it earns. The subsections list what is claimed at CERTIFICATE tier (§17.6.1), what stays at AUDIT — chiefly the above-cutoff unitarity that is conditional on the UV-completion certificate of §14 — and the falsifiers attached to each.

### 17.6.1 Claimed (CERTIFICATE-tier)

- Perturbative S-matrix unitarity for each force sector at the
  truncated-KK order of §6.4, inherited from BRST cohomology of UQF-4
  and physical-Hilbert-space positivity of UQF-3.
- Microcausality of each free-field force carrier in the 4D effective
  theory, inherited from textbook free-field commutators / anticommutators
  for the carriers of §§8–11.
- Locality of the 4D effective action at energies $E \ll M_{\rm KK}$,
  inherited from the local 13D action of UQF-2 and the geometric
  compactness of $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1$.
- No-superluminal-signaling in the recovered Einstein limit,
  consistent with GW170817+GRB170817A.

### 17.6.2 Not claimed (AUDIT-tier or *Open / Diagnostic*)

- Full nonperturbative unitarity for the strong sector. This is
  inherited from UQF-11 and routes to the Clay Millennium Yang-Mills
  problem; the §17 audit does not upgrade it.
- Full nonperturbative causality under graviton self-coupling. This
  is inherited from UQF-9 / UQF-10 and routes to the open question
  of quantum gravity UV completion; the §17 audit does not upgrade
  it.
- Full cluster decomposition with the infinite KK tower retained.
  This is inherited from UQF-10 and routes to compactification
  stability; the §17 audit does not upgrade it.
- Nonperturbative EW unitarity (instantons, sphalerons, baryon-
  number violation at high temperature). This is excluded by the
  hard claim boundary of UQFC-1 and routes to Paper 4's BG-10
  diagnostic discussion; the §17 audit inherits *Open / Diagnostic*.
- Any vacuum-energy / cosmological-constant cancellation as a by-product
  of high-energy completion. The §17 high-energy unitarity inherits from
  UQF-9 / UQF-10, and the corpus has settled the Λ line as a **computed
  honest fail** (TOE_FINAL v12 supertrace FAIL at every coefficient order;
  v14 chamber route THEOREM_REFUTED — Λ operator = unit operator; Λ stays
  Weinberg-open as a computed certificate; EXTERNAL, §11). The §17 audit
  therefore neither claims nor implies a Λ-cancellation mechanism.

### 17.6.3 Anti-overclaim reminder

The §17 audit is *structural discipline*, not a deep proof. Where
standard QFT supports the property, the audit closes at certificate-tier;
where it does not, the audit *names the gap* and routes to the
corresponding UQF row. The full nonperturbative unitarity question is
*open at the same level as QCD nonperturbative* — a Clay Millennium
problem — and the §17 audit does not claim to have solved it. The
honest framing of the unified-force quantum-completion claim, per the
hard claim boundary of UQFC-1, is that the *force sectors are
interface-complete and quantum-completable at the structural level
the §§5–15 certificates discharge*, not that every conceivable
nonperturbative subtlety is resolved.

---
