# UQFC-19B — The Geometry Is Not Abstract: Its Chamber Builds a Quantum Computer

> **Status of this section, for the record.** An EXTERNAL engineering bridge at **SIMULATED** (engineering) grade. It makes **no new physics claim** and changes **no UQF status** in §3 or §19. Zero promotions. The QC corpus (the Tahoe Labs error-correction design package and its `SIMULATION_CAMPAIGN` / `GATE_CLOSURE` evidence) is EXTERNAL and registered here once; nothing in it is reproduced or modified by this document, and nothing in it moves a single UQF row. No geometry is changed (MR-6 QC-ratio test: N/A — this section *reports* a pre-existing engineering artifact; it alters no manifold, coset, radius, or code distance in this paper).

**Why this section exists (plain).** Every certificate in this paper asks you to believe that a particular six-dimensional shape — $K_6 = SU(3)/U(1)^2$, the squashed flag manifold whose isometries §9 quantizes into the gluon, weak-boson, and photon certificates — is *physically real*: the actual internal geometry of the world, not a convenient piece of mathematics. There is a way to test whether a geometry is real that has nothing to do with particle physics: **try to build something with it.** A shape that is merely a bookkeeping device cannot be machined into a working device; a shape that is real can. The same $K_6$ coset that this paper's force-sector certificates are built on also defines the *admissibility chamber* of a quantum-error-correction architecture that has been designed and simulated on standard open-source tools. This section records that bridge at its honest engineering grade — neither more nor less — because a force-sector theory whose geometry earns its keep in a buildable machine has crossed from formalism into engineering.

**Why this section exists (precise).** The bridge is structural, not metaphorical. This paper's quantization of the gauge sector (§9) projects the physical gauge states out of the $K_6$ isometry content — it *admits* the active polarizations and *rejects* the unphysical modes via the BRST/quartet mechanism (§6.4). The error-correction architecture is built on the identical operation in a different register: it admits one eigenspace of a coset-defined operator and rejects the rest (technically, the $+1$ eigenspace of a Heisenberg–Weyl / holonomy stabilizer subgroup, and its complement). *Admit one eigenspace of a coset-defined operator, reject the rest* is the same mathematical move in both places — and in the QC case it has been written as runnable code and exercised against a decoder.

## 19B.1 The shared object: one chamber, two uses

| The same structural idea | In this paper (force-sector quantization) | In the QC architecture (sibling corpus, EXTERNAL) |
|---|---|---|
| The host geometry | $K_6 = SU(3)/U(1)^2$ flag manifold — the active internal space (§2.1.1, §15.3) | The $K_6 = SU(3)/U(1)^2$ chamber of the code's stabilizer layer (the same coset; the design's "chamber") |
| The admit/reject operation | BRST cohomology + quartet projection admit the physical gauge/graviton states, reject the negative-norm and Goldstone modes (§6, §9) | Admit the $+1$ eigenspace of the stabilizer subgroup, reject the complement (the admittance algebra) |
| What it controls | Which polarizations are physical — the gauge-boson certificates (§9) and the spin-2 graviton (§8) | Which logical states are protected — the code's admissible subspace |
| The selectivity number | The per-boson polarization counts (2 transverse; 2+1 for the massive $W^\pm/Z^0$) that the certificate must reproduce | The chamber's admitted-fraction / selectivity (the figure that drives the qubit budget) |

The point is not an analogy. It is that the *same coset and the same admit-one-eigenspace-reject-the-rest operation* appear in both, and in the QC case the operation has been implemented and run.

## 19B.2 What has actually been built and simulated (honest engineering grade)

The following are recorded at **engineering grade** — the grade of a *simulated design*, not of a fabricated and measured chip, and explicitly *not* at this paper's certificate grade. Each carries its status label:

- **The chamber concept is validated in simulation (SIMULATED).** The admissibility-chamber projector is implemented and exercised; the four-layer error-correction stack it sits in (GKP + chamber + surface + modular) runs end-to-end, and the simulation suite executes cleanly — `verify_campaign.py` exits 0 with its core checks PASS on live re-runs (SIMULATED; EXTERNAL, the QC corpus).
- **The design is locally simulatable today (SIMULATED).** The toolchain is open-source and installed — Stim + PyMatching (stabilizer simulation and decoding), QuTiP and scqubits (the bosonic / transmon layer), with EM parasitic extraction verified. The architecture is not slideware; it is exercised against a real decoder at ~$10^8$ shots.
- **The honest overhead floor is competitive, not heroic (BOUNDED).** The design's physical-to-logical memory overhead at scale sits in a **~9.6–14.5** band (BOUNDED, SIMULATED), with a **robust fallback of 3.24** as the conservative four-layer figure (BOUNDED). This is competitive in the specific sense that the ~9.6–14.5 band sits against IBM's qLDPC memory overhead of ~24:1 (EXTERNAL) — and it is explicitly a **memory floor**, not a full-algorithm ratio. The formerly-quoted sub-2 ratios are **retired** — they were an algebra-clamp artifact and a single-module figure, withdrawn on the record (see the self-caught discipline below). No sub-2 ratio is claimed anywhere in this document.
- **The decoder advantage is real and survived audit (SIMULATED).** The biased-noise advantage of the deformed code was tested with a genuine Hadamard-deformed XZZX circuit in Stim with a deterministic observable; the design operates **below threshold at its operating point** (SIMULATED), with a measured single-logical biased **decoder-channel advantage (not a memory-overhead ratio) of ~8.4× (CI 4.2–16.9)** on the decoded logical channel.

## 19B.3 Why the engineering discipline is itself the evidence

The reason to trust the bridge is the same reason to trust the physics in this paper: **the QC program caught and reversed its own optimistic errors, and got more credible for it** — exactly the discipline this paper applies when it checks the most tempting AUDIT row (strong CP) and leaves it open (§11.3). The honest-discipline record carries at least **seven self-caught corrections**:

1. **A "4.3×" decoder gain was REVERSED** when a real decoded simulation showed it was an undecoded raw-syndrome artifact; the honest decoded figure (~8.4×, CI 4.2–16.9) actually *vindicated* the original conservative claim (SIMULATED).
2. **A $d \geq 8$ classical-signaling claim was DOWNGRADED** to PAM-8-plus-parity once it was proven (with the `galois` library) that the construction was the kernel of a GF(2) parity check — the coset advantage survives only in the coherent quantum embodiment, and the design says so (REFUTED-class, recorded).
3. **An SU(N) selectivity escalator was LOWERED** when the admitted fraction was shown to scale as $1/(N+1)$ — *decreasing* with rank, not increasing (the inconvenient direction, recorded).
4. **The design is recorded as FAILING the Shor-2048 error budget even at an idealized unit ratio** — a floor ratio is not a runnable algorithm, and the program writes that limitation down rather than burying it (recorded).
5. **Several off-topic engineering estimates were also walked back in public** — a 15–25% thermal-via benefit lowered to ~6.5% once an FEM solver included the spreading resistance; a 91% lever-success model corrected to a decision-grade ~12.6%; a circuit time-constant that was 1000× off (1 ns vs the correct 1 ps) found and fixed (each SIMULATED / BOUNDED, recorded).

Each of these is a place the engineering corpus made its own claim *weaker* in public. That is the same instrument as this paper's status discipline — the min-rule headline, the AUDIT rows shipped as AUDIT, the verified-and-left-open strong-CP row — and it is why the chamber bridge is offered as evidence rather than decoration: **a program that audits itself this hard, in two independent domains, is showing its work.**

## 19B.4 What §19B does and does not license

| It licenses (the honest reading) | It does NOT license (the forbidden over-read) |
|---|---|
| "The $K_6$ chamber idea is concrete enough to implement and simulate" | "The QC ratio makes the force-sector completion correct" — it does not, and no such inference is drawn; §19B changes no UQF status |
| "The geometry has a working engineering application at simulated grade" | "The design is a fabricated, measured device" — it is simulated, not built in silicon |
| "The same self-audit discipline governs both corpora" | "The retired sub-2 ratios are real" — they are withdrawn, and appear nowhere as claims |
| "An independent domain finds the chamber structure useful" | Any feedback from QC numbers into the physics claims — barred (no-target-loading) |

The standing geometry-change discipline (MR-6) is the mirror image of this section: any future geometry move in the corpus must answer *"would it lower the physical:logical qubit ratio at 10,000 logical qubits?"* — a gate that exists **precisely because the geometry is shared**, so a change made to flatter the physics could silently harm the machine, and vice versa. §19B is that gate's positive face: the record that, used forward, the geometry *builds* something. The force-sector certificates of §§8–13 and the engineering chamber of this section answer to **one** geometry, and that is the strongest reason to take the geometry seriously.

## 19B.5 — Test it yourself (by hand or with any AI): five prompts

*These five checks are corpus-level — they span Papers 1–3, and most resolve against the sibling manuscripts named in each prompt. They split into two kinds, and the kind controls what a green check is allowed to mean. **Prompts 1–3 are Type-A: they must return the same answer with or without the construction's geometry** — the geometry only re-labels the textbook ledger object-for-object, and it does **not** claim to replace general relativity or Maxwell. **Prompts 4–5 are Type-B: they check the geometry's free-parameter outputs against data** ($\delta_{\rm CKM}$ and the generation count are genuine Standard-Model free parameters the SM cannot derive), and a sub-$1\sigma$ match is consistency-with-data only — a non-falsification, never a confirmation. They raise no gate tier; Σ = AUDIT is unchanged (§3.4.4, §19B.4). The anomaly check (Prompt 1) is native-adjacent (the cubic rows are worked in this paper); the other four resolve against the sibling papers and say so. The two in-doc free-field checks of the front-matter fast-check box are the by-hand grade of this same instrument; the prompts below are its reproducible cross-corpus grade. Each prompt is copy-paste-ready into a calculator or any competent AI, and each carries a two-column **confirms / does-not-show** reading so a result can never be over-read into a confirmation of the theory itself.*

**Prompt 1 — One-line anomaly cancellation (Type A; native-adjacent — the cubic rows are worked here, the linear witness is Paper 1).**
> You are a particle physicist checking gauge-anomaly cancellation by hand for one Standard Model generation. Take the quarks of one generation: a color-triplet left-handed quark doublet (multiplicity 3 from color) of weak-hypercharge $Y = +1/6$, and the left-handed lepton doublet of $Y = -1/2$. For the mixed SU(2)²–U(1) (and gravitational–U(1)) anomaly, the relevant trace over the left-handed weak doublets is the sum of their hypercharges weighted by multiplicity. Compute $3\cdot(1/6) + (-1/2)$ and state whether it vanishes. Show the one line.

*Expected:* $3\cdot(1/6) - 1/2 = 0$. This paper works the SU(3)³ and $\Sigma Y^3$ **cubic** anomaly rows (§7 / the object-ledger Row 5 anomaly accounting); the one-line SU(2)²–U(1) **linear** witness above is Paper 1, `Fable_GUT_merged.md` Appendix E′ (Gate 5). The geometry earns the pass only by producing the right particle list — anomaly cancellation is *inherited, not arranged*.
| It confirms (Type A) | It does NOT show |
|---|---|
| The geometry's particle content balances the anomaly ledger exactly — consistency with the Standard Model's own cancellation | That the geometry is the *sole* origin of the SM list (it is one of six anomaly ledgers; the full set incl. the mod-2 Witten condition is in Paper 1 Appendix E′) |

**Prompt 2 — Charged-shell field energy (Type A; sibling — Paper 1 Appendix O).**
> You are a careful physicist with a calculator. A thin spherical shell carries total charge $Q = 1.00000$ C at radius $R_s = 5.00000$ m. Two concentric Gaussian surfaces sit at $r_1 = 1.00000$ m and $r_2 = 10.0000$ m. Using only standard Einstein–Maxwell electrostatics, compute the electromagnetic field energy stored in the spherical region between $r_1$ and $r_2$, with the field given by the vacuum Coulomb law $E(r) = Q/(4\pi\varepsilon_0 r^2)$ for $r > R_s$ and zero for $r < R_s$, energy density $u = \varepsilon_0 E^2/2$, and $\varepsilon_0 = 8.8541878128\times10^{-12}$ F/m. Give the result to six significant figures in joules, then state the closed form you used.

*Expected:* $U_{\rm EM} = 4.49378\times10^{8}$ J, from $U = \dfrac{Q^2}{8\pi\varepsilon_0}\left(\dfrac{1}{R_s} - \dfrac{1}{r_2}\right)$. Check: $Q^2/(8\pi\varepsilon_0) = 4.49378\times10^{9}$ J·m; $(1/5 - 1/10) = 0.100000$; product $= 4.49378\times10^{8}$ J. Sibling: `Fable_GUT_merged.md` Appendix O.4 (equivalence table), O.5 Case B; the geometry side (Appendix O.3 ×,⊕,⊗ ledger) returns the identical digits because it re-labels region/rulebook/actors, it does not change the physics. **Guardrail: do not back out a mass-equivalent and compare to a $\Delta m$ quoted elsewhere — that $5.00079\times10^{-9}$ figure is a round-then-square artifact; the falsifiable claim is $U_{\rm EM}$ to six figures only.**
| It confirms (Type A) | It does NOT show |
|---|---|
| The 13D ×,⊕,⊗ machinery reproduces the textbook field-energy ledger object-for-object — equivalence, not new physics | That the framework replaces general relativity or Maxwell (it explicitly does not — Paper 1 Appendix O.7) |

**Prompt 3 — Weak-field reductions to Newton and Coulomb (Type A; sibling — Paper 2).**
> You are a physicist auditing whether a higher-dimensional unification proposal reproduces textbook low-energy physics. (a) For gravity: state the weak-field, slow-motion (Newtonian) limit of general relativity as a field equation for the gravitational potential $\Phi$ sourced by mass density $\rho$, with Newton's constant $G$. (b) For electrostatics: state Gauss's law in differential form and the resulting Coulomb field of a point charge $Q$ in vacuum. Write both standard results explicitly.

*Expected:* (a) $\nabla^2\Phi = 4\pi G\rho$ (equivalently the linearized $\nabla^2 h_{00} = -8\pi G\rho$, native at **§8.5** of this paper); (b) $\nabla\cdot\mathbf E = \rho/\varepsilon_0$, giving $E = Q/(4\pi\varepsilon_0 r^2)$ — the Coulomb/Gauss leg in `Fable_Forces_merged.md` §9.6. The geometry claims only that its 4D effective Einstein–Hilbert sector and composite QED projection *land on these same equations*.
| It confirms (Type A) | It does NOT show |
|---|---|
| The construction recovers the exact Newtonian and electrostatic limits — a necessary consistency check passed | That it *replaces* GR or solves the full / nonperturbative regimes (scoped out, C-FF12); the gravity leg is conditional on the volume-modulus freeze (soft spot WL-1) |

**Prompt 4 — CKM CP phase (Type B: an SM free parameter, checked for consistency with data; sibling Paper 1).**
> You are a flavor physicist. The Standard Model does not predict the CKM CP-violating phase $\delta_{\rm CKM}$ (equivalently the unitarity-triangle angle $\gamma$); it is a free parameter fixed only by measurement. (1) Confirm that in the Standard Model this phase is an input, not a derived quantity. (2) Given a theoretical proposal that the phase emerges from an order-three geometric holonomy equal to $-2\pi/3 = -120°$ (raw), which after the standard Wolfenstein phase-convention alignment corresponds to a compared value of $+60.0°$, evaluate the consistency of $+60.0°$ against the measured PDG value of $65.5°$ for $\gamma$. Report the discrepancy in units of the experimental standard deviation (the "pull"), assuming roughly 10% structural precision on the prediction, and state whether $+60.0°$ is consistent with data at that level.

*Expected:* the SM genuinely cannot derive $\delta_{\rm CKM}$. Geometry value: **raw holonomy $-2\pi/3 = -120°$; Wolfenstein-aligned $+60.0°$**, compared to PDG $65.5°$ → pull $(65.5 - 60.0)/\sigma$ with $\sigma \approx 6\text{–}7°$ at 10% structural precision → **0.79σ**. Sibling: `Fable_GUT_merged.md` §7.6 table and Appendix I / Appendix J. **Guardrail: the *raw* holonomy is $-120°$, and only the *Wolfenstein-aligned* $+60.0°$ is the quantity compared to PDG; quoting $-120°$ against $65.5°$ would be a false ~185° "mismatch."**
| It confirms (Type B) | It does NOT show |
|---|---|
| $+60.0°$ vs $65.5°$ is sub-1σ agreement — non-falsification of a genuine SM free parameter at the stated precision | A *confirmation* of the theory — a null result would have been a falsifier, but a sub-1σ pull is consistency-with-data only, never a verdict that the theory is right |

**Prompt 5 — Exactly three generations (Type B: an SM free parameter, checked for consistency with data; sibling Paper 1, inherited not re-derived here).**
> You are a model-building physicist. (1) Confirm that the Standard Model does not explain why there are exactly three generations of matter — the number 3 is an empirical input, not derived from SM principles. (2) A theoretical proposal obtains the generation number as a topological index (a spin-ℂ / Borel–Weil–Bott index on the internal flag manifold $K_6 = SU(3)/U(1)^2$, evaluating to $-3$, i.e. three chiral families), an integer that cannot be continuously tuned. Treating the family count as fixed by topology rather than by hand, verify that the value "exactly three" is consistent with experiment: state what the LEP measurement of the number of light neutrino species ($N_\nu \approx 2.984 \pm 0.008$ from the $Z$ invisible width) and the absence of fourth-generation discoveries imply about the allowed number of standard chiral generations.

*Expected:* the SM does not predict the generation count (genuine unexplained fact). Geometry: topological index $\chi(K_6,\mathcal{E}) = -3$ → exactly three chiral families, forced (not a dial). Consistency anchor: LEP $N_\nu \approx 2.984 \pm 0.008$ and no fourth generation; the index-changing line-bundle deformation that would give two or four families is excluded by the LEP $N_\nu$ bound. Sibling: `Fable_GUT_merged.md` §1.3 / §3.4 and Objection 4 there; per §11.5.3 of this paper the generation count is **inherited from Paper 1, not re-derived here**.
| It confirms (Type B) | It does NOT show |
|---|---|
| The index value $-3$ → three chiral families is consistent with the observed count (LEP $N_\nu \approx 3$, no fourth generation) — non-falsification of a genuine SM free parameter | That nature *must* have three; minimality holds only inside the declared search category, and a reviewer who supplies a natural excluded competitor triggers a documented downgrade to category-relative diagnostic |

# THE STRONGEST OBJECTIONS, ANSWERED

*Plain.* A serious reviewer arrives with serious objections, and a paper that ducks them earns nothing. So here are the five strongest objections a hostile expert raises against a programme like this one — each stated **at full force first**, in the form its sharpest critic would use, and only then answered, by pointing at the exact place in this document where the claim → mechanism → certificate → falsifier chain already lives. No objection below is softened before it is answered; where the answer is partial, it says so.

**Objection 1 — "The gate stack is circular. If you wrote every chapter to satisfy a gate template, of course the chapters pass the gates."**
*Stated at full force:* a self-graded exam is no exam. A seventeen-row checklist that the author both writes and scores tests nothing but the author's diligence at filling in boxes.
*Answered:* this is answered in the paper's own currency, because the gates carry **tiers, and tiers are earned, not declared** (§9, the inversion). Writing a chapter to a row's template buys at most INTERFACE; climbing to CANDIDATE or CERTIFICATE requires a named, frozen argument meeting the row's pass/fail criterion, and **eight rows of this very paper sit at AUDIT** — visible proof the construction did not pre-pay them. The rows are coupled (§3.4.2): an anomaly failure drags five rows down a tier, losing UV completion strips CERTIFICATE from four, so satisfying each template separately still owes the joint conditions on one Hilbert space. And the honest-status rule (§3.4.4) makes any aggregate sentence stronger than the computed minimum a drafting bug **by definition** — the public standard for judging *is* the private standard for building.

**Objection 2 — "AUDIT is just a polite word for 'we haven't done it.' You are shipping a to-do list and calling it a result."**
*Stated at full force:* a tier label is not a theorem. Calling a sector AUDIT rather than OPEN dresses an unsolved problem in procedural clothing without solving anything.
*Answered:* correct that AUDIT is not a certificate — and the paper **routes every AUDIT row to the top** (§19, the falsification map; the §10 scoreboard) rather than hiding it. But AUDIT here is precisely defined, not a hedge: it means a gate has a *draft argument and a named falsification surface with at least one open dependency* (§3.2.3), which is strictly more than OPEN — the dependency is named, the falsifier is attached, and the row states what would raise it. The difference between AUDIT and CANDIDATE is a specific listed object (a positivity proof on the interacting sector, an anomaly lift under 4D descent, a UV fixed point), not a mood. A to-do list with a falsifier on every line, an owner, and a min-rule that forbids over-claiming is an evidence chain, not a wish.

**Objection 3 — "You left strong CP open. The most elegant thing your geometry could have done, and you didn't do it — so the elegance is decorative."**
*Stated at full force:* strong CP is the showcase test for a geometric theory of forces. Leaving $\bar\theta$-smallness underived, after building so much structure, suggests the structure does not actually constrain the hard cases.
*Answered:* the paper does **not** claim to solve strong CP, and says so without flinching — UQF-12 is *"a candidate and a falsifier, not a solution"* (§3.2.2, §11.3). What it offers is narrower and labeled: a named structural mechanism (the $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ boundary-parity lead) with a **named falsification surface** (the 1.64-rad spin-c-holonomy locus) and a live experimental adjudicator (the nEDM bound), all at AUDIT (LOW confidence). The credibility-building move is that this was the *single most tempting row to "complete"* — and it was checked against the live corpus and **deliberately left open** (§11.3, the load-bearing proof of an honest reconciliation: $\bar\theta$-smallness is honestly underived, nEDM probes it). A programme that declines to overclaim on the exact row where overclaiming would be most rewarded is showing you its discipline, not its weakness.

**Objection 4 — "The quantum-computer bridge is a parlor trick. The same coset appearing in a code is a coincidence dressed up as a proof, and the machine is simulated, not built."**
*Stated at full force:* using the same letters ($K_6$) in two places is not a physical argument. A simulation is not a chip, and an analogy is not evidence that the internal geometry is real.
*Answered:* the bridge is offered at exactly its honest grade — **EXTERNAL, SIMULATED, zero promotions, changing no UQF status** (§19B) — and the answer is structural, not lexical. The shared object is not the *name* $K_6$ but the *operation*: BRST cohomology admits the physical gauge polarizations and rejects the negative-norm and Goldstone modes (§6, §9); the code's admittance algebra admits the $+1$ eigenspace of a coset-defined stabilizer and rejects its complement (§19B.1). *Admit one eigenspace of a coset-defined operator, reject the rest* is the identical move, and in the QC case it has been written as runnable code and exercised against a real decoder at $\sim10^8$ shots (SIMULATED). On the "simulated, not built" point the paper agrees in its own table (§19B.4): it licenses *"the geometry has a working engineering application at simulated grade,"* and explicitly forbids *"the design is a fabricated, measured device."* The honest claim is a buildable, simulated design on open tools — and the no-target-loading rule (§19B.4) bars any QC number from ever feeding back into the physics.

**Objection 5 — "Almost everything here is AUDIT or CANDIDATE. This is a research programme, not a theory of quantum forces."**
*Stated at full force:* the scoreboard's own counts (§10) show eight of seventeen rows at AUDIT and the aggregate at AUDIT. That is a long way from a closed quantum theory of the forces.
*Answered:* the counts are stated **by the paper, in its own front-page table** (§10) — the objection is quoting the document's honesty back at it, which is the system working. The reframing that matters: this paper never claimed to *close* the quantum-force question; it claims, in its first sentence (§1.0), a force-sector unified-quantum-completion **audit**, at the tier the weakest gate admits, with TOE-scale questions walled off to Paper 4 by name. Within that declared scope the closed-and-candidate load is not small: active-branch inheritance at CERTIFICATE, the nine-row object ledger, three-formulation framework equivalence on the perturbative overlap, a positive-norm physical Hilbert space for the retained sector, the linearized graviton and gauge-boson and tree-level Higgs certificates, and the self-applying downgrade map are each banked at CANDIDATE or CERTIFICATE (§10, §20). A paper that labeled all seventeen rows "closed" would be the thing to distrust; one that closes what it can, conditions what it can gate, and ships the rest *at AUDIT with the experiment or calculation that settles each* is showing its evidence chain — which is exactly what the §10 scoreboard and the §19 map record.

*The takeaway is:* none of these five objections is answered by assertion; each is answered by a pointer to a banked certificate, a named gate, a labeled tier, or a pre-registered falsifier already in this document. That is the difference between a paper asking to be believed and one inviting you to check.


---


# UQFC-20 — Conclusion
> **Status-preservation declaration.** This section does not edit C-FF0..C-FF14, does not modify the hard-gate vector, does not litigate BG-10, and does not edit any frozen artifact. The per-row closure status of UQF-0..UQF-16 is taken from §3.4.3 (per-row tier ledger) and from each row's own section (§§4–19); §20 does not over-write or upgrade any per-row tier. "Chris does the physics" — the conclusion organizes the existing certificate stack into a single status statement and a single forward-looking work plan, and does not invent any new physics result.

---

## 20.1 Summary — what Paper 3 attempts and what it does not

**Paper 3 ships at AUDIT on purpose: it ran four forces through seventeen gates and prints its weakest link — not its best result — as the headline. That is the whole discipline in one line, and the rest of this conclusion is the accounting behind it.** Where it sits in the four-paper hierarchy is fixed in the front matter and §20.5; here the question is only what the audit found.

The question this paper attempts is *narrower than TOE* and *broader than Paper 2's interface compatibility*: it asks whether the four force-sector interfaces of Paper 2 — gravity, the strong force, the weak force, and QED — admit quantum-completion *as force theories*. The 17-gate UQF stack UQF-0..UQF-16 of §3 is the certificate spine that polices every claim made on that question; §§4–19 are the per-gate certificate writeups; §20 is the aggregate status statement and the work-plan toward higher-tier closure.

What this paper claims, under declared assumptions and at the per-row tier admitted by §§4–19:

- **Active-branch inheritance.** The same active branch $\mathfrak B_{\rm active}$ of Paper 1 is used everywhere; no implicit branch substitution occurs. (UQF-0; §2.1.)
- **Quantum object ledger.** Every quantized object in the paper traces back to a row of the §4 ledger (9 rows: $G_{\mu\nu}, G_{\mu A}, G_{AB}, A_\mu^a, \Psi, H$, KK tower, ghosts, antifields). (UQF-1; §4.)
- **Quantization framework.** Canonical, BV-BRST, and path-integral formulations are written down and shown equivalent on the perturbative / linearised / KK-zero-mode + low-KK overlap. (UQF-2; §5.)
- **Physical Hilbert space.** A positive-norm physical Hilbert space exists, by BRST cohomology and the Kugo-Ojima quartet mechanism, for the retained 4D zero-mode + low-KK perturbative sector. (UQF-3; §6.)
- **Anomaly and measure closure.** Ten of sixteen distinct anomaly classes close at CERTIFICATE tier by inheritance from the Paper 1 SM anomaly ledger and the textbook even/odd-dimension rules; five are AUDIT-with-roadmap; one (coset-twist) is OPEN-with-pathway. (UQF-4; §7.)
- **Graviton.** A linearised, two-helicity, positive-norm, massless spin-2 graviton is extracted from $G_{\mu\nu}$ with universal $T^{\mu\nu}$ coupling and Newtonian / Einstein-Hilbert IR. (UQF-5; §8.)
- **Gauge bosons.** Eight massless gluons (perturbative), three massive $W^\pm, Z$ at tree level after EW breaking, and one massless transverse photon with $Q = T_3 + Y$ matter coupling. (UQF-6; §9.)
- **Higgs / Goldstone.** Physical Higgs separated from three eaten Goldstones at tree level; $m_W = gv/2$, $m_Z = \sqrt{g^2+g'^2}\,v/2$, $\rho = 1$. (UQF-8; §10.)
- **Chiral fermions.** One generation of left-handed Weyl fermions per family, three families from the $K_6$ spin-c index, no surviving mirror partners, anomaly closure inherited. (UQF-7; §11.)

What this paper does **not** claim:

- **Not a Theory of Everything.** Cosmology, dark matter, dark energy, baryogenesis (BG-10), initial conditions, the measurement problem, the emergence of classicality, and "why this universe" all defer to Paper 4.
- **Not a certificate of all force physics.** Nonperturbative QCD remains a Clay Millennium open problem; strong CP carries LOW-confidence candidate status; UV completion is audit-tier with a partner FRG calculation deliverable named but not performed.
- **Not a gate-upgrade for Paper 1 or Paper 2.** No C-FF row is modified; no Paper 1 freeze record is re-litigated; no hard-gate is upgraded or downgraded.
- **Not a baryogenesis or cosmology claim.** BG-10 = *Open / Diagnostic* is preserved without modification; it is Paper 4 reserve material.

The honest summary: Paper 3 is a *candidate unified quantum-force completion at AUDIT tier under declared assumptions*, with structurally complete certificate machinery for every row, perturbative-and-tree-level closures for the matter-and-force-carrier rows, and named research paths for every row whose tier is below CERTIFICATE.

## 20.2 Per-gate status table (UQF-0..UQF-16)

The table consolidates the per-gate tier from each section's own status statement. The tier ladder is the §3.2.3 ladder: $\mathrm{INTERFACE} < \mathrm{AUDIT} < \mathrm{CANDIDATE} < \mathrm{CERTIFICATE}$.

| Gate | Name | Source section | Current tier | Most consequential open item |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| **UQF-0** | Active-branch inheritance | §2.1 | **CERTIFICATE** | (none; held by inheritance discipline) |
| **UQF-1** | Quantum object ledger | §4 | **CANDIDATE** | Phase-2 consumption of every row at CERTIFICATE-tier |
| **UQF-2** | Canonical / path-integral equivalence | §5 | **CERTIFICATE** (textbook on overlap region; AUDIT for nonpert) | Constructive interacting 13D positivity (UQF-3 / UQF-9 cross) |
| **UQF-3** | Physical Hilbert space | §6 | **CANDIDATE** (CERTIFICATE on retained 4D zero + low-KK perturbative sector) | Full interacting positivity (Clay-class, 4D Yang-Mills) |
| **UQF-4** | BRST/BV nilpotency + anomaly closure | §7 | **AUDIT-with-named-roadmap** (10 CERT / 5 AUDIT / 1 OPEN) | Coset-twist anomaly (row 17), 3-step pathway named |
| **UQF-5** | Graviton certificate | §8 | **CANDIDATE** linearised (UQF-5A/B CERTIFICATE; UQF-5C AUDIT / DEFERRED) | UV completion + interacting positivity (routed to §14, §15) |
| **UQF-6** | Gauge-boson certificates | §9 | **CANDIDATE** per sub-row at perturbative level | Nonpert QCD for gluons; full EW precision for $W/Z$; Landau pole for photon |
| **UQF-7** | Fermion quantization | §11 | **AUDIT** (UQF-7A–F CERTIFICATE; UQF-7G AUDIT on neutrino mechanism) | Neutrino mass mechanism (Paper 1 Appendix K) |
| **UQF-8** | Higgs / Goldstone / vacuum | §10 | **CANDIDATE** tree-level (UQF-8A CERTIFICATE; UQF-8B AUDIT; UQF-8C DEFERRED) | Wilson-line origin closure (Paper 1 Appendix H); radiative-stability under 13D KK |
| **UQF-9** | UV-completion certificate | §14 | **AUDIT** with structured certificate sketch | One partner FRG calculation on FRG-1 (asymptotic-safety) |
| **UQF-10** | Quantum compactification stability | §15 | **AUDIT** with declared truncation (3 CERT-within-truncation / 4 AUDIT) | Volume-modulus runaway (S-7); most consequential cross-link to §6.9.3a |

| **UQF-12** | Strong CP | §13 | **AUDIT** LOW-confidence on candidate (Path α / β / γ branch) | $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ boundary-parity propagation to $\arg\det M_q$ |
| **UQF-13** | Precision-force phenomenology | §16 | **CANDIDATE** (Tier-1 framework CERTIFICATE / Tier-2 numerics AUDIT) | $m_W$ tension; proton-decay channel predictions |

| **UQF-15** | No-hidden-sector force leakage | §18 | **AUDIT** (every experimental bound satisfied by inheritance) | Most-likely falsifier is precision-EW $m_W$ tension |
| **UQF-16** | Final downgrade map | §19 | **CERTIFICATE** for map structure (meta-rule) | (none; map is complete) |

Three rows close at CERTIFICATE in the strict §3.2.3 ladder sense (UQF-0, UQF-2 on the overlap region, UQF-16 for map structure). Six rows are at CANDIDATE (UQF-1, UQF-3, UQF-5, UQF-6, UQF-8, UQF-13). Eight rows are at AUDIT (UQF-4, UQF-7, UQF-9, UQF-10, UQF-11, UQF-12, UQF-14, UQF-15). Zero rows are FAILED or OPEN at the strict §3.2.3 ladder; one anomaly sub-row (row 17 coset-twist) is OPEN-with-pathway *inside* UQF-4's audit, but does not by itself force UQF-4 below AUDIT.

The visible distribution is therefore: **3 CERTIFICATE + 6 CANDIDATE + 8 AUDIT + 0 FAILED.**

---

## 20.3 Min-rule outcome — $\Sigma(\mathrm{UQFC})$

Per §3.4.3 the aggregate-tier rule is

$$
\Sigma(\mathrm{UQFC}) \;=\; \min_{k \in \{0,1,\ldots,16\}} \;\sigma_k,
$$

where $\sigma_k$ is the per-row tier of UQF-$k$ on the ladder $\mathrm{INTERFACE} < \mathrm{AUDIT} < \mathrm{CANDIDATE} < \mathrm{CERTIFICATE}$.

Reading the §20.2 table: the *minimum* over the 17 rows is taken by eight rows simultaneously — UQF-4, UQF-7, UQF-9, UQF-10, UQF-11, UQF-12, UQF-14, UQF-15 — each at **AUDIT**. Therefore

$$
\boxed{\;\Sigma(\mathrm{UQFC}) \;=\; \mathrm{AUDIT}\;}
$$

at the close of the current draft.

In §3.2.4 / §19.7 vocabulary, this places the overall paper at the *audit* tier — *below* the *Minimum Viable* claim ladder ("candidate unified quantum-force completion under declared assumptions") and well below *Strong* and *Full*. The honest reading is that **the paper is structurally complete (all 17 rows have certificate machinery, frozen inputs, pass/fail criteria, downgrade rules, and named research paths)** but is **not yet a candidate-tier closure** because eight rows are still at AUDIT.

The min-rule bites on the bottleneck rows in this order of consequence:

1. **UQF-11 (nonperturbative QCD)** — Clay Millennium Yang-Mills mass gap; the largest open problem in the stack, multi-decade horizon at the level of the global community.
2. **UQF-9 (UV completion)** — asymptotic safety as a programme has not been closed since 1979; the 13D-specific narrowings of §14.3 shrink the partner FRG calculation but do not solve it.
3. **UQF-10 (compactification stability)** — coupled to UQF-9 via FRG-7; the volume-modulus runaway question (S-7) is the most consequential cross-link to Paper 2 §6.9.3a.
4. **UQF-12 (strong CP)** — LOW-confidence candidate mechanism (lead (d), the $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ boundary-parity), Path α / β / γ decision branch named.
5. **UQF-4 (anomaly closure)** — 10 of 16 distinct classes already at CERTIFICATE; 5 AUDIT-with-roadmap rows (boundary anomalies) expected to close at certificate tier within Year 0–2 by Hořava-Witten + Dai-Freed + Cordova-Ohmori machinery; 1 OPEN-with-pathway row (row 17, coset-twist).
6. **UQF-7 (fermion quantization)** — UQF-7A–F at CERTIFICATE; the row sits at AUDIT on the UQF-7G neutrino-mass mechanism, pending the Paper 1 Appendix K Dirac-vs-Majorana decision.
7. **UQF-14 (unitarity / causality / locality)** — CERTIFICATE on the structural audit; AUDIT on the nonperturbative sector by inheritance from UQF-9, UQF-10, UQF-11; promotes as those upstream rows close.
8. **UQF-15 (no-hidden-force leakage)** — every experimental bound satisfied by inheritance from §4 ledger + §6.9.3a stabilization; the highest-likelihood falsifier is the precision-EW $m_W$ tension.

These eight rows define the work surface for any future revision aiming above $\mathrm{AUDIT}$.

---

## 20.4 What would need to land for Minimum-Viable / Strong / Full pass

Each tier is a checklist of named rows, not a promise — so a reader can see the distance from the current Σ to the next rung. Per the source handoff §16, the three tier targets are:

### 20.4.1 Minimum-Viable pass — *candidate unified quantum-force completion under declared assumptions*

Required: BRST/BV model + physical-state definition + graviton / gauge / Higgs certificates + anomaly closure + truncated UV certificate + nonperturbative QCD route + strong-CP candidate + precision comparison.

Status against current draft:
- BRST/BV model: §5 closed at textbook CERTIFICATE on overlap region. ✓
- Physical-state definition: §6 CERTIFICATE on retained perturbative sector. ✓
- Graviton certificate: §8 UQF-5A/B CERTIFICATE linearised. ✓
- Gauge certificates: §9 UQF-6A/B/C CERTIFICATE perturbative per sub-row. ✓
- Higgs certificate: §10 UQF-8A CERTIFICATE tree-level. ✓
- Anomaly closure: §7 *10 of 16 distinct classes CERTIFICATE; 5 AUDIT + 1 OPEN remain.* **Pending.**
- Truncated UV certificate: §14 *FRG-1 / FRG-3 / FRG-8 declarable today; FRG-2 partner calculation not performed.* **Pending.**
- Nonperturbative QCD route: §12 *AUDIT-TIER + ROADMAP; route specified, lattice inheritance documented.* **Pending — but route is in hand.**
- Strong-CP candidate: §13 *Candidate mechanism (lead (d)) named with falsifier; Path α / β / γ decision branch.* **Pending — Phase 1 of §13.7 must be performed.**
- Precision comparison: §16 *Tier-1 framework structure CERTIFICATE; Tier-2 numerics AUDIT.* **Tier-1 ✓; Tier-2 pending.**

The shortest gap from current draft to Minimum-Viable: the four-item set { Phase-1 strong-CP audit per §13.7.1; partner FRG calculation on §14 FRG-1; Hořava-Witten boundary anomaly polynomial for §7 rows 11–12; coset-twist Jacobian for §7 row 17 }. Three of these are 0–2-year named in-house items; the fourth (FRG) requires one partner-community delivery.

If those four close, $\Sigma(\mathrm{UQFC})$ promotes from AUDIT to **CANDIDATE**, and the paper qualifies for the Minimum-Viable claim language.

### 20.4.2 Strong pass — *certificate-complete unified quantum force theory under declared assumptions*

Required (Minimum-Viable items plus): positive physical Hilbert space + stable UV trajectory + quantum compactification stability + nonperturbative QCD certificate + strong-CP certificate + global force-sector likelihood + reproduction artifacts.

Status against current draft:
- Positive physical Hilbert space at full interacting level: §6.5.3 *open at the global physics literature level.* Strong-pass requires either (a) constructive 4D Yang-Mills positivity (Clay-class), or (b) asymptotic-safety closure with positive-residue propagators at the UV fixed point.
- Stable UV trajectory: §14 FRG-4 + FRG-5 + FRG-6 + FRG-7 cross-truncation closure required.
- Quantum compactification stability: §15 S-2 + S-5 + S-6 + S-7 all promoted from AUDIT to CERTIFICATE within truncation, conditional on §14 FRG calculation closing.
- Nonperturbative QCD certificate: §12 minimum-practical UQF-11B certificate (positive lowest gap under declared regulator and continuum extrapolation); the Clay-grade certificate is *not* the strong-pass target.
- Strong-CP certificate: §13 Path α closure (structural cancellation), per §13.7.2; or Path β with viable $f_a$ in an experimentally allowed window after careful Hosotani arithmetic.
- Global force-sector likelihood: §16 Tier-2 numerical sweep populated by partner pipelines (HEPfit, CKMfitter, NuFIT, flavio, RBC-UKQCD, etc.).
- Reproduction artifacts: §16 reproducibility envelope + §14 FRG-8.

All of these are multi-year / multi-partner / field-wide-progress items. Strong pass is conditional on substantial progress in *external* communities (asymptotic safety, nonperturbative QCD, lattice precision); the 13D programme cannot deliver them alone.

### 20.4.3 Full pass — *complete unified quantum theory of all known forces*

Required (Strong items plus): truncation-independent UV closure + constructive positivity + Lorentzian / operator-algebraic completion + very few "diagnostic only" rows.

This is a multi-decade target *at the level of the global quantum-gravity programme*, not at the level of the 13D programme alone. The 13D theory inherits Full closure from the field's progress; it does not produce it on its own.

---

## 20.5 Relation to Paper 2 (interface complete via C-FF backbone) and Paper 4 (TOE reserve)

Downward (§20.5.1) lies Paper 2, which closed the four-force *interface* question this paper builds its quantum completion on top of; upward lies Paper 4, which holds the TOE-tier reserve (cosmology, dark sector, baryogenesis) this paper deliberately does not litigate. The seams are fixed below so neither double-counts the other.

### 20.5.1 Downward (Paper 2)

Paper 2 closed the four-force *interface* compatibility question via the C-FF0..C-FF14 backbone. Paper 3 extends *above* that backbone: every UQF row in §3 inherits at least one C-FF row (§2.2.2 / §19.3), and the composition rule of §19.5 propagates C-FF failures to UQF failures. The two papers do not double-count: Paper 2 owns the interface question; Paper 3 owns the quantum-completion question; the C-FF / UQF hierarchy makes the dependency explicit.

Paper 3 does **not** modify Paper 2. C-FF0..C-FF14 are not edited. The matter ledger of Paper 2 §8.4 is not modified. The four projection maps $\pi_{\rm grav}, \pi_{\rm strong}, \pi_{\rm weak}, \pi_{\rm QED}$ are inherited as-given. The §6.3 BV-BRST package and the §6.5 FRG target are inherited as-given. The §6.7 outside-scope rows are *narrowed* (some promoted from "outside scope" to AUDIT-with-roadmap) but never *closed* in this paper without explicit per-row certificate work.

### 20.5.2 Upward (Paper 4)

Paper 4 inherits *everything Paper 3 explicitly excludes*: cosmology, dark matter, dark energy, baryogenesis (BG-10), initial conditions, the measurement problem, the emergence of classicality, and "why this universe." The hard claim boundary of §1 is the upward boundary of this paper; the moment a discussion turns to any of those topics, the discussion has left Paper 3's scope.

In particular:

- **BG-10 = *Open / Diagnostic*** is preserved unchanged. The first-pass $R = 1.0001$ at $z_1 = -0.07 - 1.35 i$ result of 2026-06-04 was withdrawn the same day after deep audit, and the four physics fixes for any future BG-10 attempt (canonical CI; proper $\Delta L = 2$; $N_2, N_3$ damping; density-matrix flavor evolution) are recorded in the corpus. **Paper 3 does not litigate BG-10. BG-10 is Paper 4 material.**
- **$\Lambda$-1 placeholder** of Article B §4.4 is preserved as a placeholder. The cosmological constant is not solved in this paper.
- **No dark-matter candidate is proposed in this paper.** The five candidate classes enumerated in the prior UQC-6 audit (with the lean toward $S^1/\mathbb Z_2$ boundary-localized hidden modes) are Paper 4 reserve.
- **Appendix N arrow-of-time** work is referenced in the corpus as ToE-extension, not required for force-sector closure; deferred to Paper 4.

The two-paper-split discipline is what allows Paper 3 to aggregate at AUDIT honestly within its own scope. Folding cosmology into Paper 3 would pull the aggregate down to whatever the cosmology rows' tier is, even where the force-completion rows admit a stronger tier. The corpus discipline (Paper 3 = force-sector only, 17 gates; Paper 4 = TOE, separate gate stack) is what makes this aggregation tractable.

---

## 20.6 Open-physics-problems acknowledgment

This subsection names the open problems honestly, as problems the whole field shares rather than defects peculiar to this framework. The subsections take each in turn — the Yang-Mills mass gap (§20.6.1), asymptotic safety as an open programme, and strong CP without a derived mechanism — recording for each that it is a recognized hard problem the paper inherits at AUDIT, not a place the 13D construction silently fails.

The §20.3 min-rule lands at AUDIT because three classes of open problem sit inside the force-sector scope and are *not* artifacts of the 13D programme:

### 20.6.1 The Yang-Mills mass gap (Clay Millennium)

UQF-11A (confinement) and UQF-11B (mass gap) are two of the seven Clay Mathematics Institute Millennium Prize problems (Jaffe-Witten 2000). No analytic programme — center-vortex, dual-superconductor, generalized-symmetry, lattice-rigorous, FRG, holographic, stochastic-quantization, algebraic-axiomatic — has produced a Clay-grade certificate as of 2026. The 13D framework supplies UV boundary data $(\alpha_3(M_Z)$ from $\mathrm{Vol}(K_6)$; quark masses from $K_6$ chamber overlap integrals) compatible with any future IR certificate, but is structurally unable to produce the certificate itself. This is the Wilsonian universality disclosure of §12.2 and is the same structural disclosure that every UV-completion programme (SUSY-GUT, technicolor, asymptotic safety, string compactifications) carries for the same reason.

### 20.6.2 Asymptotic safety as an open programme

UQF-9 (UV completion) is audit-tier because asymptotic safety as a research programme has been active since Weinberg's 1979 conjecture and is still without a closed existence theorem in 4D, let alone in $d > 4$. The 13D-specific narrowings of §14.3 *shrink* the partner FRG calculation by (i) supplying a finite, structured operator basis under residual gauge symmetry, (ii) restricting boundary anomaly classes to a finite Dai-Freed checklist, and (iii) reducing moduli stabilization to a single-modulus question, but they do not solve the existence problem.

### 20.6.3 Strong CP without a derived mechanism

UQF-12 (strong CP) is at AUDIT with LOW confidence because the most promising 13D-internal candidate (the $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ orbifold-boundary parity, lead (d) of §13.4) has not been computed; it is a candidate *inspection point*, not a derived cancellation. The structural mechanism would need to (i) propagate the orbifold parity to a CP-like parity action on the Yukawa map after dimensional reduction, (ii) force $\arg\det M_q$ to zero (or to a value cancelling $\theta_{\rm QCD}$) by parity rather than tuning, and (iii) preserve the CKM Jarlskog invariant $J$ at PDG machine precision (cross-sector tie via the same $\omega^{(1,0)}$ spin-c connection, per Article B §8.2). The 1.64-rad contribution to $\arg\det M_q$ from the spin-c holonomy $\Phi = -0.12827$ rad on $K_6$ is the falsification surface that any successful structural mechanism must cancel.

These three are the dominant audit-tier landings; the remaining AUDIT rows (UQF-4 boundary anomalies + coset-twist, UQF-7 neutrino-mass mechanism, UQF-10 moduli stability under FRG flow, UQF-14 nonperturbative unitarity by inheritance, UQF-15 no-hidden-force leakage) inherit from one or more of them.

---

The status-preservation invariant of this project is **"Chris does the physics."** Agents organize, audit, and draft; agents do not invent new physics or fabricate certificates for open problems. The work plan below names, per gate, the next-step physics task that must be performed *by direct calculation* (not by agent assertion) for the gate to promote tier.

For brevity, gates already at CERTIFICATE are not listed (UQF-0, UQF-2 textbook overlap, UQF-16 map structure).

| Gate | Task name | Horizon | Lead | Deliverable |
|---|---|---|---|---|

Promotes §6.5.2 from textbook-inherited to corpus-frozen. |
| **UQF-4 rows 11–12** | Hořava-Witten boundary anomaly polynomial for $S^1/\mathbb Z_2 \times$ active SM matter | 0–1 year | in-house | Boundary anomaly polynomial vanishes by SM inheritance; bulk Chern-Simons coefficient set to zero. CERTIFICATE-tier upgrade. |
| **UQF-4 rows 13–14** | Bordism-group calculation for spin-c bundles on $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1$ with active boundary parity | 1–2 years | partnership (Freed / Hopkins / Tachikawa group) | Trivial bordism class certificate. CERTIFICATE-tier upgrade. |
| **UQF-4 row 17** | Coset-twist Jacobian on $K_6 \times S^2 \times S^1$ harmonic basis | 0–2 years | in-house | 3-step calculation per §7.5.2 (Jacobian → cohomology classification → conditional inflow construction). Expected step-2 reduction to row 13 with no new inflow. |
| **UQF-5** | KK-graviton-mass spectrum at locked §6.9.3a volume modulus | 0–1 year | in-house | Frozen KK-graviton tower spectrum at the active branch; promotes UQF-5B beyond mode-identification |
| **UQF-6** | Tree-level + one-loop polarisation-count audit per sub-row + Run-3 Higgs-coupling consistency check | 1–2 years | in-house + partnership | Sub-row CERTIFICATE upgrades, conditional on §10 UQF-8B Wilson-line closure |
| **UQF-7G** | Paper 1 Appendix K mechanism decision (Dirac vs Majorana via see-saw vs Weinberg dim-5) | 1–2 years | in-house (Paper 1 work) | Appendix K closure; selects option (i), (ii), or (iii) of §11.7.1; UQF-7G promotes from AUDIT to CERTIFICATE |

Either is Minimum-tier closure for UQF-9. |

If Path α: full strong-CP certificate. If Path β: careful Hosotani $f_a$ + axion-window check. If Path γ: honest exclusion at the UQF-12 gate. |

The single most important next item — the one whose closure most efficiently promotes the aggregate $\Sigma(\mathrm{UQFC})$ — is **UQF-12 Phase 1 (the $S^1_Y/\mathbb Z_2$ orbifold-parity audit, lead (d) of §13.4.4)**. It is a 3–6-month in-house Chris-physics task; it does not require partnership; it does not depend on any other UQF gate closing first; and a successful Path α closure would settle one of the eight AUDIT rows of §20.3 with the highest stylistic-preference outcome (structural cancellation > axion fallback > permanent exclusion).

The second most important item is **the partner FRG calculation on UQF-9 FRG-1**: it is the *only* row at AUDIT that has a *single concrete external delivery* that promotes it to Minimum-tier closure; it also (per the §15 cross-certificate) closes the four AUDIT rows S-2 / S-5 / S-6 / S-7 of UQF-10 to AUDIT-resolution within truncation.

The third is **Phase 1 of UQF-4 boundary-anomaly closure** (Hořava-Witten + Dai-Freed + coset-twist); this is a 0–2-year in-house item that closes 5 of the 6 currently non-CERTIFICATE anomaly rows.

If those three pieces close — Phase-1 strong-CP audit, one partner FRG truncation, Phase-1 boundary-anomaly + coset-twist closure — the aggregate min-rule promotes from AUDIT to **CANDIDATE**, and the paper qualifies for the Minimum-Viable claim language ("candidate unified quantum-force completion under declared assumptions"). That is the *near-term* (0–2 years) work plan.

---

## 20.8 Closing statement

Paper 3 is structurally complete and at AUDIT tier under the §3.4.3 min-rule. Every UQF row carries explicit purpose, certificate, frozen inputs, pass/fail criterion, downgrade rule, status label, C-FF inheritance, and named research path. Three rows are at CERTIFICATE; six are at CANDIDATE; eight are at AUDIT; zero are FAILED or OPEN at the §3.4.3 ladder.

The eight AUDIT rows (UQF-4, UQF-7, UQF-9, UQF-10, UQF-11, UQF-12, UQF-14, UQF-15) are the work surface. The three tasks ranked in §20.7 would, together, promote $\Sigma(\mathrm{UQFC})$ from AUDIT to CANDIDATE and qualify the paper for the Minimum-Viable claim language.

The paper does not claim a Theory of Everything. It does not claim a certificate of all force physics. It does not claim a gate-upgrade for Paper 1 or Paper 2. It does not claim any cosmological, dark-sector, or baryogenesis result; BG-10 = *Open / Diagnostic* is preserved without modification as Paper 4 reserve material.

The honest scope statement: *Paper 3 is a candidate unified quantum-force completion at AUDIT tier under declared assumptions, with structurally complete certificate machinery, perturbative-and-tree-level closures for the matter and force-carrier rows, and named research paths for every row whose tier is below CERTIFICATE.* The forward route to Minimum-Viable (CANDIDATE), Strong (CERTIFICATE under declared assumptions), and Full (truncation-independent CERTIFICATE) is explicit and routed gate-by-gate.

Chris does the physics; agents organize, audit, and draft.

And so, stated in this build's terms, the paper's contribution is its own scoreboard: seventeen gates, each read in two tenses — what is closed, and what would close it — with the weakest link printed on the cover, not buried. The front page says the only number the min-rule permits: **Σ = AUDIT**, with the rows that would raise it named, frozen, and falsifiable.

*Trailing technical note — status-preservation invariants confirmed.* Hard-gate vector $\mathsf D, \mathsf D\text{-local}, \mathsf D, \mathsf D, \mathsf D$ preserved. BG-10 = *Open / Diagnostic* preserved (Paper 4 reserve). SoT hash `88e5903fe1c3d17655acef7e4fb45078e3168add25362040e21598b3b161ff17` preserved. C-FF0..C-FF14 in Paper 2 not modified. Stage B iter-4e FINAL-WINNER-SCIENCE-PASS preserved. No edits to filed-patent material, NRC packet, SoT manuscript, baryogenesis_build, Article C §8.2, candidate-improvement-9-spec, candidate-improvement-10-spec. "Chris does the physics" — this conclusion organizes the existing certificate stack into a single status statement; no new physics is invented; no certificate is fabricated. *(End of UQFC-20 — Conclusion.)*


# Appendix U — Interface Certificate Registry

One runnable folder per stack-integrity certificate, schema identical to the Q/R0.R sets of Papers I–II: `frozen_inputs.yaml`, `src/check.py`, `run.sh`, `outputs/`, `hashes/`, `falsifiers/`; each embeds its negative control; the no-doc-only-completion rule applies. The U-set certifies the *stack discipline of this paper* — the seventeen-row template, the min-rule Σ, the routing, the ledger closure, the cross-paper consumption, the preserved invariants, and the honesty guards. Physics-content certification remains per-row per §3; Paper 1/2 regeneration remains with their own registries.

| Folder | Checks (one line) | Result | Negative control |
